// ============================================================
// MOCK ATTENDANCE HISTORY — Monthly calendar data
// ============================================================
const generateMockAttendanceHistory = () => {
  const result = {};
  const workers = [
    { id: "w1" }, { id: "w2" }, { id: "w3" },
    { id: "w4" }, { id: "w5" }, { id: "w6" },
    { id: "sv1" }, { id: "sv2" }, { id: "sv3" }, { id: "sv4" },
  ];
  // Generate for last 4 months
  const now = new Date();
  const months = [];
  for (let i = 0; i < 4; i++) {
    const d = new Date(now.getFullYear(), now.getMonth() - i, 1);
    months.push(`${d.getFullYear()}-${String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, "0")}`);
  }
  // Seeded pseudo-random for consistency
  const seededRand = (seed) => {
    const x = Math.sin(seed + 1) * 10000;
    return x - Math.floor(x);
  };
  workers.forEach(worker => {
    months.forEach(month => {
      const [year, mon] = month.split("-").map(Number);
      const daysInMonth = new Date(year, mon, 0).getDate();
      const key = `${worker.id}_${month}`;
      result[key] = {};
      for (let d = 1; d <= daysInMonth; d++) {
        const dateStr = `${month}-${String(d).padStart(2, "0")}`;
        const dayOfWeek = new Date(dateStr).getDay();
        const seed = worker.id.charCodeAt(1) * 100 + mon * 10 + d;
        const rand = seededRand(seed);
        if (dayOfWeek === 0) {
          result[key][dateStr] = "holiday"; // Sunday
        } else if (dayOfWeek === 7) {
          result[key][dateStr] = rand < 0.3 ? "present" : "holiday";
        } else {
          if (rand < 0.78)      result[key][dateStr] = "present";
          else if (rand < 0.88) result[key][dateStr] = "absent";
          else if (rand < 0.94) result[key][dateStr] = "leave";
          else                  result[key][dateStr] = "half";
        }
      }
      // Mark last few days of current month as none (future)
      if (month === months[0]) {
        for (let d = now.getDate() + 1; d <= daysInMonth; d++) {
          const dateStr = `${month}-${String(d).padStart(2, "0")}`;
          result[key][dateStr] = "none";
        }
      }
    });
  });
  return result;
};
const MOCK_ATTENDANCE_HISTORY = generateMockAttendanceHistory();

// ============================================================
// UTILITY COMPONENTS
// ============================================================
const Badge = ({ color, children, size = "sm" }) => {
  const colors = {
    green:  "bg-green-50 text-green-700 border-green-200",
    red:    "bg-red-50 text-red-600 border-red-200",
    amber:  "bg-amber-50 text-amber-700 border-amber-200",
    blue:   "bg-blue-50 text-blue-700 border-blue-200",
    purple: "bg-purple-50 text-purple-700 border-purple-200",
    orange: "bg-orange-50 text-orange-700 border-orange-200",
    slate:  "bg-gray-100 text-gray-600 border-gray-200",
  };
  return (
    <span className={`inline-flex items-center border rounded-full font-semibold ${size === "xs" ? "px-2 py-0.5 text-[11px]" : "px-3 py-1 text-xs"} ${colors[color] || colors.blue}`}>
      {children}
    </span>
  );
};

const StatCard = ({ label, value, sub, icon, color = "orange" }) => {
  const colorMap = {
    orange: "border-orange-100 bg-white",
    green:  "border-green-100 bg-white",
    blue:   "border-blue-100 bg-white",
    purple: "border-purple-100 bg-white",
  };
  const iconBg = {
    orange: "bg-orange-50 text-orange-500",
    green:  "bg-green-50 text-green-500",
    blue:   "bg-blue-50 text-blue-500",
    purple: "bg-purple-50 text-purple-500",
  };
  const valueColor = {
    orange: "text-orange-600",
    green:  "text-green-600",
    blue:   "text-blue-600",
    purple: "text-purple-600",
  };
  return (
    <div className={`${colorMap[color]} border-2 rounded-2xl p-4 shadow-sm`}>
      <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-2">
        <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
          <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs font-semibold mb-1 uppercase tracking-wide">{label}</p>
          <p className={`text-2xl font-black ${valueColor[color]} leading-none mb-1`}>{value}</p>
          {sub && <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs mt-1">{sub}</p>}
        </div>
        <span className={`text-2xl w-10 h-10 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 ${iconBg[color]}`}>{icon}</span>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const Modal = ({ open, onClose, title, children, size = "md" }) => {
  const scrollRef = React.useRef(null);

  // Prevent body scroll when modal open + reset scroll only when modal opens
  React.useEffect(() => {
    if (open) {
      document.body.style.overflow = "hidden";
      if (scrollRef.current) scrollRef.current.scrollTop = 0;
    }
    return () => { document.body.style.overflow = ""; };
  }, [open]);

  if (!open) return null;
  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex flex-col justify-end sm:justify-center sm:items-center sm:p-4">
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-black/60 backdrop-blur-sm" onClick={onClose} />
      {/* Bottom sheet — rises above keyboard automatically */}
      <div className="relative w-full sm:max-w-lg bg-white rounded-t-3xl sm:rounded-2xl shadow-2xl z-10 flex flex-col"
        style={{ maxHeight:"85dvh", maxWidth:"512px" }}>
        {/* Drag handle */}
        <div className="flex justify-center pt-3 pb-1 shrink-0">
          <div className="w-10 h-1 bg-gray-300 rounded-full" />
        </div>
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-5 py-3 border-b border-gray-100 shrink-0">
          <h3 className="text-base font-extrabold text-gray-900">{title}</h3>
          <button onClick={onClose}
            className="w-10 h-10 flex items-center justify-center rounded-2xl bg-gray-100 active:bg-red-100 text-gray-500 font-bold text-lg transition">✕</button>
        </div>
        {/* Scrollable body */}
        <div ref={scrollRef} className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto px-5 py-4 pb-8" style={{WebkitOverflowScrolling:"touch"}}>
          {children}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

// Mobile-friendly Input — 16px font prevents iOS zoom
const Input = ({ label, labelHindi, className = "", type, ...props }) => (
  <div className="space-y-1.5">
    {label && (
      <label className="block text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">
        {label}{labelHindi && <span className="text-gray-400 font-normal ml-1 text-xs">({labelHindi})</span>}
      </label>
    )}
    <input
      type={type}
      inputMode={type === "number" ? "numeric" : type === "tel" ? "tel" : undefined}
      pattern={type === "number" ? "[0-9]*" : undefined}
      {...props}
      className={`w-full bg-white border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 text-gray-900 focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-400 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-orange-100 placeholder-gray-300 transition shadow-sm ${className}`}
      style={{ fontSize: "16px" }}
    />
  </div>
);

// Mobile-friendly Select — 16px font prevents iOS zoom
const Select = ({ label, labelHindi, children, ...props }) => (
  <div className="space-y-1.5">
    {label && (
      <label className="block text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">
        {label}{labelHindi && <span className="text-gray-400 font-normal ml-1 text-xs">({labelHindi})</span>}
      </label>
    )}
    <div className="relative">
      <select
        {...props}
        className="w-full bg-white border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 text-gray-900 focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-400 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-orange-100 transition appearance-none pr-10 shadow-sm"
        style={{ fontSize: "16px" }}
      >
        {children}
      </select>
      <span className="absolute right-4 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-orange-400 pointer-events-none font-bold">▾</span>
    </div>
  </div>
);

const Btn = ({ children, variant = "primary", size = "md", className = "", disabled = false, ...props }) => {
  const variants = {
    primary:   "bg-orange-500 active:bg-orange-600 text-white shadow-md shadow-orange-200 hover:bg-orange-600",
    secondary: "bg-white active:bg-gray-50 text-gray-700 border-2 border-gray-200 hover:border-orange-300 hover:text-orange-600",
    danger:    "bg-red-50 active:bg-red-100 text-red-600 border-2 border-red-200 hover:bg-red-100",
    success:   "bg-green-500 active:bg-green-600 text-white shadow-md shadow-green-200",
    ghost:     "active:bg-orange-50 text-orange-600 hover:bg-orange-50",
  };
  const sizes = { sm: "px-3.5 py-2 text-xs min-h-[36px] font-bold", md: "px-5 py-3 text-sm min-h-[46px] font-bold", lg: "px-6 py-3.5 text-base min-h-[52px] font-extrabold" };
  return (
    <button
      {...props}
      disabled={disabled}
      className={`${variants[variant]} ${sizes[size]} rounded-xl font-semibold transition-all active:scale-95 ${disabled ? "opacity-40 cursor-not-allowed pointer-events-none" : ""} ${className}`}
    >
      {children}
    </button>
  );
};

const Table = ({ headers, rows, emptyMsg = "कोई data नहीं" }) => (
  <div className="overflow-x-auto rounded-2xl border-2 border-gray-100 shadow-sm">
    <table className="w-full text-sm">
      <thead>
        <tr className="bg-gradient-to-r from-orange-500 to-orange-600">
          {headers.map((h, i) => (
            <th key={i} className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-extrabold text-white uppercase tracking-wide whitespace-nowrap">{h}</th>
          ))}
        </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody className="divide-y divide-gray-50 bg-white">
        {rows.length === 0
          ? <tr><td colSpan={headers.length} className="text-center py-12 text-gray-400 text-sm">{emptyMsg}</td></tr>
          : rows.map((row, i) => <tr key={i} className={i % 2 === 0 ? "bg-white" : "bg-orange-50/30"}>{row}</tr>)
        }
      </tbody>
    </table>
  </div>
);

const Td = ({ children, className = "" }) => (
  <td className={`px-4 py-3 text-gray-900 whitespace-nowrap ${className}`}>{children}</td>
);

// ── Pagination Utility ──────────────────────────────────────
const usePagination = (data, pageSize = 25) => {
  const [page, setPage] = useState(1);
  const totalPages = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(data.length / pageSize));
  const paged = data.slice((page - 1) * pageSize, page * pageSize);
  useEffect(() => { setPage(1); }, [data.length]);
  return { paged, page, setPage, totalPages, total: data.length, pageSize };
};

const Paginator = ({ page, setPage, totalPages, total, pageSize }) => {
  if (totalPages <= 1) return null;
  const from = (page - 1) * pageSize + 1;
  const to   = Math.min(page * pageSize, total);
  const pages = Array.from({ length: Math.min(5, totalPages) }, (_, i) => {
    if (totalPages <= 5) return i + 1;
    if (page <= 3) return i + 1;
    if (page >= totalPages - 2) return totalPages - 4 + i;
    return page - 2 + i;
  });
  return (
    <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2.5 bg-gray-50 border-t border-gray-100">
      <span className="text-xs text-gray-500">{from}–{to} of {total}</span>
      <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
        <button onClick={() => setPage(p => Math.max(1, p - 1))} disabled={page === 1}
          className="w-7 h-7 rounded-lg border border-gray-200 text-xs font-bold text-gray-600 disabled:opacity-30 hover:bg-orange-50 hover:border-orange-300 transition">&lt;</button>
        {pages.map(p => (
          <button key={p} onClick={() => setPage(p)}
            className={"w-7 h-7 rounded-lg text-xs font-bold border transition " +
              (p === page ? "bg-orange-500 text-white border-orange-500" : "border-gray-200 text-gray-600 hover:bg-orange-50 hover:border-orange-300")}>
            {p}
          </button>
        ))}
        <button onClick={() => setPage(p => Math.min(totalPages, p + 1))} disabled={page === totalPages}
          className="w-7 h-7 rounded-lg border border-gray-200 text-xs font-bold text-gray-600 disabled:opacity-30 hover:bg-orange-50 hover:border-orange-300 transition">&gt;</button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

// ============================================================
// PAGE COMPONENTS
// ============================================================

// LOGIN
const LoginPage = ({ onLogin }) => {
  const [screen,   setScreen]   = useState("login"); // "login" | "register" | "success"
  const [mobile,   setMobile]   = useState("9876543210");
  const [password, setPassword] = useState("admin123");
  const [role,     setRole]     = useState("admin");
  const [loading,  setLoading]  = useState(false);
  const [err,      setErr]      = useState("");

  // Registration form state
  const [reg, setReg] = useState({
    name: "", mobile: "", password: "", confirm: "",
    department: "", aadhaar: "", address: "", emergency: "",
  });
  const [regErr,  setRegErr]  = useState("");
  const [regStep, setRegStep] = useState(1); // 1 = personal, 2 = work

  const handleLogin = () => {
    setLoading(true); setErr("");
    setTimeout(() => {
      if (!mobile || !password) { setErr("Mobile और Password डालें।"); setLoading(false); return; }
      // Check supervisor accounts first (real login)
      if (role === "supervisor") {
        const sv = MOCK_DB.supervisorAccounts.find(s => s.mobile === mobile && s.password === password);
        if (sv) { onLogin({ ...sv }); setLoading(false); return; }
        // Demo fallback
        const svDemo = MOCK_DB.supervisorAccounts[0];
        onLogin({ ...svDemo }); setLoading(false); return;
      }
      // Admin / worker / contractor
      onLogin({ ...MOCK_DB.currentUser, role });
      setLoading(false);
    }, 800);
  };

  const handleRegNext = () => {
    if (!reg.name.trim())                          { setRegErr("नाम जरूरी है।"); return; }
    if (!/^\d{10}$/.test(reg.mobile))             { setRegErr("10 अंकों का मोबाइल नंबर डालें।"); return; }
    if (reg.password.length < 6)                  { setRegErr("Password कम से कम 6 characters का होना चाहिए।"); return; }
    if (reg.password !== reg.confirm)             { setRegErr("Password और Confirm Password मेल नहीं खाते।"); return; }
    setRegErr(""); setRegStep(2);
  };

  const handleRegSubmit = () => {
    if (!reg.department)                          { setRegErr("Department चुनें।"); return; }
    setLoading(true); setRegErr("");
    setTimeout(() => { setLoading(false); setScreen("success"); }, 1000);
  };

  const setField = (key) => (e) => setReg(p => ({ ...p, [key]: e.target.value }));

  /* ── SUCCESS SCREEN ── */
  if (screen === "success") return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-white flex items-center justify-center p-4"
      style={{ backgroundImage: "radial-gradient(ellipse at 20% 50%, rgba(249,115,22,0.08) 0%, transparent 60%)" }}>
      <div className="w-full max-w-md text-center">
        <div className="w-20 h-20 bg-green-100 rounded-3xl flex items-center justify-center mx-auto mb-5">
          <svg width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none">
            <path d="M5 13l4 4L19 7" stroke="#16A34A" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
          </svg>
        </div>
        <h2 className="text-2xl font-extrabold text-gray-900 mb-2">Registration Submitted!</h2>
        <p className="text-gray-500 text-sm mb-1">आपकी request भेज दी गई है।</p>
        <p className="text-gray-500 text-sm mb-6">Admin approval के बाद आप login कर पाएंगे।</p>
        <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-2xl p-4 mb-6 text-left space-y-2">
          <div className="flex justify-between text-sm"><span className="text-gray-500">Name</span><span className="font-bold text-gray-900">{reg.name}</span></div>
          <div className="flex justify-between text-sm"><span className="text-gray-500">Mobile</span><span className="font-bold text-gray-900">{reg.mobile}</span></div>
          <div className="flex justify-between text-sm"><span className="text-gray-500">Department</span><span className="font-bold text-gray-900">{reg.department}</span></div>
          <div className="flex justify-between text-sm"><span className="text-gray-500">Status</span><span className="font-bold text-amber-600">Pending Approval</span></div>
        </div>
        <button onClick={() => { setScreen("login"); setReg({ name:"",mobile:"",password:"",confirm:"",department:"",aadhaar:"",address:"",emergency:"" }); setRegStep(1); }}
          className="w-full bg-orange-500 text-white font-extrabold py-4 rounded-2xl active:scale-[0.98] transition shadow-md shadow-orange-200">
          Back to Login
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );

  /* ── REGISTER SCREEN ── */
  if (screen === "register") return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-white flex items-center justify-center p-4"
      style={{ backgroundImage: "radial-gradient(ellipse at 80% 20%, rgba(59,130,246,0.06) 0%, transparent 50%)" }}>
      <div className="w-full max-w-md">
        {/* Back to Login */}
        <button onClick={() => { setScreen("login"); setRegErr(""); setRegStep(1); }}
          className="flex items-center gap-1.5 text-orange-500 font-bold text-sm mb-5 active:opacity-70 transition">
          <svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none">
            <path d="M19 12H5M5 12l7 7M5 12l7-7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2.2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
          </svg>
          Login पर वापस जाएं
        </button>

        {/* Header */}
        <div className="text-center mb-6">
          <div className="inline-flex items-center justify-center w-14 h-14 mb-3">
            <GarmentLogo size={56} />
          </div>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-extrabold text-gray-900">Worker Registration</h1>
          <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs mt-1">नया Account बनाएं</p>
        </div>

        {/* Step indicator */}
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-5">
          <div className={`flex-1 h-1.5 rounded-full transition-all ${regStep>=1?"bg-orange-500":"bg-gray-200"}`}/>
          <div className={`flex-1 h-1.5 rounded-full transition-all ${regStep>=2?"bg-orange-500":"bg-gray-200"}`}/>
          <span className="text-xs text-gray-400 shrink-0">Step {regStep}/2</span>
        </div>

        <div className="bg-gray-50 rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 p-6 shadow-xl space-y-4">
          {regErr && <div className="bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-xl p-3 text-red-600 text-sm">{regErr}</div>}

          {regStep === 1 && (
            <>
              <h3 className="font-extrabold text-gray-900">Personal Details / व्यक्तिगत जानकारी</h3>
              <Input label="Full Name" labelHindi="पूरा नाम" value={reg.name}
                onChange={setField("name")} placeholder="आपका पूरा नाम" />
              <Input label="Mobile Number" labelHindi="मोबाइल" type="tel" value={reg.mobile}
                onChange={setField("mobile")} placeholder="10 digit mobile number" />
              <Input label="Password" labelHindi="पासवर्ड" type="password" value={reg.password}
                onChange={setField("password")} placeholder="कम से कम 6 characters" />
              <Input label="Confirm Password" labelHindi="पासवर्ड दोबारा" type="password" value={reg.confirm}
                onChange={setField("confirm")} placeholder="Password दोबारा डालें" />
              <Input label="Address" labelHindi="पता" value={reg.address}
                onChange={setField("address")} placeholder="घर का पता (optional)" />
              <Btn onClick={handleRegNext} className="w-full flex justify-center" size="lg">
                Next — Work Details →
              </Btn>
            </>
          )}

          {regStep === 2 && (
            <>
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                <button onClick={() => { setRegStep(1); setRegErr(""); }}
                  className="text-orange-500 font-bold text-sm">← Back</button>
                <h3 className="font-extrabold text-gray-900">Work Details / काम की जानकारी</h3>
              </div>
              <Select label="Department" labelHindi="विभाग" value={reg.department} onChange={setField("department")}>
                <option value="">-- Department चुनें --</option>
                {MOCK_DB.departments.map(d => <option key={d.id} value={d.name}>{d.name} — {d.nameHindi}</option>)}
              </Select>
              <Input label="Aadhaar Number" labelHindi="आधार नंबर" type="tel" value={reg.aadhaar}
                onChange={setField("aadhaar")} placeholder="12 digit Aadhaar (optional)" />
              <Input label="Emergency Contact" labelHindi="आपातकालीन संपर्क" type="tel" value={reg.emergency}
                onChange={setField("emergency")} placeholder="Emergency contact number (optional)" />

              <div className="bg-amber-50 border border-amber-200 rounded-xl p-3 text-xs text-amber-700 leading-relaxed">
                Registration submit करने के बाद Admin review करेगा। Approval मिलने पर आप login कर पाएंगे।
              </div>

              <Btn onClick={handleRegSubmit} disabled={loading} className="w-full flex justify-center" size="lg">
                {loading ? "Submitting..." : "Submit Registration →"}
              </Btn>
            </>
          )}
        </div>

        <p className="text-center text-sm mt-5">
          <span className="text-gray-500">पहले से account है? </span>
          <button onClick={() => { setScreen("login"); setRegErr(""); setRegStep(1); }}
            className="text-orange-500 font-extrabold">Login करें</button>
        </p>
      </div>
    </div>
  );

  /* ── LOGIN SCREEN ── */
  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center p-4 relative overflow-hidden"
      style={{ background: "linear-gradient(135deg, #fff7ed 0%, #ffffff 50%, #eff6ff 100%)" }}>

      {/* Background decorative circles */}
      <div className="absolute top-0 right-0 w-72 h-72 rounded-full opacity-20 pointer-events-none"
        style={{ background: "radial-gradient(circle, #f97316, transparent)", transform: "translate(30%, -30%)" }} />
      <div className="absolute bottom-0 left-0 w-64 h-64 rounded-full opacity-15 pointer-events-none"
        style={{ background: "radial-gradient(circle, #3b82f6, transparent)", transform: "translate(-30%, 30%)" }} />

      <div className="w-full max-w-md relative z-10">
        {/* Logo section */}
        <div className="text-center mb-8">
          <div className="inline-flex items-center justify-center w-20 h-20 mb-4 rounded-3xl shadow-xl shadow-orange-200/60"
            style={{ background: "linear-gradient(135deg, #f97316, #ea580c)" }}>
            <GarmentLogo size={48} />
          </div>
          <h1 className="text-3xl font-black text-gray-900 tracking-tight">Garment Factory</h1>
          <p className="text-gray-500 text-sm mt-1 font-medium">Production Management System</p>
          <div className="inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 mt-2 bg-orange-50 border border-orange-200 rounded-full px-3 py-1">
            <div className="w-1.5 h-1.5 bg-orange-400 rounded-full animate-pulse" />
            <p className="text-orange-600 text-xs font-bold">गारमेंट फैक्टरी प्रबंधन प्रणाली</p>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Login card */}
        <div className="bg-white rounded-3xl border-2 border-gray-100 p-6 shadow-xl shadow-gray-200/60">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-5">
            <div className="w-1 h-6 bg-orange-500 rounded-full" />
            <h2 className="text-lg font-extrabold text-gray-900">Login / लॉगिन करें</h2>
          </div>

          {err && (
            <div className="mb-4 p-3.5 bg-red-50 border-2 border-red-200 rounded-xl text-red-600 text-sm font-medium flex items-center gap-2">
              <span className="text-lg">⚠️</span> {err}
            </div>
          )}

          <div className="space-y-4">
            <Input label="Mobile Number" labelHindi="मोबाइल नंबर" type="tel" value={mobile}
              onChange={e => setMobile(e.target.value)} placeholder="Enter mobile number" />
            <Input label="Password" labelHindi="पासवर्ड" type="password" value={password}
              onChange={e => setPassword(e.target.value)} placeholder="Enter password" />
            <Select label="Login As" labelHindi="भूमिका चुनें" value={role} onChange={e => setRole(e.target.value)}>
              <option value="admin">🔑 Admin (Factory Owner)</option>
              <option value="supervisor">👷 Supervisor</option>
              <option value="worker">🧵 Worker</option>
              <option value="contractor">📋 Contractor</option>
            </Select>
            <Btn onClick={handleLogin} disabled={loading} className="w-full justify-center flex items-center gap-2" size="lg">
              {loading ? (
                <><span className="w-4 h-4 border-2 border-white/40 border-t-white rounded-full animate-spin" />Logging in...</>
              ) : (
                <>Login करें <span>→</span></>
              )}
            </Btn>
          </div>

          {/* Demo credentials */}
          <div className="mt-5 pt-4 border-t-2 border-dashed border-gray-100">
            <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs text-center mb-3 font-semibold uppercase tracking-wide">Demo Accounts</p>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2">
              <button onClick={() => { setRole("admin"); setMobile("9876543210"); setPassword("demo123"); }}
                className="flex items-center gap-2 bg-purple-50 border-2 border-purple-100 rounded-xl px-3 py-2.5 text-purple-700 font-bold text-xs hover:border-purple-300 transition active:scale-95">
                <span className="text-base">🔑</span> Admin
              </button>
              <button onClick={() => { setRole("supervisor"); setMobile("9811111111"); setPassword("sup123"); }}
                className="flex items-center gap-2 bg-blue-50 border-2 border-blue-100 rounded-xl px-3 py-2.5 text-blue-700 font-bold text-xs hover:border-blue-300 transition active:scale-95">
                <span className="text-base">👷</span> Supervisor
              </button>
              <button onClick={() => { setRole("worker"); setMobile("9876543210"); setPassword("demo123"); }}
                className="flex items-center gap-2 bg-green-50 border-2 border-green-100 rounded-xl px-3 py-2.5 text-green-700 font-bold text-xs hover:border-green-300 transition active:scale-95">
                <span className="text-base">🧵</span> Worker
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Register link */}
        <div className="mt-4 bg-white border-2 border-orange-100 rounded-2xl p-4 text-center shadow-sm">
          <p className="text-gray-500 text-sm mb-2.5">नया Worker हैं? पहली बार join कर रहे हैं?</p>
          <button onClick={() => { setScreen("register"); setErr(""); }}
            className="bg-gradient-to-r from-orange-500 to-orange-600 text-white font-extrabold text-sm px-6 py-2.5 rounded-xl active:scale-[0.98] transition shadow-md shadow-orange-200">
            Self Registration / खुद रजिस्टर करें →
          </button>
        </div>

        <p className="text-center text-gray-300 text-xs mt-4 font-medium">
          Garment Factory SaaS v1.0 • PWA Ready
        </p>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

  { id: "se3", date: "2024-01-13", style: "Kids T-Shirt",       styleId: "s3", operation: "Button Sewing", operationId: "op3", pieces: 200, pieceRate: 0.75, amount: 150.00, status: "approved", note: "" },
  { id: "se4", date: "2024-01-12", style: "Women's Kurta",      styleId: "s2", operation: "Stitching",     operationId: "op1", pieces: 130, pieceRate: 2.50, amount: 325.00, status: "rejected", note: "Pieces count mismatch" },
  { id: "se5", date: "2024-01-11", style: "Denim Jeans",        styleId: "s4", operation: "Overlock",      operationId: "op2", pieces: 80,  pieceRate: 1.50, amount: 120.00, status: "approved", note: "" },
  { id: "se6", date: "2024-01-10", style: "Men's Formal Shirt", styleId: "s1", operation: "Stitching",     operationId: "op1", pieces: 105, pieceRate: 2.50, amount: 262.50, status: "approved", note: "" },
];

// ============================================================
// WORKER PANEL — Complete Redesign
// ============================================================

const WorkerPanel = ({ onLogout }) => {
  const { user, sharedEntries, sharedCuts, sharedActions, sharedNotifs } = useContext(AppContext);
  const myDept   = user.department || "Stitching";
  const deptColor = MOCK_DB.departments.find(d=>d.name===myDept)?.color || "#F97316";
  const [tab, setTab] = useState("entry");
  const [entries, setEntries] = useState([
    { id:"se1", date:"2024-01-15", style:"Kids T-Shirt",       operation:"Stitching",     pieces:95,  pieceRate:2.50, amount:237.50, status:"pending",  note:"" },
    { id:"se2", date:"2024-01-14", style:"Men's Formal Shirt", operation:"Overlock",      pieces:110, pieceRate:1.50, amount:165.00, status:"approved", note:"Supervisor verified" },
    { id:"se3", date:"2024-01-13", style:"Kids T-Shirt",       operation:"Button Sewing", pieces:200, pieceRate:0.75, amount:150.00, status:"approved", note:"" },
    { id:"se4", date:"2024-01-12", style:"Women's Kurta",      operation:"Stitching",     pieces:130, pieceRate:2.50, amount:325.00, status:"rejected", note:"Pieces count mismatch" },
    { id:"se5", date:"2024-01-11", style:"Denim Jeans",        operation:"Overlock",      pieces:80,  pieceRate:1.50, amount:120.00, status:"approved", note:"" },
    { id:"se6", date:"2024-01-10", style:"Men's Formal Shirt", operation:"Stitching",     pieces:105, pieceRate:2.50, amount:262.50, status:"approved", note:"" },
  ]);
  const [showForm,  setShowForm]  = useState(false);
  const [form,      setForm]      = useState({ date:"", styleId:"", operationId:"", pieces:"", note:"", selectedCuts:[] });
  const [formErr,   setFormErr]   = useState("");
  const [saved,     setSaved]     = useState(false);
  const [entryFilter, setEntryFilter] = useState("all");
  const [applied,   setApplied]   = useState({});
  const [showJobs,  setShowJobs]  = useState(false);
  const wInfo = MOCK_DB.workers[0];

  const TODAY      = new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0];
  const pieceRate  = MOCK_DB.operations.find(o => o.id === form.operationId)?.pieceRate || 0;
  const autoAmount = (parseInt(form.pieces) || 0) * pieceRate;

  // Balance pieces — operation wise
  const balancePieces = (() => {
    if (!form.styleId || !form.operationId) return null;
    const allStyleCuts = (sharedCuts||[]).filter(c => c.styleId === form.styleId);
    const cuttingTotal = allStyleCuts.reduce((s,c) => s+(+c.totalPieces||0), 0);
    if (cuttingTotal === 0) return null;
    const allEntriesToCheck = [...(sharedEntries||[]), ...entries];
    const usedPieces = allEntriesToCheck
      .filter(e => e.styleId===form.styleId && e.operationId===form.operationId && e.status!=="rejected")
      .reduce((s,e) => s+(+e.pieces||0), 0);
    return { total: cuttingTotal, used: usedPieces, remaining: Math.max(0, cuttingTotal - usedPieces) };
  })();

  const approved = entries.filter(e => e.status === "approved");
  const totalAmt = approved.reduce((s,e) => s + e.amount, 0);
  const totalPcs = approved.reduce((s,e) => s + e.pieces, 0);

  const handleSubmit = () => {
    if (!form.styleId || !form.operationId || !form.pieces || !form.date) { setFormErr("सभी fields भरना जरूरी है।"); return; }
    if (parseInt(form.pieces) <= 0) { setFormErr("Pieces 0 से ज्यादा होनी चाहिए।"); return; }

    // Duplicate check
    const allEntries = [...(sharedEntries||[]), ...entries];
    const duplicate = allEntries.find(e =>
      (e.workerId===user.id || e.staffId===user.staffId) &&
      e.styleId===form.styleId &&
      e.operationId===form.operationId &&
      e.date===form.date &&
      e.status!=="rejected"
    );
    if (duplicate) { setFormErr(`⚠️ इस style+operation में ${form.date} को entry पहले से है! (${duplicate.pieces} pcs)`); return; }

    // Balance check
    if (balancePieces !== null && +form.pieces > balancePieces.remaining) {
      setFormErr(`⚠️ Pieces (${form.pieces}) balance (${balancePieces.remaining}) से ज्यादा हैं!`); return;
    }

    const style = MOCK_DB.styles.find(s => s.id === form.styleId);
    const op    = MOCK_DB.operations.find(o => o.id === form.operationId);
    const selCutsData = (form.selectedCuts||[]).map(id => {
      const c = (sharedCuts||[]).find(x=>x.id===id);
      return c ? { id:c.id, marker:c.marker, totalPieces:c.totalPieces, date:c.date } : null;
    }).filter(Boolean);

    const newEntry = {
      id:"se"+Date.now(), date:form.date,
      style:style?.styleName||"", styleName:style?.styleName||"",
      styleId:form.styleId, operationId:form.operationId,
      operation:op?.name||"", pieces:parseInt(form.pieces),
      pieceRate, amount:autoAmount, status:"pending", note:form.note,
      workerId:user.id||"w1", workerName:user.name||"Worker",
      staffId:user.staffId||"SG001", department:user.department||"Stitching",
      cuttingRefs: selCutsData,
    };
    setEntries(prev => [newEntry, ...prev]);
    if (sharedActions?.addEntry) sharedActions.addEntry(newEntry);
    setForm({ date:"", styleId:"", operationId:"", pieces:"", note:"", selectedCuts:[] });
    setFormErr(""); setShowForm(false); setSaved(true);
    setTimeout(()=>setSaved(false), 3000);
  };

  const TABS = [
    { id:"entry",    label:"My Work"  },
    { id:"payment",  label:"Payment"  },
    { id:"profile",  label:"Profile"  },
  ];

  const [profile, setProfile] = useState({
    name:       user.name,
    mobile:     user.mobile,
    staffId:    wInfo?.staffId     || "SG001",
    department: wInfo?.department  || "Stitching",
    joinDate:   wInfo?.joinDate    || "2022-03-15",
    address:    "Ludhiana, Punjab",
    emergency:  "",
    language:   "Hindi",
  });
  const [editMode,    setEditMode]    = useState(false);
  const [editProfile, setEditProfile] = useState(profile);
  const [profileSaved, setProfileSaved] = useState(false);

  const statusMeta = {
    pending:  { label:"Pending",  barColor:"bg-amber-400",  textColor:"text-amber-600",  bgColor:"bg-amber-50"  },
    approved: { label:"Approved", barColor:"bg-green-500",  textColor:"text-green-600",  bgColor:"bg-green-50"  },
    rejected: { label:"Rejected", barColor:"bg-red-400",    textColor:"text-red-500",    bgColor:"bg-red-50"    },
  };

  // 🔗 Sync worker entries with supervisor approvals + supervisor-added entries
  React.useEffect(() => {
    if (sharedEntries) {
      const myShared = sharedEntries.filter(e => e.workerId===user.id || e.staffId===user.staffId);
      if (myShared.length > 0) {
        setEntries(prev => {
          // Update status of existing entries
          const updated = prev.map(local => {
            const found = myShared.find(s => s.id === local.id);
            return found ? {...local, status: found.status} : local;
          });
          // Add new entries added by supervisor that don't exist locally
          const localIds = new Set(updated.map(e => e.id));
          const newFromSup = myShared.filter(e => !localIds.has(e.id));
          return [...newFromSup, ...updated];
        });
      }
    }
  }, [sharedEntries]);

  const filteredEntries = entryFilter === "all" ? entries : entries.filter(e => e.status === entryFilter);

  /* ── TAB: Approved Work ── */
  const ApprovedTab = () => (
    <div className="px-4 pt-5 pb-28 space-y-5">
      {/* Approved list — Date | Style | Operation | Qty | Rate | Amount */}
      <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-100 shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
        <div className="grid bg-gray-900 px-2 py-1.5" style={{gridTemplateColumns:"2fr 2.5fr 2.5fr 1.2fr 1.5fr 1.8fr"}}>
          {["Date","Style","Operation","Qty","Rate","Amount"].map((h,i)=>(
            <div key={h} className={"text-[9px] font-extrabold text-gray-300 uppercase tracking-wider "+(i>=3?"text-right":"")}>
              {h}
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
        {approved.length === 0 && (
          <div className="text-center py-10 text-gray-400 text-xs">कोई approved entry नहीं</div>
        )}
        {approved.map((e, idx)=>(
          <div key={e.id} className={"border-b border-gray-100 last:border-0 " + (idx%2===0?"bg-white":"bg-gray-50/40")}>
            <div className="grid px-2 py-2 items-center gap-x-1" style={{gridTemplateColumns:"2fr 2.5fr 2.5fr 1.2fr 1.5fr 1.8fr"}}>
              <div>
                <p className="text-gray-800 font-extrabold text-[11px] leading-none">{e.date?.slice(5)}</p>
                <p className="text-gray-400 text-[9px] mt-0.5">{e.date?.slice(0,4)}</p>
              </div>
              <div className="min-w-0 pr-1">
                <p className="text-gray-900 font-semibold text-[10px] truncate leading-tight">{e.style}</p>
              </div>
              <div className="min-w-0 pr-1">
                <span className="text-[9px] font-bold bg-blue-50 text-blue-600 px-1 py-0.5 rounded block truncate leading-tight">{e.operation}</span>
              </div>
              <div className="text-right">
                <p className="text-orange-500 font-extrabold text-[11px] leading-none">{e.pieces}</p>
                <p className="text-gray-400 text-[8px]">pcs</p>
              </div>
              <div className="text-right">
                <p className="text-gray-600 font-bold text-[10px] leading-none">&#8377;{(e.pieceRate||0).toFixed(2)}</p>
                <p className="text-gray-400 text-[8px]">/pc</p>
              </div>
              <div className="text-right">
                <p className="text-green-600 font-extrabold text-[11px] leading-none">&#8377;{(e.amount||0).toFixed(0)}</p>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
        {approved.length > 0 && (
          <div className="grid bg-gray-900 px-2 py-1.5 items-center" style={{gridTemplateColumns:"2fr 2.5fr 2.5fr 1.2fr 1.5fr 1.8fr"}}>
            <div className="col-span-1 text-gray-400 text-[9px] font-bold">{approved.length} rows</div>
            <div/>
            <div className="text-[9px] text-gray-400 font-bold">TOTAL</div>
            <div className="text-right text-orange-300 font-extrabold text-[10px]">{approved.reduce((s,e)=>s+(e.pieces||0),0)}</div>
            <div/>
            <div className="text-right text-green-400 font-extrabold text-[11px]">&#8377;{approved.reduce((s,e)=>s+(e.amount||0),0).toFixed(0)}</div>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );

  /* ── TAB: Self Entry ── */
  const SelfEntryTab = () => (
    <div className="px-4 pt-5 pb-28 space-y-4">
      {/* CTA */}
      <button onClick={()=>{setShowForm(true);setFormErr("");setForm({date:TODAY,styleId:"",operationId:"",pieces:"",note:""});}}
        className="w-full bg-orange-500 active:bg-orange-600 text-white font-extrabold text-base py-4 rounded-2xl shadow-md shadow-orange-200 active:scale-[0.98] transition flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
        <svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M12 5v14M5 12h14" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
        नई Entry डालें
      </button>

      {saved && (
        <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-2xl px-4 py-3 flex items-center gap-2">
          <div className="w-5 h-5 rounded-full bg-green-500 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
            <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 12 12" fill="none"><path d="M2 6l3 3 5-5" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
          </div>
          <p className="text-green-700 text-sm font-semibold">Entry submit हो गई — Supervisor verify करेगा</p>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Filter */}
      <div className="flex bg-gray-100 rounded-2xl p-1">
        {["all","pending","approved","rejected"].map(s=>(
          <button key={s} onClick={()=>setEntryFilter(s)}
            className={"flex-1 py-2 rounded-xl text-xs font-bold transition "+(entryFilter===s?"bg-white text-gray-900 shadow-sm":"text-gray-400")}>
            {s==="all"?"All":statusMeta[s].label}
          </button>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* List — Date | Style | Operation | Qty | Rate | Amount */}
      <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-100 shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
        <div className="grid bg-gray-900 px-2 py-1.5" style={{gridTemplateColumns:"2fr 2.5fr 2.5fr 1.2fr 1.5fr 1.8fr"}}>
          {["Date","Style","Operation","Qty","Rate","Amount"].map((h,i)=>(
            <div key={h} className={"text-[9px] font-extrabold text-gray-300 uppercase tracking-wider "+(i>=3?"text-right":"")}>
              {h}
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
        {filteredEntries.length===0 && (
          <div className="text-center py-10 text-gray-400 text-xs">कोई entry नहीं</div>
        )}
        {filteredEntries.map((e, idx)=>{
          const m = statusMeta[e.status];
          return (
            <div key={e.id} className={"border-b border-gray-100 last:border-0 " + (idx%2===0?"bg-white":"bg-gray-50/40")}>
              <div className={"h-0.5 "+m.barColor}/>
              <div className="grid px-2 py-2 items-center gap-x-1" style={{gridTemplateColumns:"2fr 2.5fr 2.5fr 1.2fr 1.5fr 1.8fr"}}>
                <div>
                  <p className="text-gray-800 font-extrabold text-[11px] leading-none">{e.date?.slice(5)}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-[9px] mt-0.5">{e.date?.slice(0,4)}</p>
                </div>
                <div className="min-w-0 pr-1">
                  <p className="text-gray-900 font-semibold text-[10px] truncate leading-tight">{e.style}</p>
                  <span className={"text-[9px] font-bold "+m.textColor}>{m.label}</span>
                </div>
                <div className="min-w-0 pr-1">
                  <span className="text-[9px] font-bold bg-blue-50 text-blue-600 px-1 py-0.5 rounded block truncate leading-tight">{e.operation}</span>
                  {e.note && <p className="text-[8px] text-gray-400 truncate mt-0.5">{e.note}</p>}
                </div>
                <div className="text-right">
                  <p className="text-orange-500 font-extrabold text-[11px] leading-none">{e.pieces}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-[8px]">pcs</p>
                </div>
                <div className="text-right">
                  <p className="text-gray-600 font-bold text-[10px] leading-none">&#8377;{(e.pieceRate||0).toFixed(2)}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-[8px]">/pc</p>
                </div>
                <div className="text-right">
                  <p className={"font-extrabold text-[11px] leading-none "+(e.status==="approved"?"text-green-600":e.status==="rejected"?"text-red-400":"text-gray-700")}>&#8377;{(e.amount||0).toFixed(0)}</p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          );
        })}
        {filteredEntries.length > 0 && (
          <div className="grid bg-gray-900 px-2 py-1.5 items-center" style={{gridTemplateColumns:"2fr 2.5fr 2.5fr 1.2fr 1.5fr 1.8fr"}}>
            <div className="text-gray-400 text-[9px] font-bold">{filteredEntries.length} rows</div>
            <div/>
            <div className="text-[9px] text-gray-400 font-bold">TOTAL</div>
            <div className="text-right text-orange-300 font-extrabold text-[10px]">{filteredEntries.reduce((s,e)=>s+(e.pieces||0),0)}</div>
            <div/>
            <div className="text-right text-green-400 font-extrabold text-[11px]">&#8377;{filteredEntries.reduce((s,e)=>s+(e.amount||0),0).toFixed(0)}</div>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Form Modal */}
      <Modal open={showForm} onClose={()=>setShowForm(false)} title="नई Work Entry">
        <div className="space-y-4">
          {formErr && <div className="bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-xl p-3 text-red-600 text-sm">{formErr}</div>}
          <Input label="Date" type="date" value={form.date} max={TODAY}
            onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({...f,date:e.target.value}))}/>

          <Select label="Style / Order" value={form.styleId}
            onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({...f,styleId:e.target.value,selectedCuts:[],pieces:""}))}>
            <option value="">-- Style चुनें --</option>
            {MOCK_DB.styles.filter(s=>s.status==="active").map(s=>(
              <option key={s.id} value={s.id}>{s.styleName}</option>
            ))}
          </Select>

          {/* Cutting Cards — style select ke baad auto show */}
          {form.styleId && (() => {
            const styleCuts = (sharedCuts||[]).filter(c => c.styleId === form.styleId);
            if (styleCuts.length === 0) return null;
            const selCuts = form.selectedCuts || [];
            const totalSelPcs = styleCuts.filter(c=>selCuts.includes(c.id)).reduce((s,c)=>s+(+c.totalPieces||0),0);
            return (
              <div className="space-y-2">
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                  <p className="text-xs font-extrabold text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wide">✂️ Cutting Records</p>
                  {selCuts.length > 0 && (
                    <span className="text-xs font-bold bg-orange-50 text-orange-600 border border-orange-200 px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full">
                      {selCuts.length} selected · {totalSelPcs} pcs
                    </span>
                  )}
                </div>
                {styleCuts.map(c => {
                  const isSel = selCuts.includes(c.id);
                  return (
                    <button key={c.id} type="button"
                      onClick={() => setForm(f => {
                        const newSel = isSel ? (f.selectedCuts||[]).filter(id=>id!==c.id) : [...(f.selectedCuts||[]),c.id];
                        const total = (sharedCuts||[]).filter(x=>newSel.includes(x.id)).reduce((s,x)=>s+(+x.totalPieces||0),0);
                        return { ...f, selectedCuts:newSel, pieces: total > 0 ? String(total) : f.pieces };
                      })}
                      className={`w-full text-left rounded-2xl border-2 p-3 transition-all active:scale-[0.98] ${isSel?"border-orange-400 bg-orange-50":"border-gray-200 bg-white"}`}>
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                        <div className={`w-6 h-6 rounded-lg border-2 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 ${isSel?"bg-orange-500 border-orange-500":"border-gray-300 bg-white"}`}>
                          {isSel && <svg width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M5 13l4 4L19 7" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/></svg>}
                        </div>
                        <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                          <p className={`font-extrabold text-sm ${isSel?"text-orange-700":"text-gray-800"}`}>
                            {c.marker ? `Cut No: ${c.marker}` : `Cut #${c.id.slice(-4)}`}
                          </p>
                          <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{c.date}</p>
                        </div>
                        <div className="text-right shrink-0">
                          <p className={`font-black text-xl ${isSel?"text-orange-600":"text-gray-700"}`}>{c.totalPieces}</p>
                          <p className="text-gray-400 text-[10px]">pieces</p>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    </button>
                  );
                })}
              </div>
            );
          })()}

          <Select label="Operation" value={form.operationId}
            onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({...f,operationId:e.target.value}))}>
            <option value="">-- Operation चुनें --</option>
            {MOCK_DB.operations.map(o=>(
              <option key={o.id} value={o.id}>{o.name} — Rs {o.pieceRate}/pc</option>
            ))}
          </Select>

          <Input label="Pieces" type="number" min="1" value={form.pieces} placeholder="कितने pieces?"
            onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({...f,pieces:e.target.value}))}/>

          {/* Balance Box */}
          {balancePieces !== null && (
            <div className={`rounded-xl border-2 overflow-hidden ${(+form.pieces||0)>balancePieces.remaining?"border-red-200":"border-blue-200"}`}>
              <div className="grid grid-cols-3 divide-x divide-gray-100">
                <div className="px-3 py-2.5 text-center bg-gray-50">
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-[10px] font-bold uppercase">Total Cut</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-800 font-black text-base">{balancePieces.total}</p>
                </div>
                <div className="px-3 py-2.5 text-center bg-gray-50">
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-[10px] font-bold uppercase">Used</p>
                  <p className="text-orange-600 font-black text-base">{balancePieces.used}</p>
                </div>
                <div className={`px-3 py-2.5 text-center ${(+form.pieces||0)>balancePieces.remaining?"bg-red-50":"bg-blue-50"}`}>
                  <p className={`text-[10px] font-bold uppercase ${(+form.pieces||0)>balancePieces.remaining?"text-red-400":"text-blue-400"}`}>Balance</p>
                  <p className={`font-black text-base ${(+form.pieces||0)>balancePieces.remaining?"text-red-600":"text-blue-600"}`}>
                    {Math.max(0, balancePieces.remaining-(+form.pieces||0))}
                  </p>
                </div>
              </div>
              {(+form.pieces||0) > balancePieces.remaining && (
                <div className="bg-red-50 px-3 py-1.5 border-t border-red-100">
                  <p className="text-red-500 text-xs font-bold text-center">⚠️ Pieces balance से ज्यादा हैं!</p>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          )}

          {form.pieces && form.operationId && (
            <div className="bg-orange-50 border border-orange-100 rounded-xl px-4 py-3">
              <p className="text-orange-700 font-extrabold text-lg">Rs {autoAmount.toFixed(2)}</p>
              <p className="text-orange-400 text-xs">{form.pieces} pcs × Rs {pieceRate}/pc</p>
            </div>
          )}
          <Input label="Note (optional)" value={form.note} placeholder="कोई comment?"
            onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({...f,note:e.target.value}))}/>
          <div className="bg-amber-50 border border-amber-100 rounded-xl p-3 text-xs text-amber-700 leading-relaxed">
            Submit करने पर entry <strong>Pending</strong> रहेगी। Supervisor verify करने पर <strong>Approved</strong> होगी।
          </div>
          <div className="flex gap-3">
            <Btn variant="secondary" className="flex-1" onClick={()=>setShowForm(false)}>Cancel</Btn>
            <Btn className="flex-1" onClick={handleSubmit}>Submit →</Btn>
          </div>
        </div>
      </Modal>
    </div>
  );

  /* ── TAB: Jobs ── */
  const JobsTab = () => {
    const jobs = MOCK_DB.jobs.filter(j=>j.status==="active");
    return (
      <div className="px-4 pt-5 pb-28 space-y-4">
        <div className="rounded-3xl p-5" style={{background:"linear-gradient(135deg,#1D4ED8,#3B82F6)"}}>
          <p className="text-blue-200 text-xs font-bold uppercase tracking-widest">Available Now</p>
          <p className="text-white text-4xl font-black mt-1">{jobs.length} Jobs</p>
          <p className="text-blue-200 text-sm mt-1">Sharma Garments Pvt Ltd</p>
        </div>
        <div className="space-y-3">
          {jobs.map(job=>(
            <div key={job.id} className="bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-2xl shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
              <div className="h-1 bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-400 to-blue-600"/>
              <div className="p-4">
                <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-2 mb-3">
                  <div>
                    <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold">{job.title}</p>
                    <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs mt-0.5">{job.department}</p>
                  </div>
                  <span className="bg-blue-50 text-blue-600 text-xs font-bold px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full border border-blue-100 shrink-0">{job.openings} posts</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-3">
                  <span className="bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 text-gray-600 text-xs font-semibold px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl">{job.salary}</span>
                  <span className="bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 text-gray-600 text-xs font-semibold px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl">{job.experience} exp</span>
                </div>
                {job.description && <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs leading-relaxed mb-3">{job.description}</p>}
                {applied[job.id] ? (
                  <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-xl py-2.5 text-center text-green-600 text-sm font-bold">✓ Applied!</div>
                ) : (
                  <button onClick={()=>setApplied(a=>({...a,[job.id]:true}))}
                    className="w-full bg-blue-500 active:bg-blue-600 text-white font-bold text-sm py-3 rounded-xl active:scale-[0.98] transition">
                    Apply Now
                  </button>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  };

  /* ── TAB: Profile ── */
  const ProfileTab = () => {
    const saveProfile = () => {
      setProfile(editProfile);
      setEditMode(false);
      setProfileSaved(true);
      setTimeout(() => setProfileSaved(false), 2500);
    };
    const field = (label, key, type="text", opts=null) => (
      <div key={key} className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-gray-50 last:border-0">
        <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs font-semibold mb-1">{label}</p>
        {editMode ? (
          opts ? (
            <select value={editProfile[key]} onChange={e=>setEditProfile(p=>({...p,[key]:e.target.value}))}
              className="w-full bg-gray-50 border border-orange-300 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 text-gray-900 text-sm font-semibold focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-500" style={{fontSize:"16px"}}>
              {opts.map(o=><option key={o}>{o}</option>)}
            </select>
          ) : (
            <input type={type} value={editProfile[key]}
              onChange={e=>setEditProfile(p=>({...p,[key]:e.target.value}))}
              className="w-full bg-gray-50 border border-orange-300 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 text-gray-900 text-sm font-semibold focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-500" style={{fontSize:"16px"}}/>
          )
        ) : (
          <p className="text-gray-900 text-sm font-bold">{profile[key] || <span className="text-gray-300 font-normal">—</span>}</p>
        )}
      </div>
    );

    return (
      <><div className="px-4 pt-5 pb-28 space-y-4">
        {profileSaved && (
          <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-2xl px-4 py-3 flex items-center gap-2">
            <div className="w-5 h-5 rounded-full bg-green-500 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
              <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 12 12" fill="none"><path d="M2 6l3 3 5-5" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
            </div>
            <p className="text-green-700 text-sm font-semibold">Profile save हो गई!</p>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Edit / Save button */}
        <div className="flex gap-2">
          {editMode ? (
            <>
              <button onClick={()=>{setEditMode(false);setEditProfile(profile);}}
                className="flex-1 bg-gray-100 border border-gray-200 text-gray-700 font-bold text-sm py-3 rounded-2xl active:scale-[0.98] transition">
                Cancel
              </button>
              <button onClick={saveProfile}
                className="flex-1 bg-orange-500 text-white font-bold text-sm py-3 rounded-2xl shadow-md shadow-orange-200 active:scale-[0.98] transition">
                Save Changes
              </button>
            </>
          ) : (
            <button onClick={()=>{setEditMode(true);setEditProfile(profile);}}
              className="flex-1 bg-white border-2 border-orange-400 text-orange-500 font-bold text-sm py-3 rounded-2xl active:scale-[0.98] transition flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
              <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M11 4H4a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v14a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h14a2 2 0 0 0 2-2v-7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/><path d="M18.5 2.5a2.12 2.12 0 0 1 3 3L12 15l-4 1 1-4z" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
              Edit Profile
            </button>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* Personal Info */}
        <div className="bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-2xl shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
          <div className="px-4 py-3 bg-gray-50 border-b border-gray-100 flex items-center justify-between">
            <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wider">Personal Info</p>
            {editMode && <span className="text-orange-400 text-xs font-bold">Editing...</span>}
          </div>
          {field("Full Name / पूरा नाम",   "name")}
          {field("Mobile / मोबाइल",         "mobile",   "tel")}
          {field("Address / पता",            "address")}
          {field("Emergency Contact",        "emergency","tel")}
          {field("Language",                 "language", "text", ["Hindi","English","Hindi + English"])}
        </div>

        {/* Work Info — view only */}
        <div className="bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-2xl shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
          <div className="px-4 py-3 bg-gray-50 border-b border-gray-100">
            <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wider">Work Info (Read Only)</p>
          </div>
          {[
            { label:"Staff ID",   value: profile.staffId    },
            { label:"Department", value: profile.department },
            { label:"Join Date",  value: profile.joinDate   },
            { label:"Factory",    value: user.tenantName || "Sharma Garments" },
            { label:"Status",     value: "Active" },
          ].map(item=>(
            <div key={item.label} className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3.5 border-b border-gray-50 last:border-0">
              <span className="text-gray-500 text-sm">{item.label}</span>
              <span className="text-gray-900 text-sm font-bold">{item.value}</span>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* Jobs Button */}
        <button onClick={()=>setShowJobs(true)}
          className="w-full bg-blue-500 text-white font-extrabold text-sm py-4 rounded-2xl shadow-md shadow-blue-200 active:scale-[0.98] active:bg-blue-600 transition flex items-center justify-center gap-3">
          <svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><rect x="2" y="7" width="20" height="14" rx="2" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2" fill="none"/><path d="M16 7V5a2 2 0 0 0-2-2h-4a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v2M12 12v4M10 14h4" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
          Available Jobs
          <span className="bg-white text-blue-600 text-xs font-black px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full">{MOCK_DB.jobs.filter(j=>j.status==="active").length}</span>
        </button>

        {/* Logout */}
        <button onClick={onLogout}
          className="w-full bg-red-50 border border-red-200 text-red-500 font-bold text-sm py-4 rounded-2xl active:scale-[0.98] transition">
          Sign Out / लॉगआउट
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* Jobs Full Panel */}
      {showJobs && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-gray-50 flex flex-col" style={{fontFamily:"'DM Sans','Segoe UI',sans-serif"}}>
          {/* Header */}
          <div className="bg-white border-b border-gray-100 px-4 py-4 flex items-center gap-3 shadow-sm">
            <button onClick={()=>setShowJobs(false)}
              className="w-9 h-9 rounded-xl bg-gray-100 flex items-center justify-center active:scale-95 transition">
              <svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M15 18l-6-6 6-6" stroke="#374151" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/></svg>
            </button>
            <div>
              <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-base">Available Jobs</p>
              <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{MOCK_DB.jobs.filter(j=>j.status==="active").length} openings • Sharma Garments</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Jobs List */}
          <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto px-4 py-4 space-y-3 pb-8">
            {/* Banner */}
            <div className="rounded-3xl p-5" style={{background:"linear-gradient(135deg,#1D4ED8,#3B82F6)"}}>
              <p className="text-blue-200 text-xs font-bold uppercase tracking-widest">Hiring Now</p>
              <p className="text-white text-3xl font-black mt-1">{MOCK_DB.jobs.filter(j=>j.status==="active").length} Jobs Open</p>
              <p className="text-blue-200 text-sm mt-1">Sharma Garments Pvt Ltd</p>
            </div>

            {MOCK_DB.jobs.map(job=>(
              <div key={job.id} className="bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-2xl shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
                <div className="h-1 bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-400 to-blue-600"/>
                <div className="p-4">
                  <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-2 mb-2">
                    <div>
                      <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold">{job.title}</p>
                      <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs mt-0.5">{job.department} · {job.posted||job.postedDate||""}</p>
                    </div>
                    <span className={`text-xs font-bold px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full border shrink-0 ${job.status==="active"?"bg-green-50 text-green-600 border-green-200":"bg-gray-50 text-gray-400 border-gray-200"}`}>
                      {job.openings} posts
                    </span>
                  </div>
                  <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-3">
                    {job.salary && <span className="bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 text-gray-600 text-xs font-semibold px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl">{job.salary}</span>}
                    {job.experience && <span className="bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 text-gray-600 text-xs font-semibold px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl">{job.experience} exp</span>}
                  </div>
                  {job.description && <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs leading-relaxed mb-3">{job.description}</p>}
                  {job.status==="active" && (
                    applied[job.id] ? (
                      <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-xl py-2.5 text-center text-green-600 text-sm font-bold">✓ Applied!</div>
                    ) : (
                      <button onClick={()=>setApplied(a=>({...a,[job.id]:true}))}
                        className="w-full bg-blue-500 active:bg-blue-600 text-white font-bold text-sm py-3 rounded-xl active:scale-[0.98] transition">
                        Apply Now
                      </button>
                    )
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </>
    );
  };
  const PaymentHistoryTab = () => {
    const [period, setPeriod]     = useState("monthly");
    const [selMonth, setSelMonth] = useState(() => {
      const d = new Date();
      return `${d.getFullYear()}-${String(d.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,"0")}`;
    });
    const [selHalf, setSelHalf]   = useState("1");

    const monthOptions = Array.from({length:6}, (_,i) => {
      const d = new Date(); d.setMonth(d.getMonth()-i);
      const val   = `${d.getFullYear()}-${String(d.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,"0")}`;
      const label = d.toLocaleString("hi-IN", {month:"long", year:"numeric"});
      return { val, label };
    });

    const periodEntries = approved.filter(e => {
      if (!e.date) return false;
      const [yr, mo, day] = e.date.split("-");
      const em = `${yr}-${mo}`;
      if (period === "monthly")   return em === selMonth;
      if (period === "halfmonth") {
        if (em !== selMonth) return false;
        const d = parseInt(day);
        return selHalf === "1" ? d <= 15 : d >= 16;
      }
      return false;
    });

    const grossAmt  = periodEntries.reduce((s,e) => s+(e.amount||0), 0);
    const totalPcsP = periodEntries.reduce((s,e) => s+(e.pieces||0), 0);
    const deductions = MOCK_DB.payments.find(p => p.staffId === wInfo?.staffId)?.deductions || 0;
    const netAmt    = Math.max(0, grossAmt - deductions);

    const [yr, mo] = selMonth.split("-");
    const monthName   = new Date(+yr,+mo-1).toLocaleString("hi-IN",{month:"long",year:"numeric"});
    const periodLabel = period==="monthly" ? monthName : selHalf==="1" ? `1–15 ${monthName}` : `16–31 ${monthName}`;

    const byStyle = {};
    periodEntries.forEach(e => {
      if (!byStyle[e.style]) byStyle[e.style] = {style:e.style, pieces:0, amount:0};
      byStyle[e.style].pieces += e.pieces||0;
      byStyle[e.style].amount += e.amount||0;
    });

    return (
      <div className="px-4 pt-5 pb-28 space-y-4">

        {/* Period toggle */}
        <div className="flex bg-gray-100 rounded-2xl p-1 gap-1">
          {[{id:"monthly",label:"📅 Monthly"},{id:"halfmonth",label:"📆 15 Din"}].map(p=>(
            <button key={p.id} onClick={()=>setPeriod(p.id)}
              className={"flex-1 py-2.5 rounded-xl text-xs font-extrabold transition "+(period===p.id?"bg-white text-orange-600 shadow-sm":"text-gray-400")}>
              {p.label}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* Selectors */}
        <div className="flex gap-2">
          <div className="flex-1 relative">
            <select value={selMonth} onChange={e=>setSelMonth(e.target.value)}
              className="w-full bg-white border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-2xl px-4 py-3 text-gray-900 font-bold focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-400 appearance-none pr-8"
              style={{fontSize:"15px"}}>
              {monthOptions.map(m=><option key={m.val} value={m.val}>{m.label}</option>)}
            </select>
            <span className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-orange-400 pointer-events-none text-sm">▾</span>
          </div>
          {period==="halfmonth" && (
            <div className="relative">
              <select value={selHalf} onChange={e=>setSelHalf(e.target.value)}
                className="bg-white border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-2xl px-4 py-3 text-gray-900 font-bold focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-400 appearance-none pr-8"
                style={{fontSize:"15px"}}>
                <option value="1">1–15</option>
                <option value="2">16–31</option>
              </select>
              <span className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-orange-400 pointer-events-none text-sm">▾</span>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* Payment Slip */}
        <div className="bg-white rounded-3xl border-2 border-orange-100 overflow-hidden shadow-sm">

          {/* Slip Header */}
          <div className="bg-gray-900 px-5 py-4">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2.5">
                <GarmentLogo size={28}/>
                <div>
                  <p className="text-white font-extrabold text-sm">Sharma Garments</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-[10px]">Payment Slip</p>
                </div>
              </div>
              <div className="text-right">
                <p className="text-orange-400 text-[10px] font-bold uppercase">Period</p>
                <p className="text-white text-xs font-extrabold">{periodLabel}</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="bg-white/10 rounded-xl px-3 py-2.5 flex items-center justify-between">
              <div>
                <p className="text-white font-extrabold text-sm">{profile.name}</p>
                <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{profile.staffId} · {profile.department}</p>
              </div>
              <div className="text-right">
                <p className="text-gray-400 text-[10px]">Join Date</p>
                <p className="text-white text-xs font-bold">{profile.joinDate}</p>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          {periodEntries.length === 0 ? (
            <div className="py-14 text-center">
              <p className="text-4xl mb-2">📋</p>
              <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm font-semibold">इस period में कोई approved entry नहीं</p>
              <p className="text-gray-300 text-xs mt-1">{periodLabel}</p>
            </div>
          ) : (
            <>
              {/* Work entries table */}
              <div className="overflow-x-auto">
                <div className="min-w-[480px]">
                  <div className="grid bg-gray-50 border-b border-gray-100 px-3 py-2" style={{gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 2fr 2fr 0.8fr 1fr 1.2fr"}}>
                    {["Date","Style","Operation","Pcs","Rate","Amount"].map((h,i)=>(
                      <p key={h} className={"text-[9px] font-extrabold text-gray-400 uppercase tracking-wide "+(i>=3?"text-right":"")}>
                        {h}
                      </p>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                  {periodEntries.map((e,idx)=>(
                    <div key={e.id} className={"grid px-3 py-2.5 border-b border-gray-50 last:border-0 items-center "+(idx%2===0?"bg-white":"bg-gray-50/40")} style={{gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 2fr 2fr 0.8fr 1fr 1.2fr"}}>
                      <p className="text-gray-500 text-[10px] font-semibold">{e.date?.slice(5)}</p>
                      <p className="text-gray-800 text-[10px] font-semibold truncate pr-1">{e.style}</p>
                      <p className="text-gray-600 text-[10px] truncate pr-1">{e.operation}</p>
                      <p className="text-gray-800 text-[10px] font-bold text-right">{e.pieces}</p>
                      <p className="text-gray-500 text-[10px] text-right">₹{e.pieceRate}</p>
                      <p className="text-green-600 text-[10px] font-extrabold text-right">₹{(e.amount||0).toFixed(0)}</p>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* Style-wise summary */}
              {Object.keys(byStyle).length > 1 && (
                <div className="px-4 py-3 border-t border-gray-100 bg-blue-50/40">
                  <p className="text-gray-500 text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wide mb-2">Style Summary</p>
                  <div className="space-y-2">
                    {Object.values(byStyle).map(s=>(
                      <div key={s.style} className="flex items-center justify-between">
                        <p className="text-gray-700 text-xs font-semibold">{s.style}</p>
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-4">
                          <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{s.pieces} pcs</p>
                          <p className="text-green-600 text-xs font-extrabold">₹{s.amount.toFixed(0)}</p>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}

              {/* Totals */}
              <div className="border-t-2 border-dashed border-gray-200 px-4 py-4 space-y-2.5 bg-gray-50">
                <div className="flex justify-between">
                  <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs">Total Entries</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-700 text-xs font-extrabold">{periodEntries.length} entries</p>
                </div>
                <div className="flex justify-between">
                  <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs">Total Pieces</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-700 text-xs font-extrabold">{totalPcsP} pcs</p>
                </div>
                <div className="flex justify-between">
                  <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs">Gross Amount</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-700 text-xs font-extrabold">₹{grossAmt.toFixed(2)}</p>
                </div>
                {deductions > 0 && (
                  <div className="flex justify-between">
                    <p className="text-red-500 text-xs">Deductions</p>
                    <p className="text-red-500 text-xs font-extrabold">– ₹{deductions}</p>
                  </div>
                )}
                <div className="flex justify-between items-center pt-2 border-t-2 border-gray-200">
                  <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-sm">Net Payable</p>
                  <p className="text-green-600 font-black text-xl">₹{netAmt.toFixed(0)}</p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </>
          )}

          {/* Footer */}
          <div className="px-4 py-2.5 bg-orange-50 border-t border-orange-100 flex justify-between">
            <p className="text-orange-400 text-[10px]">System Generated Slip</p>
            <p className="text-orange-400 text-[10px] font-bold">{new Date().toLocaleDateString("hi-IN")}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  };

  /* ── ICONS ── */
  const TabIcons = {
    approved: <svg width="22" height="22" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M9 12l2 2 4-4" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="9" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7"/></svg>,
    entry:    <svg width="22" height="22" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M11 4H4a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v14a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h14a2 2 0 0 0 2-2v-7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" strokeLinecap="round" fill="none"/><path d="M18.5 2.5a2.12 2.12 0 0 1 3 3L12 15l-4 1 1-4z" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" strokeLinecap="round" fill="none"/></svg>,
    payment:  <svg width="22" height="22" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><rect x="2" y="5" width="20" height="14" rx="2" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" fill="none"/><path d="M2 9h20" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7"/><path d="M6 14h4" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>,
    jobs:     <svg width="22" height="22" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><rect x="2" y="7" width="20" height="14" rx="2" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" fill="none"/><path d="M16 7V5a2 2 0 0 0-2-2h-4a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v2" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>,
    profile:  <svg width="22" height="22" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><circle cx="12" cy="8" r="4" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" fill="none"/><path d="M4 20c0-4 3.6-7 8-7s8 3 8 7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" strokeLinecap="round" fill="none"/></svg>,
  };
  const TAB_TITLE = { approved:"Approved Work", entry:"My Work", payment:"Payment History", jobs:"Jobs", profile:"Profile" };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-50" style={{fontFamily:"'DM Sans','Segoe UI',sans-serif"}}>
      

      {/* Content */}
      <main className="max-w-lg mx-auto">
        {tab==="entry"    && SelfEntryTab()}
        {tab==="payment"  && <PaymentHistoryTab/>}
        {tab==="profile"  && ProfileTab()}
      </main>

      {/* Bottom nav */}
      <nav className="fixed bottom-0 left-0 right-0 z-30 bg-white border-t border-gray-100 shadow-[0_-4px_20px_rgba(0,0,0,0.06)]" style={{paddingBottom:"env(safe-area-inset-bottom)"}}>
        <div className="flex max-w-lg mx-auto">
          {TABS.map(t=>(
            <button key={t.id} onClick={()=>setTab(t.id)}
              className={"flex-1 flex flex-col items-center py-3 gap-0.5 transition "+(tab===t.id?"text-orange-500":"text-gray-400")}>
              <div className={tab===t.id?"scale-110 transition-transform":""}>
                {TabIcons[t.id]}
              </div>
              <span className="text-xs font-bold">{t.label}</span>
              {tab===t.id && <div className="w-4 h-0.5 rounded-full bg-orange-500 mt-0.5"/>}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>
      </nav>
    </div>
  );
};

// SelfEntry alias kept for admin/supervisor navigation
const SelfEntry = () => {
