const Dashboard = () => {
  const { user } = useContext(AppContext);
  const [styleFilter, setStyleFilter] = useState("all");
  const [hourlyDept, setHourlyDept]   = useState("all");
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab]     = useState("active");
  const isAdmin = user.role === "admin";

  // ── 1. Hourly grouped by dept ──
  const hourlyByDept = MOCK_DB.hourlyReports.reduce((acc, h) => {
    if (!acc[h.department]) acc[h.department] = { department: h.department, slots: [], totalPass: 0, totalAlter: 0, totalReject: 0, totalPieces: 0 };
    acc[h.department].slots.push(h);
    acc[h.department].totalPass    += h.pass;
    acc[h.department].totalAlter   += h.alter;
    acc[h.department].totalReject  += h.reject;
    acc[h.department].totalPieces  += h.total;
    return acc;
  }, {});
  const hourlyDepts   = Object.values(hourlyByDept);
  const filteredHourly = hourlyDept === "all" ? hourlyDepts : hourlyDepts.filter(d => d.department === hourlyDept);

  // ── 2. Style-wise ──
  const styleReport = MOCK_DB.styles.map(style => {
    const entries       = MOCK_DB.workEntries.filter(e => e.styleId === style.id);
    const entryPieces   = entries.reduce((s, e) => s + e.pieces, 0);
    const entryAmount   = entries.reduce((s, e) => s + e.amount, 0);
    const uniqueWorkers = new Set(entries.map(e => e.workerId)).size;
    const deptBreakdown = entries.reduce((acc, e) => { acc[e.department] = (acc[e.department] || 0) + e.pieces; return acc; }, {});
    const pct = Math.round((style.completedQty / style.totalQuantity) * 100);
    return { ...style, entryPieces, entryAmount, uniqueWorkers, deptBreakdown, pct };
  });

  // ── 3. Today active/inactive ──
  const mockToday = "2024-01-15";
  const todayActiveIds = new Set(MOCK_DB.workEntries.filter(e => e.date === mockToday).map(e => e.workerId));
  const deptAttendance = MOCK_DB.departments.map(dept => {
    const ws      = MOCK_DB.workers.filter(w => w.departmentId === dept.id);
    const active   = ws.filter(w => todayActiveIds.has(w.id));
    const inactive = ws.filter(w => !todayActiveIds.has(w.id));
    return { ...dept, totalWorkers: ws.length, active, inactive };
  });
  const totalActive   = deptAttendance.reduce((s, d) => s + d.active.length, 0);
  const totalInactive = deptAttendance.reduce((s, d) => s + d.inactive.length, 0);

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">





      {/* =====================================================
          ADMIN SECTION 1 — Hourly Report
      ===================================================== */}
      {isAdmin && (() => {
        // Group all slots by hourSlot time
        const allSlots = MOCK_DB.hourlyReports.filter(h =>
          hourlyDept === "all" || h.department === hourlyDept
        );
        const bySlot = allSlots.reduce((acc, h) => {
          if (!acc[h.hourSlot]) acc[h.hourSlot] = [];
          acc[h.hourSlot].push(h);
          return acc;
        }, {});
        const slotKeys = Object.keys(bySlot).sort();

        return (
          <div className="space-y-3">
            {/* Header */}
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between flex-wrap gap-3">
              <h3 className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-base">Hourly Report</h3>
              <select value={hourlyDept} onChange={e => setHourlyDept(e.target.value)}
                className="bg-white border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-3 py-1.5 text-gray-700 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-400">
                <option value="all">All Departments</option>
                {MOCK_DB.departments.map(d => <option key={d.id} value={d.name}>{d.name}</option>)}
              </select>
            </div>

            {slotKeys.length === 0 && (
              <p className="text-center py-8 text-gray-400 text-sm bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-200">कोई data नहीं</p>
            )}

            {slotKeys.map(slot => {
              const rows = bySlot[slot];
              const slotTotal = rows.reduce((s, r) => s + r.pass, 0);
              return (
                <div key={slot} className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 overflow-hidden">
                  {/* Slot header */}
                  <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2.5 bg-gray-800">
                    <span className="text-white font-extrabold text-sm">{slot}</span>
                    <span className="text-green-400 font-extrabold text-sm">{slotTotal} pcs</span>
                  </div>
                  {/* Table header */}
                  <div className="grid grid-cols-2 px-4 py-2 bg-gray-100 text-xs font-extrabold text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wide">
                    <div>Department</div>
                    <div className="text-right">Pass Pieces</div>
                  </div>
                  {/* Rows */}
                  {rows.map((r, i) => (
                    <div key={r.id} className={"grid grid-cols-2 px-4 py-3 items-center border-t border-gray-50 " + (i % 2 === 0 ? "bg-white" : "bg-gray-50/40")}>
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                        <span className="w-2.5 h-2.5 rounded-full shrink-0" style={{ background: DEPT_COLORS[r.department] || "#64748B" }} />
                        <span className="text-gray-800 font-semibold text-sm">{r.department}</span>
                      </div>
                      <div className="text-right">
                        <span className="text-green-600 font-extrabold text-sm">{r.pass} pcs</span>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        );
      })()}

      {/* =====================================================
          ADMIN SECTION 2 — Style-wise Report
      ===================================================== */}
      {isAdmin && (
        <div className="bg-gray-50 rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 p-5 space-y-4">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between flex-wrap gap-3">
            <div>
              <h3 className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-base">Style-wise Production Report</h3>
              <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs mt-0.5">Progress, earnings, workers per style</p>
            </div>
            <select value={styleFilter} onChange={e => setStyleFilter(e.target.value)}
              className="bg-white border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 text-gray-700 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-400">
              <option value="all">All Styles</option>
              <option value="active">Active</option>
              <option value="completed">Completed</option>
            </select>
          </div>
          <div className="space-y-4">
            {styleReport.filter(s => styleFilter === "all" || s.status === styleFilter).map(s => (
              <div key={s.id} className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-100 overflow-hidden">
                <div className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-gray-50 flex items-start justify-between gap-2 flex-wrap">
                  <div>
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-wrap">
                      <span className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-sm">{s.styleName}</span>
                      <span className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{s.styleNumber}</span>
                      <Badge color={s.status === "completed" ? "green" : "blue"} size="xs">{s.status}</Badge>
                    </div>
                    <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs mt-0.5">Buyer: {s.buyer} — Target: {s.targetDate}</p>
                  </div>
                  <span className="text-orange-500 font-extrabold text-lg">{s.pct}%</span>
                </div>
                <div className="px-4 pt-3">
                  <div className="w-full bg-gray-100 rounded-full h-2.5">
                    <div className="h-2.5 rounded-full" style={{ width: s.pct + "%", background: s.pct === 100 ? "#10B981" : "#F97316" }} />
                  </div>
                  <div className="flex justify-between text-xs text-gray-400 mt-1">
                    <span>{s.completedQty.toLocaleString()} done</span>
                    <span>{(s.totalQuantity - s.completedQty).toLocaleString()} left</span>
                    <span>{s.totalQuantity.toLocaleString()} total</span>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-px bg-gray-100 mt-3">
                  {[
                    { label: "Entry Pieces", value: s.entryPieces.toLocaleString(), color: "text-orange-500" },
                    { label: "Entry Amount", value: "Rs " + s.entryAmount.toLocaleString(), color: "text-green-600" },
                    { label: "Workers", value: s.uniqueWorkers, color: "text-blue-600" },
                  ].map(st => (
                    <div key={st.label} className="bg-white px-3 py-2.5 text-center">
                      <p className={"font-extrabold text-sm " + st.color}>{st.value}</p>
                      <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{st.label}</p>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
                {Object.keys(s.deptBreakdown).length > 0 && (
                  <div className="px-4 py-3">
                    <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs font-bold uppercase tracking-wide mb-2">Dept Breakup</p>
                    <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                      {Object.entries(s.deptBreakdown).map(([dept, pcs]) => (
                        <span key={dept} className="flex items-center gap-1.5 bg-gray-50 border border-gray-100 rounded-lg px-2.5 py-1 text-xs font-semibold text-gray-700">
                          <span className="w-2 h-2 rounded-full" style={{ background: DEPT_COLORS[dept] || "#64748B" }} />
                          {dept}: {pcs} pcs
                        </span>
                      ))}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* =====================================================
          ADMIN SECTION 3 — Today Active/Inactive Dept-wise
      ===================================================== */}
      {isAdmin && (
        <div className="bg-gray-50 rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 p-5 space-y-4">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between flex-wrap gap-3">
            <div>
              <h3 className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-base">Today Worker Status — Department Wise</h3>
              <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs mt-0.5">Active = work entry submitted today</p>
            </div>
            <div className="flex bg-white border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-xl overflow-hidden text-xs font-bold">
              {[["active", "Active"], ["inactive", "Inactive"], ["all", "All"]].map(([k, l]) => (
                <button key={k} onClick={() => setActiveTab(k)}
                  className={"px-3 py-2 transition " + (activeTab === k ? "bg-gray-800 text-white" : "text-gray-600 hover:bg-gray-50")}>
                  {l}
                </button>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>

          <div className="flex gap-3 flex-wrap">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-xl px-4 py-2">
              <span className="w-2.5 h-2.5 rounded-full bg-green-500" />
              <span className="text-green-700 font-extrabold text-sm">{totalActive} Active</span>
            </div>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-xl px-4 py-2">
              <span className="w-2.5 h-2.5 rounded-full bg-red-400" />
              <span className="text-red-600 font-extrabold text-sm">{totalInactive} Inactive</span>
            </div>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 bg-gray-100 border border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-4 py-2">
              <span className="text-gray-700 font-extrabold text-sm">{totalActive + totalInactive} Total</span>
              <span className="text-gray-400 text-xs">
                ({totalActive + totalInactive > 0 ? Math.round((totalActive / (totalActive + totalInactive)) * 100) : 0}% present)
              </span>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div className="grid sm:grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            {deptAttendance.map(dept => {
              const showWorkers  = activeTab === "active" ? dept.active : activeTab === "inactive" ? dept.inactive : [...dept.active, ...dept.inactive];
              const deptColor    = dept.color || "#64748B";
              const attendRate   = dept.totalWorkers > 0 ? Math.round((dept.active.length / dept.totalWorkers) * 100) : 0;
              return (
                <div key={dept.id} className="bg-white rounded-xl border border-gray-100 overflow-hidden">
                  <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2.5" style={{ borderLeft: "4px solid " + deptColor }}>
                    <div>
                      <span className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-sm">{dept.name}</span>
                      <span className="text-gray-400 text-xs ml-1.5">{dept.nameHindi}</span>
                    </div>
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-xs">
                      <span className="text-green-600 font-bold">{dept.active.length} active</span>
                      <span className="text-red-500 font-bold">{dept.inactive.length} absent</span>
                      <span className="bg-gray-100 text-gray-600 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full font-bold">{attendRate}%</span>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <div className="px-4 py-1.5">
                    <div className="w-full bg-gray-100 rounded-full h-1.5">
                      <div className="h-1.5 rounded-full bg-green-400" style={{ width: attendRate + "%" }} />
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  {showWorkers.length > 0 ? (
                    <div className="px-4 pb-3 space-y-1.5 mt-1">
                      {showWorkers.map(w => {
                        const isAct = todayActiveIds.has(w.id);
                        return (
                          <div key={w.id} className="flex items-center gap-2">
                            <span className={"w-2 h-2 rounded-full shrink-0 " + (isAct ? "bg-green-500" : "bg-red-400")} />
                            <span className="text-gray-800 text-xs font-medium flex-1">{w.name}</span>
                            <span className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{w.staffId}</span>
                            <span className={"text-xs font-bold " + (isAct ? "text-green-600" : "text-red-400")}>
                              {isAct ? "Active" : "Absent"}
                            </span>
                          </div>
                        );
                      })}
                    </div>
                  ) : (
                    <p className="px-4 pb-3 text-gray-300 text-xs italic">No workers in this view</p>
                  )}
                </div>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Style Progress (non-admin) */}
      {!isAdmin && (
        <div className="bg-gray-50 rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 p-5">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
            <h3 className="text-gray-900 font-semibold">Style Progress</h3>
            <select value={styleFilter} onChange={e => setStyleFilter(e.target.value)}
              className="bg-gray-100 border border-gray-200 rounded-lg px-3 py-1.5 text-gray-700 text-sm focus:outline-none">
              <option value="all">All</option>
              <option value="active">Active</option>
              <option value="completed">Completed</option>
            </select>
          </div>
          <div className="space-y-3">
            {MOCK_DB.styles.filter(s => styleFilter === "all" || s.status === styleFilter).map(style => {
              const pct = Math.round((style.completedQty / style.totalQuantity) * 100);
              return (
                <div key={style.id} className="bg-gray-100 rounded-xl p-4">
                  <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-3 mb-2">
                    <div>
                      <span className="text-gray-900 text-sm font-medium">{style.styleName}</span>
                      <span className="ml-2 text-gray-700 text-xs">{style.styleNumber}</span>
                    </div>
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                      <Badge color={style.status === "completed" ? "green" : "blue"} size="xs">{style.status}</Badge>
                      <span className="text-orange-400 font-bold text-sm">{pct}%</span>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <div className="w-full bg-gray-200 rounded-full h-2">
                    <div className="h-2 rounded-full" style={{ width: pct + "%", background: pct === 100 ? "#10B981" : "#F97316" }} />
                  </div>
                  <div className="flex justify-between mt-1.5 text-xs text-gray-900">
                    <span>{style.completedQty.toLocaleString()} / {style.totalQuantity.toLocaleString()} pcs</span>
                    <span>Buyer: {style.buyer}</span>
                  </div>
                </div>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

    </div>
  );
};

// WORK ENTRY
// ============================================================
// OPERATION BALANCE TRACKER (shared state for rules engine)
// ============================================================
// Rule 7: Months that are closed/locked
let LOCKED_MONTHS = ["2023-12", "2023-11", "2023-10"];

const isDateLocked = (dateStr, userRole) => {
  if (!dateStr) return false;
  const [year, month] = dateStr.split("-");
  const key = `${year}-${month}`;
  if (LOCKED_MONTHS.includes(key)) return true;
  // Also lock entries older than current month for workers
  const entryDate = new Date(dateStr);
  const now = new Date();
  const entryMonth = entryDate.getFullYear() * 12 + entryDate.getMonth();
  const nowMonth = now.getFullYear() * 12 + now.getMonth();
  if (userRole === "worker" && entryMonth < nowMonth) return true;
  return false;
};

// ── Monthly History Navigator ──
const MonthNavigator = ({ selectedMonth, setSelectedMonth }) => {
  const MONTHS = ["Jan","Feb","Mar","Apr","May","Jun","Jul","Aug","Sep","Oct","Nov","Dec"];
  const [year, mon] = selectedMonth.split("-").map(Number);
  const label = `${MONTHS[mon-1]} ${year}`;
  const nowYM = new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7);
  const isCurrentMonth = selectedMonth === nowYM;

  const prev = () => {
    const d = new Date(year, mon-2, 1);
    setSelectedMonth(`${d.getFullYear()}-${String(d.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,"0")}`);
  };
  const next = () => {
    const d = new Date(year, mon, 1);
    const nextYM = `${d.getFullYear()}-${String(d.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,"0")}`;
    if (nextYM <= nowYM) setSelectedMonth(nextYM);
  };

  return (
    <div className="flex items-center justify-between bg-orange-50 border-2 border-orange-200 rounded-2xl px-4 py-3">
      <button onClick={prev}
        className="w-10 h-10 rounded-xl bg-white border-2 border-orange-200 flex items-center justify-center text-orange-600 font-black text-xl active:scale-95 transition shadow-sm">
        ‹
      </button>
      <div className="text-center">
        <p className="text-orange-600 font-extrabold text-base tracking-wide">📅 {label}</p>
        {isCurrentMonth
          ? <p className="text-orange-400 text-xs font-semibold mt-0.5">Current Month</p>
          : <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs mt-0.5">History / पुराना डेटा</p>
        }
      </div>
      <button onClick={next} disabled={isCurrentMonth}
        className={`w-10 h-10 rounded-xl border-2 flex items-center justify-center font-black text-xl active:scale-95 transition shadow-sm
          ${isCurrentMonth ? "bg-gray-100 border-gray-200 text-gray-300 cursor-not-allowed" : "bg-white border-orange-200 text-orange-600"}`}>
        ›
      </button>
    </div>
  );
};

const WorkEntry = () => {
  const { user, sharedCuts } = useContext(AppContext);
  const TODAY = new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0];
  const emptyForm = { date: TODAY, workerId: "", styleId: "", operationId: "", pieces: "", notes: "" };

  // ── ALL hooks must be at top, before any return ──
  const [entries, setEntries] = useState(MOCK_DB.workEntries.map(e => ({ ...e, status: "verified" })));
  const [selectedMonth, setSelectedMonth] = useState(new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7));
  const [showModal, setShowModal]       = useState(false);
  const [showBalanceModal, setShowBalanceModal] = useState(false);
  const [search, setSearch]             = useState("");
  const [filterStatus, setFilterStatus] = useState("all");
  const [editEntry, setEditEntry]       = useState(null);
  const [error, setError]               = useState("");
  const [form, setForm]                 = useState(emptyForm);
  const [savedOk, setSavedOk]           = useState(false); // success toast

  // ── Derived values (no stale-state bug) ──
  const pieceRate = MOCK_DB.operations.find(o => o.id === form.operationId)?.pieceRate || 0;
  const autoAmount = (parseInt(form.pieces) || 0) * pieceRate;

  // reset error when key fields change
  useEffect(() => { setError(""); }, [form.operationId, form.pieces, form.styleId, form.workerId]);

  // ── Admin block — AFTER all hooks ──
  if (user.role === "admin") {
    return (
      <div className="space-y-5">
        <h1 className="text-xl font-extrabold text-gray-900">Work Entry / काम एंट्री</h1>
        <div className="bg-red-50 border-2 border-red-200 rounded-2xl p-8 text-center">
          <div className="w-16 h-16 mx-auto mb-3 rounded-2xl bg-red-100 flex items-center justify-center"><svg width="32" height="32" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="9" stroke="#DC2626" strokeWidth="2"/><path d="M6 6l12 12M18 6 6 18" stroke="#DC2626" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg></div>
          <p className="text-red-700 font-bold text-lg">Admin के पास Work Entry नहीं होगी</p>
          <p className="text-red-500 text-sm mt-1">Admin cannot create work entries.</p>
          <p className="text-gray-600 text-sm mt-3">सिर्फ <strong>Supervisor</strong> ही Work Entry कर सकता है।</p>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  // ── Balance calculation helpers ──
  const getOperationBalance = (styleId, operationId, excludeEntryId = null) => {
    // Cutting records se limit lo (dynamic — CUTTING_LIMITS nahi)
    const cuttingTotal = (sharedCuts||[])
      .filter(c => c.styleId === styleId)
      .reduce((s, c) => s + (+c.totalPieces || 0), 0);
    const limit = cuttingTotal > 0 ? cuttingTotal : 999999; // agar cutting nahi toh unlimited
    const used = entries
      .filter(e =>
        e.styleId === styleId &&
        e.operationId === operationId &&
        e.status !== "rejected" &&
        e.id !== excludeEntryId
      )
      .reduce((sum, e) => sum + e.pieces, 0);
    return { limit, used, balance: limit - used };
  };

  const getWorkerDailyBalance = (workerId, styleId, operationId, date, excludeId = null) => {
    const { balance: opBalance } = getOperationBalance(styleId, operationId, excludeId);
    const alreadyToday = entries
      .filter(e =>
        e.workerId === workerId &&
        e.styleId === styleId &&
        e.operationId === operationId &&
        e.date === date &&
        e.status !== "rejected" &&
        e.id !== excludeId
      )
      .reduce((sum, e) => sum + e.pieces, 0);
    return { opBalance, alreadyToday, canEnter: Math.max(0, opBalance - alreadyToday) };
  };

  // ── Validation on form submit ──
  const validate = (f, excludeId = null) => {
    if (!f.workerId || !f.styleId || !f.operationId || !f.pieces || !f.date)
      return "सभी fields भरना जरूरी है।";

    const qty = parseInt(f.pieces);
    if (isNaN(qty) || qty <= 0) return "Pieces 0 से ज्यादा होनी चाहिए।";

    // Rule 7 – Date Lock
    if (isDateLocked(f.date, user.role)) {
      const [y, m] = f.date.split("-");
      const monthName = new Date(+y, +m - 1).toLocaleString("en-IN", { month: "long", year: "numeric" });
      if (user.role !== "supervisor" && user.role !== "admin") {
        return `Date Locked! ${monthName} की entries बंद हो चुकी हैं। सिर्फ Supervisor edit कर सकता है।`;
      }
    }

    // Rule 6 – Duplicate entry check
    const dup = entries.find(e =>
      e.workerId === f.workerId &&
      e.styleId === f.styleId &&
      e.operationId === f.operationId &&
      e.date === f.date &&
      e.status !== "rejected" &&
      e.id !== excludeId
    );
    if (dup) return `Duplicate Entry! ${dup.workerName} की इस date पर इस operation की entry पहले से है।`;

    // Rule 1 – Style cutting limit
    const { limit: cLimit, balance: opBalance } = getOperationBalance(f.styleId, f.operationId, excludeId);
    if (cLimit < 999999 && qty > opBalance) {
      const style = MOCK_DB.styles.find(s => s.id === f.styleId);
      const op = MOCK_DB.operations.find(o => o.id === f.operationId);
      return `Quantity exceeds cutting quantity!\nStyle: ${style?.styleName} → ${op?.name}\nCutting Total: ${cLimit} | Already Done: ${cLimit - opBalance} | Balance: ${opBalance}`;
    }

    // Rule 5 – Daily worker entry limit
    const { canEnter } = getWorkerDailyBalance(f.workerId, f.styleId, f.operationId, f.date, excludeId);
    if (qty > canEnter) {
      const worker = MOCK_DB.workers.find(w => w.id === f.workerId);
      return `Daily limit exceeded!\n${worker?.name} आज के लिए अधिकतम ${canEnter} pcs enter कर सकते हैं।`;
    }

    return null;
  };

  const handleSubmit = () => {
    const err = validate(form);
    if (err) { setError(err); return; }

    const worker = MOCK_DB.workers.find(w => w.id === form.workerId);
    const style  = MOCK_DB.styles.find(s => s.id === form.styleId);
    const op     = MOCK_DB.operations.find(o => o.id === form.operationId);

    const newEntry = {
      id: `e${Date.now()}`,
      date: form.date,
      workerId: form.workerId,
      styleId: form.styleId,
      operationId: form.operationId,
      workerName: worker.name,
      staffId: worker.staffId,
      styleName: style.styleName,
      operation: op.name,
      pieces: parseInt(form.pieces),
      pieceRate: pieceRate,
      amount: autoAmount,
      department: worker.department,
      status: "verified",
      enteredBy: user.name,
      notes: form.notes,
    };
    setEntries(prev => [newEntry, ...prev]);
    setShowModal(false);
    setForm(emptyForm);
    setError("");
    setSavedOk(true);
    setTimeout(() => setSavedOk(false), 3000);
  };

  const handleEdit = () => {
    const err = validate(form, editEntry.id);
    if (err) { setError(err); return; }
    const op = MOCK_DB.operations.find(o => o.id === form.operationId);
    setEntries(prev => prev.map(e => e.id === editEntry.id
      ? { ...e, pieces: parseInt(form.pieces), pieceRate, amount: autoAmount, notes: form.notes, operation: op?.name, operationId: form.operationId }
      : e
    ));
    setEditEntry(null);
    setShowModal(false);
    setForm(emptyForm);
    setError("");
    setSavedOk(true);
    setTimeout(() => setSavedOk(false), 3000);
  };

  const openEdit = (entry) => {
    setEditEntry(entry);
    setForm({ date: entry.date, workerId: entry.workerId || "", styleId: entry.styleId || "", operationId: entry.operationId || "", pieces: String(entry.pieces), notes: entry.notes || "" });
    setError("");
    setShowModal(true);
  };

  const deleteEntry = (id) => {
    if (window.confirm("क्या यह entry delete करना है?")) setEntries(prev => prev.filter(e => e.id !== id));
  };

  const todayEntries = entries.filter(e => e.date === new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0]);
  const todayPieces = todayEntries.reduce((s, e) => s + e.pieces, 0);
  const todayAmount = todayEntries.reduce((s, e) => s + e.amount, 0);
  const todayWorkers = new Set(todayEntries.map(e => e.workerId || e.workerName)).size;

  const filtered = entries
    .filter(e => e.date && e.date.startsWith(selectedMonth))
    .filter(e => filterStatus === "all" || e.status === filterStatus)
    .filter(e =>
      !search ||
      e.workerName?.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase()) ||
      e.styleName?.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase()) ||
      e.operation?.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase())
    );

  // Balance table data — cutting records se dynamic limit
  const balanceRows = MOCK_DB.styles.filter(s => s.status === "active").flatMap(style => {
    const cuttingTotal = (sharedCuts||[])
      .filter(c => c.styleId === style.id)
      .reduce((s, c) => s + (+c.totalPieces || 0), 0);
    if (!cuttingTotal) return [];
    return MOCK_DB.operations.map(op => {
      const { used, balance } = getOperationBalance(style.id, op.id);
      return { styleId: style.id, styleName: style.styleName, opName: op.name, limit: cuttingTotal, used, balance };
    });
  });

  const statusColor = { verified: "green", pending: "amber", rejected: "red" };
  const statusLabel = { verified: "Verified", pending: "Pending", rejected: "Rejected" };

  const currentBalance = (form.styleId && form.operationId && form.workerId && form.date)
    ? getWorkerDailyBalance(form.workerId, form.styleId, form.operationId, form.date, editEntry?.id)
    : null;

  return (
    <div className="space-y-5">
      {/* Success toast */}
      {savedOk && (
        <div className="fixed top-16 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 z-50 bg-green-500 text-white px-6 py-3 rounded-2xl shadow-2xl font-bold text-sm flex items-center gap-2">
          ✓ Entry Successfully Saved!
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Header */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between flex-wrap gap-3">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-extrabold text-gray-900">Work Entry / काम एंट्री</h1>
          <p className="text-gray-600 text-sm">Supervisor द्वारा daily verified entries</p>
        </div>
        <div className="flex gap-2">
          <Btn variant="secondary" size="sm" onClick={() => setShowBalanceModal(true)}>Balance</Btn>
          <Btn onClick={() => { setEditEntry(null); setForm(emptyForm); setError(""); setShowModal(true); }}>+ New Entry</Btn>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Rules info banner */}
      <div className="bg-blue-50 border border-blue-200 rounded-xl p-3">
        <p className="text-blue-800 text-xs font-semibold mb-1">Work Entry Rules Active:</p>
        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
          {["✓ Cutting limit check","✓ Duplicate block","✓ Daily limit","✓ Auto balance","✓ Auto amount"].map(r => (
            <span key={r} className="bg-blue-100 text-blue-700 text-xs px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full font-medium">{r}</span>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Month Navigator */}
      <MonthNavigator selectedMonth={selectedMonth} setSelectedMonth={setSelectedMonth} />

      {/* Month Summary Cards */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-3">
        {[
          { label: "Month Pieces", value: filtered.reduce((s,e)=>s+e.pieces,0).toLocaleString(), color: "text-orange-500" },
          { label: "Month Amount", value: `₹${filtered.reduce((s,e)=>s+(e.amount||0),0).toFixed(0)}`, color: "text-green-600" },
          { label: "Total Entries", value: filtered.length, color: "text-blue-600" },
        ].map(s => (
          <div key={s.label} className="bg-white rounded-xl p-3 border-2 border-gray-100 text-center shadow-sm">
            <p className={`text-lg font-bold ${s.color}`}>{s.value}</p>
            <p className="text-gray-600 text-xs font-semibold mt-0.5">{s.label}</p>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Department-wise Production Summary */}
      {filtered.length > 0 && (() => {
        const deptMap = {};
        filtered.forEach(e => {
          if (!deptMap[e.department]) deptMap[e.department] = { pieces: 0, amount: 0, entries: 0 };
          deptMap[e.department].pieces  += e.pieces;
          deptMap[e.department].amount  += e.amount || 0;
          deptMap[e.department].entries += 1;
        });
        const deptColors = { Stitching:"#3B82F6", Finishing:"#10B981", QC:"#F59E0B", Cutting:"#EF4444", Embroidery:"#8B5CF6" };
        return (
          <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border-2 border-gray-100 shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
            <div className="bg-gray-800 px-4 py-2.5">
              <p className="text-white text-xs font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wide">📊 Department-wise Production</p>
            </div>
            {Object.entries(deptMap).map(([dept, data], i) => (
              <div key={dept} className={"flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 border-b border-gray-50 last:border-0 " + (i%2===0?"bg-white":"bg-gray-50/40")}>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <div className="w-3 h-3 rounded-full shrink-0" style={{background: deptColors[dept]||"#64748B"}} />
                  <div>
                    <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-sm">{dept}</p>
                    <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{data.entries} entries</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div className="text-right">
                  <p className="text-orange-500 font-extrabold text-sm">{data.pieces.toLocaleString()} pcs</p>
                  <p className="text-green-600 font-bold text-xs">₹{data.amount.toFixed(0)}</p>
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        );
      })()}

      {/* Today summary */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-3">
        {[
          { label: "Today Pieces", value: todayPieces.toLocaleString(), color: "text-orange-500" },
          { label: "Today Amount", value: `₹${todayAmount.toFixed(0)}`, color: "text-green-600" },
          { label: "Workers Active", value: todayWorkers, color: "text-blue-600" },
        ].map(s => (
          <div key={s.label} className="bg-white rounded-xl p-3 border-2 border-gray-100 text-center shadow-sm">
            <p className={`text-lg font-bold ${s.color}`}>{s.value}</p>
            <p className="text-gray-600 text-xs font-semibold mt-0.5">{s.label}</p>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Filters */}
      <div className="flex gap-2 flex-wrap">
        {[["all","All"],["verified","Verified"],["pending","Pending"],["rejected","Rejected"]].map(([k,l]) => (
          <button key={k} onClick={() => setFilterStatus(k)}
            className={`px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg text-xs font-bold transition border ${filterStatus === k ? "bg-orange-500 text-white border-orange-500" : "bg-white text-gray-600 border-gray-200 hover:border-orange-300"}`}>
            {l} {k !== "all" && <span className="ml-1">({entries.filter(e => e.status === k).length})</span>}
          </button>
        ))}
        <input value={search} onChange={e => setSearch(e.target.value)} placeholder=" Search..."
          className="flex-1 min-w-[140px] bg-white border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-lg px-3 py-1.5 text-gray-900 text-xs focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-400" />
      </div>

      {/* Entries list — Date | Style | Operation | Rate | Amount */}
      <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border-2 border-gray-100 shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
        {/* Table header */}
        <div className="grid grid-cols-12 gap-1 bg-gray-800 px-3 py-2.5 text-xs font-extrabold text-white uppercase tracking-wide">
          <div className="col-span-2">Date</div>
          <div className="col-span-3">Style</div>
          <div className="col-span-3">Operation</div>
          <div className="col-span-2 text-right">Rate</div>
          <div className="col-span-2 text-right">Amount</div>
        </div>

        {filtered.length === 0 ? (
          <div className="text-center py-12 text-gray-400 text-sm">कोई entry नहीं मिली</div>
        ) : filtered.map((e, idx) => {
          const locked = isDateLocked(e.date, user.role) && user.role !== "supervisor" && user.role !== "admin";
          const rowBg = idx % 2 === 0 ? "bg-white" : "bg-gray-50/60";
          const statusDot = { verified: "bg-green-500", pending: "bg-amber-400", rejected: "bg-red-500" };
          return (
            <div key={e.id} className={`${rowBg} border-b border-gray-100 last:border-0 ${e.status === "rejected" ? "opacity-60" : ""}`}>
              <div className="grid grid-cols-12 gap-1 px-3 py-2.5 items-center">
                {/* Date */}
                <div className="col-span-2 min-w-0">
                  <p className="text-gray-800 font-bold text-[10px] leading-tight">{e.date?.slice(5)}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-[9px]">{e.date?.slice(0,4)}</p>
                </div>
                {/* Style */}
                <div className="col-span-3 min-w-0">
                  <p className="text-gray-900 font-semibold text-[10px] truncate leading-tight">{e.styleName}</p>
                  <p className="text-orange-500 text-[9px] font-bold">{e.pieces} pcs</p>
                </div>
                {/* Operation */}
                <div className="col-span-3 min-w-0">
                  <span className="text-[10px] font-semibold bg-blue-50 text-blue-700 px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-md leading-tight block truncate">{e.operation}</span>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-[9px] mt-0.5">{e.department}</p>
                </div>
                {/* Rate */}
                <div className="col-span-2 text-right">
                  <p className="text-gray-700 font-bold text-[10px]">&#8377;{(e.pieceRate||0).toFixed(2)}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-[9px]">per pc</p>
                </div>
                {/* Amount */}
                <div className="col-span-2 text-right">
                  <p className="text-green-600 font-extrabold text-xs">&#8377;{(e.amount||0).toFixed(0)}</p>
                  {e.status !== "rejected" && !locked ? (
                    <div className="flex gap-1 justify-end mt-0.5">
                      <button onClick={() => openEdit(e)} className="text-[9px] font-bold text-blue-500 active:opacity-70">Edit</button>
                      <span className="text-gray-300 text-[9px]">·</span>
                      <button onClick={() => deleteEntry(e.id)} className="text-[9px] font-bold text-red-400 active:opacity-70">Del</button>
                    </div>
                  ) : locked ? (
                    <p className="text-gray-400 text-[9px]">Locked</p>
                  ) : (
                    <p className="text-red-400 text-[9px]">Rejected</p>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>
              {/* Status strip */}
              <div className="px-3 pb-2 flex items-center gap-2">
                <div className={`w-2 h-2 rounded-full shrink-0 ${statusDot[e.status] || "bg-gray-400"}`} />
                <span className={`text-[10px] font-bold ${e.status === "verified" ? "text-green-600" : e.status === "pending" ? "text-amber-600" : "text-red-500"}`}>
                  {statusLabel[e.status] || e.status}
                </span>
                {e.notes && <>
                  <span className="text-gray-300 text-[10px]">•</span>
                  <span className="text-gray-400 text-[10px] italic truncate max-w-[120px]">"{e.notes}"</span>
                </>}
              </div>
            </div>
          );
        })}

        {/* Footer total */}
        {filtered.length > 0 && (
          <div className="bg-gray-800 px-3 py-2.5 flex items-center justify-between">
            <span className="text-white text-xs font-bold">कुल — {filtered.length} entries</span>
            <span className="text-green-400 font-extrabold text-sm">
              &#8377;{filtered.reduce((s, e) => s + (e.amount||0), 0).toFixed(0)}
            </span>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* ── NEW / EDIT ENTRY MODAL ── */}
      <Modal open={showModal} onClose={() => { setShowModal(false); setEditEntry(null); setError(""); }} title={editEntry ? "Entry Edit करें" : "New Work Entry / नई एंट्री"} size="md">
        <div className="space-y-4">

          {error && (
            <div className="bg-red-50 border-2 border-red-300 rounded-xl p-3">
              <p className="text-red-700 font-bold text-sm whitespace-pre-line">{error}</p>
            </div>
          )}

          <div>
            <Input label="Date / तारीख" type="date" value={form.date} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, date: e.target.value })} />
            {isDateLocked(form.date, user.role) && (
              <div className="mt-1.5 flex items-center gap-2 bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-lg px-3 py-2">
                <svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" className="inline"><rect x="4" y="9" width="12" height="9" rx="2" stroke="#F97316" strokeWidth="1.5"/><path d="M7 9V6a3 3 0 0 1 6 0v3" stroke="#F97316" strokeWidth="1.5" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
                <div>
                  <p className="text-red-700 font-bold text-xs">Month Locked / बंद महीना</p>
                  <p className="text-red-500 text-xs">{user.role === "supervisor" || user.role === "admin" ? "Supervisor होने के नाते आप edit कर सकते हैं।" : "सिर्फ Supervisor edit कर सकता है।"}</p>
                </div>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>

          <Select label="Worker / कर्मचारी" value={form.workerId} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, workerId: e.target.value })}>
            <option value="">— Worker चुनें —</option>
            {MOCK_DB.workers.filter(w => w.status === "active").map(w => (
              <option key={w.id} value={w.id}>{w.name} ({w.staffId}) — {w.department}</option>
            ))}
          </Select>

          <Select label="Style / स्टाइल" value={form.styleId} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, styleId: e.target.value })}>
            <option value="">— Style चुनें —</option>
            {MOCK_DB.styles.filter(s => s.status === "active").map(s => (
              <option key={s.id} value={s.id}>{s.styleName} ({s.styleNumber}) — Cutting: {s.totalQuantity}</option>
            ))}
          </Select>

          <Select label="Operation / काम" value={form.operationId} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, operationId: e.target.value })}>
            <option value="">— Operation चुनें —</option>
            {MOCK_DB.operations.map(o => (
              <option key={o.id} value={o.id}>{o.name} ({o.nameHindi}) — ₹{o.pieceRate}/pc</option>
            ))}
          </Select>

          {/* Live balance card */}
          {currentBalance && (
            <div className={`rounded-xl border-2 p-3 ${currentBalance.canEnter === 0 ? "bg-red-50 border-red-300" : currentBalance.canEnter < 50 ? "bg-amber-50 border-amber-300" : "bg-green-50 border-green-200"}`}>
              <p className="text-xs font-bold text-gray-700 mb-1.5">Live Balance (Rule Check)</p>
              <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2 text-center">
                <div>
                  <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold">{currentBalance.opBalance}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs">Op Balance</p>
                </div>
                <div>
                  <p className="text-orange-600 font-bold">{currentBalance.alreadyToday}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs">Today Done</p>
                </div>
                <div>
                  <p className={`font-bold ${currentBalance.canEnter === 0 ? "text-red-600" : "text-green-600"}`}>{currentBalance.canEnter}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs">Can Enter</p>
                </div>
              </div>
              {currentBalance.canEnter === 0 && <p className="text-red-600 text-xs font-bold mt-1.5 text-center">Entry not allowed — limit reached!</p>}
            </div>
          )}

          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            <div>
              <Input label="Pieces / पीस" type="number" min="1"
                max={currentBalance?.canEnter || ""}
                value={form.pieces}
                onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, pieces: e.target.value })}
                placeholder={currentBalance ? `Max: ${currentBalance.canEnter}` : "0"} />
            </div>
            <div>
              <label className="block text-sm font-bold text-gray-900 mb-1">Piece Rate ₹ (Auto)</label>
              <div className="w-full bg-gray-100 border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 text-gray-600 font-bold text-sm">
                ₹{pieceRate.toFixed(2)} / pc
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Auto amount */}
          <div className="bg-orange-50 border-2 border-orange-200 rounded-xl p-4">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
              <div>
                <p className="text-gray-600 text-xs font-semibold">Auto Calculated Amount</p>
                <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs">Pieces × Piece Rate = Amount</p>
                <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs">{form.pieces || 0} × ₹{pieceRate.toFixed(2)}</p>
              </div>
              <p className="text-3xl font-extrabold text-orange-600">₹{autoAmount.toFixed(2)}</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <Input label="Notes (optional)" value={form.notes} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, notes: e.target.value })} placeholder="कोई टिप्पणी..." />

          <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-lg p-2.5 text-xs text-green-700 font-semibold">
            ✓ Supervisor Entry → Status: <strong>Verified</strong> (Directly payment में जाएगी)
          </div>

          <div className="flex gap-3">
            <Btn variant="secondary" onClick={() => { setShowModal(false); setError(""); }} className="flex-1">Cancel</Btn>
            <Btn
              onClick={editEntry ? handleEdit : handleSubmit}
              disabled={!!(currentBalance && currentBalance.canEnter === 0)}
              className="flex-1"
            >
              {editEntry ? "✓ Update Entry" : "✓ Save Entry"}
            </Btn>
          </div>
        </div>
      </Modal>

      {/* ── BALANCE MODAL ── */}
      <Modal open={showBalanceModal} onClose={() => setShowBalanceModal(false)} title="Operation Balance / शेष मात्रा" size="lg">
        <div className="space-y-3">
          <p className="text-gray-600 text-sm">हर style/operation का cutting limit vs used vs balance</p>
          <Table
            headers={["Style", "Operation", "Limit", "Used", "Balance", "Status"]}
            rows={balanceRows.map((r, i) => {
              const pct = Math.round((r.used / r.limit) * 100);
              return [
                <Td key="s" className="font-bold text-gray-900 text-xs">{r.styleName}</Td>,
                <Td key="o" className="text-gray-700 text-xs">{r.opName}</Td>,
                <Td key="l"><span className="font-bold text-gray-900">{r.limit}</span></Td>,
                <Td key="u"><span className="text-orange-600 font-bold">{r.used}</span></Td>,
                <Td key="b">
                  <span className={`font-bold ${r.balance === 0 ? "text-red-600" : r.balance < 50 ? "text-amber-600" : "text-green-600"}`}>{r.balance}</span>
                </Td>,
                <Td key="st">
                  <div className="w-20">
                    <div className="w-full bg-gray-200 rounded-full h-1.5">
                      <div className={`h-1.5 rounded-full ${pct >= 100 ? "bg-red-500" : pct >= 75 ? "bg-amber-500" : "bg-green-500"}`} style={{ width: `${Math.min(pct, 100)}%` }} />
                    </div>
                    <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-0.5 text-center">{pct}%</p>
                  </div>
                </Td>,
              ];
            })}
          />
          <Btn onClick={() => setShowBalanceModal(false)} className="w-full mt-2" variant="secondary">
            ← वापस जाएं / Close
          </Btn>
        </div>
      </Modal>
    </div>
  );
};

// WORKERS
// ══════════════════════════════════════════
// SUPERVISOR PERMISSIONS — Admin only
// ══════════════════════════════════════════
const SupervisorPermissions = () => {
  const [accounts, setAccounts] = useState(MOCK_DB.supervisorAccounts.map(s=>({...s, permissions:{...s.permissions}})));
  const [saved, setSaved] = useState("");

  const PERM_LABELS = {
    canViewEntries:    { label:"Work Entries देखें",   icon:"👁" },
    canAddEntries:     { label:"Entry Add करें",        icon:"✏️" },
    canApproveEntries: { label:"Entry Approve/Reject",  icon:"✅" },
    canViewCutting:    { label:"Cutting देखें",         icon:"✂️" },
    canAddCutting:     { label:"Cutting Add करें",      icon:"➕" },
    canViewHourly:     { label:"Hourly Report देखें",   icon:"⏱" },
    canAddHourly:      { label:"Hourly Report Add करें",icon:"📊" },
    canViewPayments:   { label:"Payments देखें",        icon:"💰" },
    canViewAllDepts:   { label:"सभी Dept देखें",        icon:"🏭" },
  };

  const toggle = (svId, perm) => {
    setAccounts(prev => prev.map(sv => sv.id === svId
      ? {...sv, permissions:{...sv.permissions, [perm]:!sv.permissions[perm]}}
      : sv
    ));
  };

  const DEPT_COLOR = { Stitching:"#3B82F6", Finishing:"#10B981", QC:"#F59E0B", Cutting:"#EF4444" };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-5 pb-24">
      <div>
        <h1 className="text-xl font-extrabold text-gray-900">Supervisor Permissions</h1>
        <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm">Admin — har supervisor को access control करें</p>
      </div>

      {saved && (
        <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-2xl px-4 py-3 flex items-center gap-2">
          <div className="w-5 h-5 rounded-full bg-green-500 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
            <svg width="10" height="10" viewBox="0 0 12 12" fill="none"><path d="M2 6l3 3 5-5" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
          </div>
          <p className="text-green-700 text-sm font-semibold">{saved}</p>
        </div>
      )}

      {accounts.map(sv => {
        const dc = DEPT_COLOR[sv.department] || "#6366F1";
        return (
          <div key={sv.id} className="bg-white rounded-2xl border-2 border-gray-100 shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
            <div className="h-1.5" style={{background:dc}}/>
            <div className="p-4">
              {/* Supervisor header */}
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-4">
                <div className="w-12 h-12 rounded-2xl flex items-center justify-center text-white font-black text-lg shrink-0"
                  style={{background:dc}}>{sv.name.charAt(0)}</div>
                <div className="flex-1">
                  <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold">{sv.name}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm">{sv.staffId} · {sv.mobile}</p>
                  <span className="text-white text-xs font-extrabold px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full mt-0.5 inline-block"
                    style={{background:dc}}>{sv.department}</span>
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* Permission toggles */}
              <div className="space-y-2">
                {Object.entries(PERM_LABELS).map(([key, meta]) => (
                  <div key={key} className="flex items-center justify-between py-2 border-b border-gray-50 last:border-0">
                    <p className="text-gray-700 text-sm font-medium">{meta.icon} {meta.label}</p>
                    <button onClick={()=>toggle(sv.id, key)}
                      className={"w-12 h-6 rounded-full transition-all relative "+(sv.permissions[key]?"":"bg-gray-200")}
                      style={sv.permissions[key]?{background:dc}:{}}>
                      <div className={"absolute top-0.5 w-5 h-5 bg-white rounded-full shadow transition-all "+(sv.permissions[key]?"left-6":"left-0.5")}/>
                    </button>
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>

              {/* Save button */}
              <button onClick={()=>{ setSaved(sv.name+" की permissions save हो गईं! ✅"); setTimeout(()=>setSaved(""),2500); }}
                className="mt-3 w-full text-white font-extrabold py-3 rounded-2xl active:scale-[0.98] transition"
                style={{background:dc}}>
                Save Changes
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        );
      })}
    </div>
  );
};


const Workers = () => {
  const [workers, setWorkers] = useState(MOCK_DB.workers);
  const [showModal, setShowModal] = useState(false);
  const [editWorker, setEditWorker] = useState(null);
  const [filter, setFilter] = useState("all");
  const [form, setForm] = useState({ name: "", mobile: "", staffId: "", departmentId: "", joinDate: "", status: "active" });

  const filtered = workers.filter(w => filter === "all" || w.status === filter);
  const { paged, page, setPage, totalPages, total, pageSize } = usePagination(filtered, 20);

  const openAdd = () => {
    setEditWorker(null);
    setForm({ name:"", mobile:"", staffId:"", departmentId:"", joinDate:"", status:"active" });
    setShowModal(true);
  };
  const openEdit = (w) => {
    setEditWorker(w);
    setForm({ name:w.name, mobile:w.mobile, staffId:w.staffId, departmentId:w.departmentId||"", joinDate:w.joinDate, status:w.status });
    setShowModal(true);
  };
  const handleSave = () => {
    const dept = MOCK_DB.departments.find(d => d.id === form.departmentId);
    if (editWorker) {
      setWorkers(prev => prev.map(w => w.id === editWorker.id ? { ...w, ...form, department: dept?.name || w.department } : w));
    } else {
      setWorkers(prev => [...prev, { ...form, id:`w${Date.now()}`, department: dept?.name || "" }]);
    }
    setShowModal(false); setEditWorker(null);
    setForm({ name:"", mobile:"", staffId:"", departmentId:"", joinDate:"", status:"active" });
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-5">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between flex-wrap gap-3">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-extrabold text-gray-900">Workers / कर्मचारी</h1>
          <p className="text-gray-900 text-sm">{workers.length} total workers</p>
        </div>
        <Btn onClick={openAdd}>+ Add Worker</Btn>
      </div>

      <div className="flex gap-2">
        {["all", "active", "inactive", "on_leave"].map(f => (
          <button key={f} onClick={() => setFilter(f)}
            className={`px-4 py-2 rounded-xl text-sm font-medium transition ${filter === f ? "bg-orange-500 text-white" : "bg-gray-100 text-gray-900 hover:text-gray-900"}`}>
            {f === "all" ? "All" : f === "on_leave" ? "On Leave" : f.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + f.slice(1)}
          </button>
        ))}
      </div>

      <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 overflow-hidden">
        {/* Table header */}
        <div className="bg-gray-800 grid grid-cols-12 px-4 py-2.5 text-xs font-extrabold text-white uppercase tracking-wide">
          <div className="col-span-4">Name</div>
          <div className="col-span-2">Staff ID</div>
          <div className="col-span-3">Department</div>
          <div className="col-span-2 text-center">Status</div>
          <div className="col-span-1 text-right">Edit</div>
        </div>

        {filtered.length === 0 && (
          <p className="text-center py-10 text-gray-400 text-sm">कोई worker नहीं मिला</p>
        )}

        {paged.map((w, i) => (
          <div key={w.id} className={"grid grid-cols-12 px-4 py-3 items-center border-b border-gray-50 last:border-0 " + (i % 2 === 0 ? "bg-white" : "bg-gray-50/40")}>
            {/* Name */}
            <div className="col-span-4 flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0">
              <div className="w-7 h-7 rounded-lg bg-orange-100 flex items-center justify-center font-extrabold text-orange-600 text-xs shrink-0">
                {w.name.charAt(0)}
              </div>
              <div className="min-w-0">
                <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-xs truncate">{w.name}</p>
                <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{w.mobile}</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            {/* Staff ID */}
            <div className="col-span-2">
              <span className="text-gray-600 text-xs font-semibold">{w.staffId}</span>
            </div>
            {/* Department */}
            <div className="col-span-3">
              <span className="text-xs bg-blue-50 text-blue-700 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-lg font-semibold">{w.department}</span>
            </div>
            {/* Status */}
            <div className="col-span-2 text-center">
              <Badge color={w.status === "active" ? "green" : w.status === "on_leave" ? "amber" : "slate"} size="xs">
                {w.status === "on_leave" ? "Leave" : w.status}
              </Badge>
            </div>
            {/* Edit */}
            <div className="col-span-1 text-right">
              <button onClick={() => openEdit(w)} className="text-orange-500 text-xs font-bold hover:underline">Edit</button>
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}

        {/* Footer */}
        {filtered.length > 0 && (
          <div className="bg-gray-800 px-4 py-2.5 text-xs font-extrabold text-gray-300">
            TOTAL: {filtered.length} workers
          </div>
        )}
        <Paginator page={page} setPage={setPage} totalPages={totalPages} total={total} pageSize={pageSize} />
      </div>

      <Modal open={showModal} onClose={() => { setShowModal(false); setEditWorker(null); }} title={editWorker ? "Edit Worker" : "Add Worker / कर्मचारी जोड़ें"}>
        <div className="space-y-4">
          <Input label="Full Name" labelHindi="पूरा नाम" value={form.name} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, name: e.target.value })} placeholder="Worker's full name" />
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            <Input label="Mobile" labelHindi="मोबाइल" type="tel" value={form.mobile} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, mobile: e.target.value })} />
            <Input label="Staff ID" labelHindi="स्टाफ ID" value={form.staffId} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, staffId: e.target.value })} placeholder="SG001" />
          </div>
          <Select label="Department" labelHindi="विभाग" value={form.departmentId} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, departmentId: e.target.value })}>
            <option value="">Select Department</option>
            {MOCK_DB.departments.map(d => <option key={d.id} value={d.id}>{d.name} ({d.nameHindi})</option>)}
          </Select>
          <Input label="Join Date" labelHindi="जॉइनिंग तारीख" type="date" value={form.joinDate} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, joinDate: e.target.value })} />
          <Select label="Status" value={form.status} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, status: e.target.value })}>
            <option value="active">Active</option>
            <option value="inactive">Inactive</option>
            <option value="on_leave">On Leave</option>
          </Select>
          <div className="flex gap-3">
            <Btn variant="secondary" onClick={() => { setShowModal(false); setEditWorker(null); }} className="flex-1">Cancel</Btn>
            <Btn onClick={handleSave} className="flex-1">{editWorker ? "Update Worker" : "Add Worker"}</Btn>
          </div>
        </div>
      </Modal>
    </div>
  );
};

const INIT_STYLE_FILES = [
  {
    id: "sf1", styleCode: "SG-2024-001", styleName: "Men's Formal Shirt", buyerName: "Reliance Retail",
    fabricType: "Cotton", color: "White", sizeRange: "S-XXL", orderQuantity: 5000,
    issueDate: "2024-01-01", deliveryDate: "2024-02-28", status: "Active",

      { id: "p2", name: "Stitching", pieceRate: 15 },
      { id: "p3", name: "Finishing", pieceRate: 3  },
      { id: "p4", name: "Packing",   pieceRate: 2  },
    ],

  {
    id: "sf2", styleCode: "SG-2024-002", styleName: "Women's Kurta", buyerName: "Myntra",
    fabricType: "Silk", color: "Blue", sizeRange: "XS-XL", orderQuantity: 3000,

    fabricType: "Polyester", color: "Red", sizeRange: "2-14 yrs", orderQuantity: 8000,
    issueDate: "2024-01-20", deliveryDate: "2024-03-15", status: "Active",
    processes: [
      { id: "p8",  name: "Cutting",   pieceRate: 1.5 },

const STATUS_COLORS = { Draft: "slate", Active: "blue", Completed: "green", Closed: "red" };
const PROCESS_OPTIONS = ["Cutting", "Stitching", "Overlock", "Finishing", "Packing", "QC", "Embroidery", "Ironing"];

const StyleFiles = () => {
  const { sharedStyles, sharedActions } = useContext(AppContext);
  const files = sharedStyles || INIT_STYLE_FILES;
  const setFiles = (updater) => {
    // local setFiles calls — we handle via sharedActions instead
  };
  const [view, setView]             = useState("list");       // list | detail | new
  const [selected, setSelected]     = useState(null);
  const [detailTab, setDetailTab]   = useState("info");       // info | processes | entries | payment
  const [search, setSearch]         = useState("");
  const [filterStatus, setFilterStatus] = useState("all");
  const [showStyleModal, setShowStyleModal] = useState(false);
  const [showProcessModal, setShowProcessModal] = useState(false);
  const [showEntryModal, setShowEntryModal]   = useState(false);
  const [assignTarget, setAssignTarget]       = useState(null); // style being assigned
  const [assignSelected, setAssignSelected]   = useState([]); // selected supervisor IDs
  const [error, setError]           = useState("");
  const [toast, setToast]           = useState("");

  // Style entries per style
  const [allEntries, setAllEntries] = useState([
    { id: "we1", styleId: "sf1", workerName: "Sunita Devi",  staffId: "SG001", process: "Stitching", quantity: 120, date: "2024-01-15", status: "approved", amount: 1800 },
    { id: "we2", styleId: "sf1", workerName: "Ramesh Kumar", staffId: "SG002", process: "Cutting",   quantity: 200, date: "2024-01-15", status: "pending",  amount: 400  },
    { id: "we3", styleId: "sf2", workerName: "Priya Singh",  staffId: "SG003", process: "Finishing", quantity: 80,  date: "2024-01-14", status: "approved", amount: 320  },
    { id: "we4", styleId: "sf3", workerName: "Geeta Rani",   staffId: "SG005", process: "Stitching", quantity: 95,  date: "2024-01-15", status: "pending",  amount: 950  },
  ]);

  const emptyStyleForm = { styleCode: "", styleName: "", buyerName: "", fabricType: "", color: "", sizeRange: "", orderQuantity: "", issueDate: "", deliveryDate: "", status: "Draft" };
  const [styleForm, setStyleForm]   = useState(emptyStyleForm);

  const emptyProcess = { name: "Stitching", pieceRate: "" };
  const [processForm, setProcessForm] = useState(emptyProcess);

  const emptyEntry = { workerName: "", staffId: "", process: "", quantity: "", date: new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0] };
  const [entryForm, setEntryForm]   = useState(emptyEntry);

  const flash = (msg) => { setToast(msg); setTimeout(() => setToast(""), 2500); };

  // ── Style CRUD ──
  const addStyle = () => {
    if (!styleForm.styleCode || !styleForm.styleName || !styleForm.buyerName || !styleForm.orderQuantity || !styleForm.deliveryDate) {
      setError("सभी fields भरना जरूरी है।"); return;
    }
    if (+styleForm.orderQuantity <= 0) { setError("Order quantity 0 से ज्यादा होनी चाहिए।"); return; }
    if (files.find(f => f.styleCode === styleForm.styleCode)) { setError("Style Code already exists!"); return; }
    const newFile = { ...styleForm, id: "sf" + Date.now(), orderQuantity: +styleForm.orderQuantity, processes: [], visibleToSupervisors: [] };
    sharedActions?.addStyle(newFile);
    setShowStyleModal(false);
    setStyleForm(emptyStyleForm);
    setError("");
    flash("Style File created!");
  };

  const updateStatus = (id, status) => {
    sharedActions?.updateStyleStatus(id, status);
    if (selected?.id === id) setSelected(prev => ({ ...prev, status }));
  };

  // ── Process CRUD ──
  const addProcess = () => {
    if (!processForm.name || !processForm.pieceRate || +processForm.pieceRate <= 0) {
      setError("Process name और piece rate भरें।"); return;
    }
    const updated = files.map(f => f.id === selected.id
      ? { ...f, processes: [...f.processes, { id: "p" + Date.now(), name: processForm.name, pieceRate: +processForm.pieceRate }] }
      : f
    );
    setFiles(updated);
    setSelected(updated.find(f => f.id === selected.id));
    setShowProcessModal(false);
    setProcessForm(emptyProcess);
    setError("");
    flash("Process added!");
  };

  const deleteProcess = (pid) => {
    const updated = files.map(f => f.id === selected.id
      ? { ...f, processes: f.processes.filter(p => p.id !== pid) }
      : f
    );
    setFiles(updated);
    setSelected(updated.find(f => f.id === selected.id));
  };

  // ── Work Entry ──
  const addEntry = () => {
    if (!entryForm.workerName || !entryForm.process || !entryForm.quantity || !entryForm.date) {
      setError("सभी fields भरना जरूरी है।"); return;
    }
    if (selected.status === "Closed") { setError("Closed style में entry नहीं हो सकती।"); return; }
    const qty = +entryForm.quantity;
    if (qty <= 0) { setError("Quantity 0 से ज्यादा होनी चाहिए।"); return; }

    // Duplicate check
    const dup = allEntries.find(e =>
      e.styleId === selected.id &&
      e.workerName === entryForm.workerName &&
      e.process === entryForm.process &&
      e.date === entryForm.date &&
      e.status !== "rejected"
    );
    if (dup) { setError("Duplicate entry! Same worker, same process, same date."); return; }

    // Quantity check
    const totalDone = allEntries.filter(e => e.styleId === selected.id && e.status === "approved").reduce((s, e) => s + e.quantity, 0);
    if (totalDone + qty > selected.orderQuantity) {
      setError("Order quantity exceed हो जाएगी! Remaining: " + (selected.orderQuantity - totalDone)); return;
    }

    const proc = selected.processes.find(p => p.name === entryForm.process);
    const amount = qty * (proc?.pieceRate || 0);
    const newEntry = {
      id: "we" + Date.now(), styleId: selected.id,
      workerName: entryForm.workerName, staffId: entryForm.staffId,
      process: entryForm.process, quantity: qty,
      date: entryForm.date, status: "pending", amount,
    };
    setAllEntries([newEntry, ...allEntries]);
    setShowEntryModal(false);
    setEntryForm(emptyEntry);
    setError("");
    flash("Entry submitted!");
  };

  const approveEntry = (id) => { setAllEntries(allEntries.map(e => e.id === id ? { ...e, status: "approved" } : e)); flash("Approved!"); };
  const rejectEntry  = (id) => { setAllEntries(allEntries.map(e => e.id === id ? { ...e, status: "rejected" } : e)); flash("Rejected."); };

  // ── Derived ──
  const filtered = files
    .filter(f => filterStatus === "all" || f.status === filterStatus)
    .filter(f => !search || f.styleName.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase()) || f.styleCode.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase()) || f.buyerName.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase()));

  const { paged: pagedStyles, page: sfPage, setPage: setSfPage, totalPages: sfTotalPages, total: sfTotal, pageSize: sfPageSize } = usePagination(filtered, 15);

  const styleEntries = selected ? allEntries.filter(e => e.styleId === selected.id) : [];
  const approvedEntries = styleEntries.filter(e => e.status === "approved");
  const totalProduced = approvedEntries.reduce((s, e) => s + e.quantity, 0);

  // Payment summary per worker
  const paymentByWorker = approvedEntries.reduce((acc, e) => {
    if (!acc[e.workerName]) acc[e.workerName] = { workerName: e.workerName, staffId: e.staffId, pieces: 0, amount: 0 };
    acc[e.workerName].pieces += e.quantity;
    acc[e.workerName].amount += e.amount;
    return acc;
  }, {});

  // ── DETAIL VIEW ──
  if (view === "detail" && selected) {
    const progress = selected.orderQuantity > 0 ? Math.min(100, Math.round((totalProduced / selected.orderQuantity) * 100)) : 0;
    return (
      <div className="space-y-4">
        {toast && <div className="fixed top-16 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 z-50 bg-green-500 text-white px-5 py-2.5 rounded-2xl shadow-xl font-bold text-sm">{toast}</div>}

        {/* Back + title */}
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          <button onClick={() => { setView("list"); setSelected(null); }} className="px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl bg-orange-50 border border-orange-200 text-orange-600 text-sm font-bold">← Back</button>
          <div>
            <h1 className="text-lg font-extrabold text-gray-900">{selected.styleName}</h1>
            <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{selected.styleCode} • {selected.buyerName}</p>
          </div>
          <div className="ml-auto">
            <Badge color={STATUS_COLORS[selected.status] || "blue"} size="xs">{selected.status}</Badge>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Progress bar */}
        <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 px-4 py-3">
          <div className="flex justify-between text-xs text-gray-500 mb-1.5">
            <span>{totalProduced.toLocaleString()} produced</span>
            <span className="font-bold text-orange-500">{progress}%</span>
            <span>{selected.orderQuantity.toLocaleString()} ordered</span>
          </div>
          <div className="w-full bg-gray-100 rounded-full h-2.5">
            <div className="h-2.5 rounded-full transition-all" style={{ width: progress + "%", background: progress === 100 ? "#10B981" : "#F97316" }} />
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Tabs */}
        <div className="flex gap-2 overflow-x-auto pb-1">
          {[["info","Info"],["processes","Processes"],["entries","Entries"],["payment","Payment"]].map(([k, l]) => (
            <button key={k} onClick={() => setDetailTab(k)}
              className={"px-4 py-2 rounded-xl text-sm font-bold whitespace-nowrap border transition " +
                (detailTab === k ? "bg-orange-500 text-white border-orange-500" : "bg-white text-gray-600 border-gray-200")}>
              {l}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* TAB: INFO */}
        {detailTab === "info" && (
          <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 overflow-hidden">
            {[
              ["Style Code",      selected.styleCode],
              ["Style Name",      selected.styleName],
              ["Buyer",           selected.buyerName],
              ["Fabric Type",     selected.fabricType],
              ["Color",           selected.color],
              ["Size Range",      selected.sizeRange],
              ["Order Quantity",  selected.orderQuantity.toLocaleString() + " pcs"],
              ["Delivery Date",   selected.deliveryDate],
              ["Status",          selected.status],
            ].map(([label, val]) => (
              <div key={label} className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 border-b border-gray-50 last:border-0">
                <span className="text-gray-400 text-sm">{label}</span>
                <span className="text-gray-900 text-sm font-semibold">{val}</span>
              </div>
            ))}
            {/* Status change */}
            <div className="px-4 py-3 bg-gray-50 flex flex-wrap gap-2">
              {["Draft","Active","Completed","Closed"].map(s => (
                <button key={s} onClick={() => updateStatus(selected.id, s)}
                  className={"px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg text-xs font-bold border transition " +
                    (selected.status === s ? "bg-gray-800 text-white border-gray-800" : "bg-white text-gray-600 border-gray-200 hover:border-orange-400")}>
                  {s}
                </button>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* TAB: PROCESSES */}
        {detailTab === "processes" && (
          <div className="space-y-3">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
              <p className="text-gray-700 text-sm font-bold">{selected.processes.length} processes configured</p>
              <Btn size="sm" onClick={() => { setShowProcessModal(true); setError(""); }}>+ Add Process</Btn>
            </div>
            {selected.processes.length === 0 && (
              <div className="bg-gray-50 rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 p-8 text-center text-gray-400">
                <div className="w-12 h-12 mx-auto mb-2 rounded-xl bg-orange-100 flex items-center justify-center"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M12 15a3 3 0 1 0 0-6 3 3 0 0 0 0 6z" stroke="#F97316" strokeWidth="1.5"/><path d="M19.4 15a1.65 1.65 0 0 0 .33 1.82l.06.06a2 2 0 0 1-2.83 2.83l-.06-.06a1.65 1.65 0 0 0-1.82-.33 1.65 1.65 0 0 0-1 1.51V21a2 2 0 0 1-4 0v-.09A1.65 1.65 0 0 0 9 19.4a1.65 1.65 0 0 0-1.82.33l-.06.06a2 2 0 0 1-2.83-2.83l.06-.06A1.65 1.65 0 0 0 4.68 15a1.65 1.65 0 0 0-1.51-1H3a2 2 0 0 1 0-4h.09A1.65 1.65 0 0 0 4.6 9a1.65 1.65 0 0 0-.33-1.82l-.06-.06a2 2 0 0 1 2.83-2.83l.06.06A1.65 1.65 0 0 0 9 4.68a1.65 1.65 0 0 0 1-1.51V3a2 2 0 0 1 4 0v.09a1.65 1.65 0 0 0 1 1.51 1.65 1.65 0 0 0 1.82-.33l.06-.06a2 2 0 0 1 2.83 2.83l-.06.06A1.65 1.65 0 0 0 19.4 9a1.65 1.65 0 0 0 1.51 1H21a2 2 0 0 1 0 4h-.09a1.65 1.65 0 0 0-1.51 1z" stroke="#F97316" strokeWidth="1.5"/></svg></div>
                <p className="text-sm font-semibold">No processes yet</p>
              </div>
            )}
            <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 overflow-hidden">
              {selected.processes.length > 0 && (
                <div className="bg-gray-800 grid grid-cols-3 px-4 py-2.5 text-xs font-extrabold text-white uppercase tracking-wide">
                  <div>Process</div>
                  <div className="text-center">Piece Rate</div>
                  <div className="text-right">Action</div>
                </div>
              )}
              {selected.processes.map((p, i) => (
                <div key={p.id} className={"grid grid-cols-3 px-4 py-3.5 items-center border-b border-gray-50 last:border-0 " + (i % 2 === 0 ? "bg-white" : "bg-gray-50/40")}>
                  <span className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-sm">{p.name}</span>
                  <span className="text-center text-green-600 font-extrabold text-sm">Rs {p.pieceRate}/pc</span>
                  <div className="text-right">
                    <button onClick={() => deleteProcess(p.id)} className="text-red-400 hover:text-red-600 text-xs font-bold">Remove</button>
                  </div>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>

            <Modal open={showProcessModal} onClose={() => { setShowProcessModal(false); setError(""); }} title="Add Process">
              <div className="space-y-4">
                {error && <div className="bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-xl p-3 text-red-700 text-sm font-semibold">{error}</div>}
                <Select label="Process Name" value={processForm.name} onChange={e => setProcessForm({ ...processForm, name: e.target.value })}>
                  {PROCESS_OPTIONS.map(p => <option key={p}>{p}</option>)}
                </Select>
                <Input label="Piece Rate (Rs)" type="number" step="0.5" value={processForm.pieceRate} onChange={e => setProcessForm({ ...processForm, pieceRate: e.target.value })} placeholder="15" />
                <div className="flex gap-3">
                  <Btn variant="secondary" onClick={() => setShowProcessModal(false)} className="flex-1">Cancel</Btn>
                  <Btn onClick={addProcess} className="flex-1">Add Process</Btn>
                </div>
              </div>
            </Modal>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* TAB: ENTRIES */}
        {detailTab === "entries" && (
          <div className="space-y-3">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
              <p className="text-gray-700 text-sm font-bold">{styleEntries.length} entries</p>
              {selected.status !== "Closed" && (
                <Btn size="sm" onClick={() => { setShowEntryModal(true); setError(""); }}>+ Add Entry</Btn>
              )}
            </div>
            {selected.status === "Closed" && (
              <div className="bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-xl p-3 text-red-700 text-sm font-semibold text-center">
                Closed style — no new entries allowed
              </div>
            )}

            {/* Entry list */}
            <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 overflow-hidden">
              {styleEntries.length > 0 && (
                <div className="bg-gray-800 grid grid-cols-12 gap-1 px-4 py-2.5 text-xs font-extrabold text-white uppercase tracking-wide">
                  <div className="col-span-3">Worker</div>
                  <div className="col-span-2">Process</div>
                  <div className="col-span-1 text-center">Qty</div>
                  <div className="col-span-2 text-center">Amount</div>
                  <div className="col-span-2 text-center">Status</div>
                  <div className="col-span-2 text-center">Action</div>
                </div>
              )}
              {styleEntries.length === 0 && <p className="text-center py-8 text-gray-400 text-sm">कोई entry नहीं</p>}
              {styleEntries.map((e, i) => (
                <div key={e.id} className={"grid grid-cols-12 gap-1 px-4 py-3 items-center border-b border-gray-50 last:border-0 " + (i % 2 === 0 ? "bg-white" : "bg-gray-50/40")}>
                  <div className="col-span-3 min-w-0">
                    <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-xs truncate">{e.workerName.split(" ")[0]}</p>
                    <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{e.date}</p>
                  </div>
                  <div className="col-span-2">
                    <span className="text-xs bg-blue-50 text-blue-700 px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded font-semibold">{e.process}</span>
                  </div>
                  <div className="col-span-1 text-center">
                    <span className="text-orange-500 font-extrabold text-sm">{e.quantity}</span>
                  </div>
                  <div className="col-span-2 text-center">
                    <span className="text-green-600 font-bold text-xs">Rs {e.amount}</span>
                  </div>
                  <div className="col-span-2 text-center">
                    <Badge color={e.status === "approved" ? "green" : e.status === "rejected" ? "red" : "amber"} size="xs">
                      {e.status}
                    </Badge>
                  </div>
                  <div className="col-span-2 flex gap-1 justify-center">
                    {e.status === "pending" && (
                      <>
                        <button onClick={() => approveEntry(e.id)} className="text-green-600 text-xs font-bold hover:underline">✓</button>
                        <button onClick={() => rejectEntry(e.id)}  className="text-red-500 text-xs font-bold hover:underline">✗</button>
                      </>
                    )}
                  </div>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>

            <Modal open={showEntryModal} onClose={() => { setShowEntryModal(false); setError(""); }} title="New Work Entry">
              <div className="space-y-4">
                {error && <div className="bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-xl p-3 text-red-700 text-sm font-semibold whitespace-pre-line">{error}</div>}
                <Select label="Worker" value={entryForm.workerName} onChange={e => {
                  const w = MOCK_DB.workers.find(w => w.name === e.target.value);
                  setEntryForm({ ...entryForm, workerName: e.target.value, staffId: w?.staffId || "" });
                }}>
                  <option value="">Select Worker</option>
                  {MOCK_DB.workers.filter(w => w.status === "active").map(w => <option key={w.id} value={w.name}>{w.name} ({w.staffId})</option>)}
                </Select>
