                <Select label="Process" value={entryForm.process} onChange={e => setEntryForm({ ...entryForm, process: e.target.value })}>
                  <option value="">Select Process</option>
                  {selected.processes.map(p => <option key={p.id} value={p.name}>{p.name} — Rs {p.pieceRate}/pc</option>)}
                </Select>
                <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
                  <Input label="Quantity" type="number" value={entryForm.quantity} onChange={e => setEntryForm({ ...entryForm, quantity: e.target.value })} placeholder="100" />
                  <Input label="Date" type="date" value={entryForm.date} onChange={e => setEntryForm({ ...entryForm, date: e.target.value })} />
                </div>
                {entryForm.process && entryForm.quantity && (
                  <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 text-sm">
                    <span className="text-gray-600">Auto Amount: </span>
                    <span className="text-green-700 font-extrabold text-base">
                      Rs {(+entryForm.quantity * (selected.processes.find(p => p.name === entryForm.process)?.pieceRate || 0)).toLocaleString()}
                    </span>
                    <span className="text-gray-400 text-xs ml-1">
                      ({entryForm.quantity} × Rs {selected.processes.find(p => p.name === entryForm.process)?.pieceRate || 0})
                    </span>
                  </div>
                )}
                <div className="flex gap-3">
                  <Btn variant="secondary" onClick={() => setShowEntryModal(false)} className="flex-1">Cancel</Btn>
                  <Btn onClick={addEntry} className="flex-1">Submit Entry</Btn>
                </div>
              </div>
            </Modal>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* TAB: PAYMENT */}
        {detailTab === "payment" && (
          <div className="space-y-3">
            <div className="bg-orange-50 border border-orange-200 rounded-2xl px-4 py-3 flex justify-between items-center">
              <span className="text-gray-700 text-sm font-bold">Total Payout (Approved)</span>
              <span className="text-orange-600 font-extrabold text-lg">
                Rs {approvedEntries.reduce((s, e) => s + e.amount, 0).toLocaleString()}
              </span>
            </div>

            <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 overflow-hidden">
              <div className="bg-gray-800 grid grid-cols-4 px-4 py-2.5 text-xs font-extrabold text-white uppercase tracking-wide">
                <div className="col-span-2">Worker</div>
                <div className="text-center">Pieces</div>
                <div className="text-right">Amount</div>
              </div>
              {Object.values(paymentByWorker).length === 0 && (
                <p className="text-center py-8 text-gray-400 text-sm">No approved entries yet</p>
              )}
              {Object.values(paymentByWorker).map((w, i) => (
                <div key={w.workerName} className={"grid grid-cols-4 px-4 py-3.5 items-center border-b border-gray-50 last:border-0 " + (i % 2 === 0 ? "bg-white" : "bg-gray-50/40")}>
                  <div className="col-span-2 flex items-center gap-2">
                    <div className="w-7 h-7 rounded-lg bg-orange-100 flex items-center justify-center text-orange-600 font-extrabold text-xs shrink-0">
                      {w.workerName.charAt(0)}
                    </div>
                    <div>
                      <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-xs">{w.workerName}</p>
                      <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{w.staffId}</p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-center">
                    <span className="text-orange-500 font-extrabold text-sm">{w.pieces} pcs</span>
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-right">
                    <span className="text-green-600 font-extrabold text-sm">Rs {w.amount.toLocaleString()}</span>
                  </div>
                </div>
              ))}
              {Object.values(paymentByWorker).length > 0 && (
                <div className="bg-gray-800 grid grid-cols-4 px-4 py-2.5 text-xs font-extrabold">
                  <div className="col-span-2 text-gray-300">TOTAL</div>
                  <div className="text-center text-orange-400">{approvedEntries.reduce((s, e) => s + e.quantity, 0)} pcs</div>
                  <div className="text-right text-green-400">Rs {approvedEntries.reduce((s, e) => s + e.amount, 0).toLocaleString()}</div>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>

            {/* Formula info */}
            <div className="bg-blue-50 border border-blue-200 rounded-xl p-3 text-xs text-blue-700">
              <p className="font-bold mb-1">Auto Payment Formula:</p>
              <p>Payment = Quantity × Piece Rate</p>
              <p className="mt-1 text-blue-500">Example: 100 pcs × Rs 15 = Rs 1,500</p>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    );
  }

  // ── LIST VIEW ──
  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      {toast && <div className="fixed top-16 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 z-50 bg-green-500 text-white px-5 py-2.5 rounded-2xl shadow-xl font-bold text-sm">{toast}</div>}

      {/* Header */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between flex-wrap gap-3">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-extrabold text-gray-900">Style Files</h1>
          <p className="text-gray-500 text-sm">{files.length} styles — {files.filter(f => f.status === "Active").length} active</p>
        </div>
        <Btn onClick={() => { setShowStyleModal(true); setError(""); }}>+ New Style</Btn>
      </div>

      {/* Search + filter */}
      <div className="flex gap-2 flex-wrap">
        <input value={search} onChange={e => setSearch(e.target.value)} placeholder="Search style, buyer..."
          className="flex-1 min-w-[160px] bg-white border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 text-gray-900 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-400" />
        <div className="flex gap-1.5 flex-wrap">
          {["all","Draft","Active","Completed","Closed"].map(s => (
            <button key={s} onClick={() => setFilterStatus(s)}
              className={"px-3 py-2 rounded-xl text-xs font-bold border transition " +
                (filterStatus === s ? "bg-orange-500 text-white border-orange-500" : "bg-white text-gray-600 border-gray-200")}>
              {s === "all" ? "All" : s}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Style cards */}
      <div className="space-y-3">
        {filtered.length === 0 && <p className="text-center py-10 text-gray-400 bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-200">कोई style नहीं मिली</p>}
        {pagedStyles.map(f => {
          const entries = allEntries.filter(e => e.styleId === f.id && e.status === "approved");
          const produced = entries.reduce((s, e) => s + e.quantity, 0);
          const progress = f.orderQuantity > 0 ? Math.min(100, Math.round((produced / f.orderQuantity) * 100)) : 0;
          const daysLeft = Math.ceil((new Date(f.deliveryDate) - new Date()) / 86400000);
          return (
            <div key={f.id} className="bg-white rounded-2xl border-2 border-gray-100 hover:border-orange-300 transition cursor-pointer overflow-hidden"
              onClick={() => { setSelected(f); setView("detail"); setDetailTab("info"); }}>
              {/* Top colored bar based on target status */}
              <div className={"h-1.5 " + (daysLeft < 0 ? "bg-red-500" : daysLeft < 7 ? "bg-amber-400" : "bg-green-500")}/>
              <div className="px-4 py-3 flex items-start justify-between gap-2">
                <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-wrap">
                    <span className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-sm">{f.styleName}</span>
                    <span className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{f.styleCode}</span>
                  </div>
                  <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs mt-0.5">{f.buyerName} • {f.fabricType} • {f.color}</p>
                </div>
                <Badge color={STATUS_COLORS[f.status] || "blue"} size="xs">{f.status}</Badge>
              </div>
              {/* Issue + Target dates */}
              <div className="px-4 pb-2 flex items-center gap-3">
                {f.issueDate && (
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 bg-blue-50 border border-blue-100 rounded-xl px-3 py-1.5">
                    <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><rect x="3" y="4" width="18" height="18" rx="2" stroke="#3B82F6" strokeWidth="1.8"/><path d="M16 2v4M8 2v4M3 10h18" stroke="#3B82F6" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
                    <div>
                      <p className="text-blue-400 text-[10px] font-bold leading-none">Issue Date</p>
                      <p className="text-blue-700 text-xs font-extrabold">{f.issueDate}</p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
                <div className={"flex items-center gap-1.5 rounded-xl px-3 py-1.5 border " + (daysLeft < 0 ? "bg-red-50 border-red-200" : daysLeft < 7 ? "bg-amber-50 border-amber-200" : "bg-green-50 border-green-200")}>
                  <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="9" stroke={daysLeft < 0 ? "#EF4444" : daysLeft < 7 ? "#F59E0B" : "#10B981"} strokeWidth="1.8"/><path d="M12 7v5l3 3" stroke={daysLeft < 0 ? "#EF4444" : daysLeft < 7 ? "#F59E0B" : "#10B981"} strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
                  <div>
                    <p className={"text-[10px] font-bold leading-none " + (daysLeft < 0 ? "text-red-400" : daysLeft < 7 ? "text-amber-500" : "text-green-500")}>Target Date</p>
                    <p className={"text-xs font-extrabold " + (daysLeft < 0 ? "text-red-600" : daysLeft < 7 ? "text-amber-600" : "text-green-700")}>{f.deliveryDate}</p>
                  </div>
                  {daysLeft < 0 ? (
                    <span className="ml-1 text-red-500 text-[10px] font-black">🔴 Overdue</span>
                  ) : daysLeft < 7 ? (
                    <span className="ml-1 text-amber-500 text-[10px] font-black">⚠️ {daysLeft}d left</span>
                  ) : (
                    <span className="ml-1 text-green-500 text-[10px] font-black">✅ {daysLeft}d left</span>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>
              {/* Progress */}
              <div className="px-4 pb-2">
                <div className="flex justify-between text-xs text-gray-400 mb-1">
                  <span>{produced.toLocaleString()} / {f.orderQuantity.toLocaleString()} pcs</span>
                  <span className="font-bold text-orange-500">{progress}%</span>
                </div>
                <div className="w-full bg-gray-100 rounded-full h-1.5">
                  <div className="h-1.5 rounded-full" style={{ width: progress + "%", background: progress === 100 ? "#10B981" : "#F97316" }} />
                </div>
              </div>
              {/* Footer */}
              <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-px bg-gray-100">
                <div className="bg-white px-3 py-2 text-center">
                  <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-xs">{f.processes.length}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">Processes</p>
                </div>
                <div className="bg-white px-3 py-2 text-center">
                  <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-xs">{allEntries.filter(e => e.styleId === f.id).length}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">Entries</p>
                </div>
                <div className="bg-white px-3 py-2 text-center">
                  <p className={"font-bold text-xs " + (daysLeft < 0 ? "text-red-500" : daysLeft < 7 ? "text-amber-500" : "text-green-600")}>
                    {daysLeft < 0 ? "Overdue" : daysLeft + "d"}
                  </p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">Delivery</p>
                </div>
                <div className="bg-white px-2 py-2 text-center" onClick={e => {
                  e.stopPropagation();
                  setAssignTarget(f);
                  setAssignSelected(f.visibleToSupervisors || []);
                }}>
                  <p className={"font-bold text-xs " + ((f.visibleToSupervisors||[]).length > 0 ? "text-green-600" : "text-gray-400")}>
                    {(f.visibleToSupervisors||[]).length > 0 ? `✅ ${(f.visibleToSupervisors||[]).length}` : "🔒 0"}
                  </p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">Assign</p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          );
        })}
        <Paginator page={sfPage} setPage={setSfPage} totalPages={sfTotalPages} total={sfTotal} pageSize={sfPageSize} />
      </div>

      {/* Assign Supervisors Modal */}
      {assignTarget && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black/50 z-50 flex items-end" onClick={() => setAssignTarget(null)}>
          <div className="bg-white w-full rounded-t-3xl p-5 pb-8 max-h-[80vh] overflow-y-auto" onClick={e => e.stopPropagation()}>
            <div className="w-10 h-1 bg-gray-200 rounded-full mx-auto mb-4"/>
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-1">
              <h3 className="text-base font-extrabold text-gray-800">Supervisors Assign करें</h3>
              <span className="text-xs text-orange-500 font-bold bg-orange-50 px-2 py-1 rounded-lg">{assignSelected.length} selected</span>
            </div>
            <p className="text-xs text-gray-400 mb-4">{assignTarget.styleName} · {assignTarget.styleCode}</p>

            {/* Select All / Clear */}
            <div className="flex gap-2 mb-3">
              <button onClick={() => setAssignSelected(MOCK_DB.supervisorAccounts.map(s=>s.id))}
                className="flex-1 text-xs font-bold py-2 rounded-xl bg-blue-50 text-blue-600 active:bg-blue-100">
                सभी Select करें
              </button>
              <button onClick={() => setAssignSelected([])}
                className="flex-1 text-xs font-bold py-2 rounded-xl bg-gray-50 text-gray-500 active:bg-gray-100">
                Clear
              </button>
            </div>

            {/* Supervisor list */}
            <div className="flex flex-col gap-2 mb-5">
              {MOCK_DB.supervisorAccounts.map(sv => {
                const checked = assignSelected.includes(sv.id);
                return (
                  <div key={sv.id}
                    onClick={() => setAssignSelected(prev => checked ? prev.filter(x=>x!==sv.id) : [...prev, sv.id])}
                    className={"flex items-center gap-3 p-3 rounded-2xl border-2 cursor-pointer transition " + (checked ? "border-orange-400 bg-orange-50" : "border-gray-100 bg-white")}>
                    <div className={"w-5 h-5 rounded-full border-2 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 " + (checked ? "border-orange-500 bg-orange-500" : "border-gray-300")}>
                      {checked && <svg width="10" height="10" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M5 13l4 4L19 7" stroke="white" strokeWidth="3" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>}
                    </div>
                    <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                      <p className="text-sm font-bold text-gray-800">{sv.name}</p>
                      <p className="text-xs text-gray-400">{sv.department} · {sv.staffId}</p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                );
              })}
            </div>

            <div className="flex gap-3">
              <button onClick={() => setAssignTarget(null)}
                className="flex-1 border border-gray-200 text-gray-600 font-bold py-3 rounded-xl text-sm">
                Cancel
              </button>
              <button onClick={() => {
                sharedActions?.assignSupervisors(assignTarget.id, assignSelected);
                setAssignTarget(null);
                flash(`✅ ${assignSelected.length} supervisors को assign किया`);
              }}
                className="flex-1 bg-orange-500 text-white font-extrabold py-3 rounded-xl text-sm shadow shadow-orange-200">
                Save Assignment
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
      <Modal open={showStyleModal} onClose={() => { setShowStyleModal(false); setError(""); }} title="New Style File">
        <div className="space-y-4">
          {error && <div className="bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-xl p-3 text-red-700 text-sm font-semibold">{error}</div>}
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            <Input label="Style Code *" value={styleForm.styleCode} onChange={e => setStyleForm({ ...styleForm, styleCode: e.target.value })} placeholder="SG-2024-005" />
            <Input label="Style Name *" value={styleForm.styleName} onChange={e => setStyleForm({ ...styleForm, styleName: e.target.value })} placeholder="Men's Shirt" />
          </div>
          <Input label="Buyer Name *" value={styleForm.buyerName} onChange={e => setStyleForm({ ...styleForm, buyerName: e.target.value })} placeholder="Reliance Retail" />
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            <Input label="Fabric Type" value={styleForm.fabricType} onChange={e => setStyleForm({ ...styleForm, fabricType: e.target.value })} placeholder="Cotton" />
            <Input label="Color" value={styleForm.color} onChange={e => setStyleForm({ ...styleForm, color: e.target.value })} placeholder="White" />
          </div>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            <Input label="Size Range" value={styleForm.sizeRange} onChange={e => setStyleForm({ ...styleForm, sizeRange: e.target.value })} placeholder="S-XXL" />
            <Input label="Order Qty *" type="number" value={styleForm.orderQuantity} onChange={e => setStyleForm({ ...styleForm, orderQuantity: e.target.value })} placeholder="5000" />
          </div>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            <Input label="Issue Date" type="date" value={styleForm.issueDate} onChange={e => setStyleForm({ ...styleForm, issueDate: e.target.value })} />
            <Input label="Target/Delivery Date *" type="date" value={styleForm.deliveryDate} onChange={e => setStyleForm({ ...styleForm, deliveryDate: e.target.value })} />
          </div>
            <Select label="Status" value={styleForm.status} onChange={e => setStyleForm({ ...styleForm, status: e.target.value })}>
              {["Draft","Active","Completed","Closed"].map(s => <option key={s}>{s}</option>)}
            </Select>
          </div>
          <div className="flex gap-3">
            <Btn variant="secondary" onClick={() => { setShowStyleModal(false); setError(""); }} className="flex-1">Cancel</Btn>
            <Btn onClick={addStyle} className="flex-1">Create Style File</Btn>
          </div>
        </div>
      </Modal>
    </div>
  );
};

const Styles = StyleFiles;


// OPERATIONS
const Operations = () => {
  const [ops, setOps] = useState(MOCK_DB.operations);
  const [showModal, setShowModal] = useState(false);
  const [editOp, setEditOp] = useState(null);
  const [form, setForm] = useState({ name: "", nameHindi: "", pieceRate: "", department: "Stitching" });

  const openAdd = () => { setEditOp(null); setForm({ name:"", nameHindi:"", pieceRate:"", department:"Stitching" }); setShowModal(true); };
  const openEdit = (op) => { setEditOp(op); setForm({ name:op.name, nameHindi:op.nameHindi, pieceRate:String(op.pieceRate), department:op.department }); setShowModal(true); };
  const handleSave = () => {
    if (!form.name || !form.pieceRate) return;
    if (editOp) {
      setOps(prev => prev.map(o => o.id === editOp.id ? { ...o, ...form, pieceRate: +form.pieceRate } : o));
    } else {
      setOps(prev => [...prev, { ...form, id:`op${Date.now()}`, pieceRate:+form.pieceRate }]);
    }
    setShowModal(false); setEditOp(null);
  };
  const handleDelete = (id) => setOps(prev => prev.filter(o => o.id !== id));

  return (
    <div className="space-y-5">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between flex-wrap gap-3">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-extrabold text-gray-900">Operations / काम के प्रकार</h1>
          <p className="text-gray-500 text-sm">{ops.length} operations · piece rate</p>
        </div>
        <Btn onClick={openAdd}>+ Add Operation</Btn>
      </div>

      {/* Card layout — one frame, no scroll */}
      <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-100 overflow-hidden shadow-sm">
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="grid grid-cols-12 bg-orange-500 px-4 py-2.5">
          <div className="col-span-8 text-white text-xs font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wider">Operation</div>
          <div className="col-span-3 text-white text-xs font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wider">Rate</div>
          <div className="col-span-1"></div>
        </div>
        {/* Rows */}
        {ops.map((op, i) => (
          <div key={op.id} className={"grid grid-cols-12 px-4 py-3 items-center " + (i % 2 === 0 ? "bg-white" : "bg-gray-50")}>
            <div className="col-span-8">
              <p className="text-sm font-bold text-gray-800">{op.name}</p>
            </div>
            <div className="col-span-3">
              <span className="text-sm font-extrabold text-green-600">₹{op.pieceRate.toFixed(2)}</span>
            </div>
            <div className="col-span-1 flex flex-col gap-1 items-end">
              <button onClick={() => openEdit(op)} className="text-blue-400 text-xs font-bold">✏️</button>
              <button onClick={() => handleDelete(op.id)} className="text-red-400 text-xs font-bold">🗑️</button>
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      <Modal open={showModal} onClose={() => { setShowModal(false); setEditOp(null); }} title={editOp ? "Edit Operation" : "Add Operation / नया काम"}>
        <div className="space-y-4">
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            <Input label="Operation Name" value={form.name} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, name: e.target.value })} placeholder="Stitching" />
            <Input label="Hindi Name" value={form.nameHindi} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, nameHindi: e.target.value })} placeholder="सिलाई" />
          </div>
          <Select label="Department" value={form.department} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, department: e.target.value })}>
            {MOCK_DB.departments.map(d => <option key={d.id}>{d.name}</option>)}
          </Select>
          <Input label="Piece Rate (₹)" type="number" step="0.01" value={form.pieceRate} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, pieceRate: e.target.value })} placeholder="2.50" />
          <div className="flex gap-3">
            <Btn variant="secondary" onClick={() => { setShowModal(false); setEditOp(null); }} className="flex-1">Cancel</Btn>
            <Btn onClick={handleSave} className="flex-1">{editOp ? "Update" : "Add"}</Btn>
          </div>
        </div>
      </Modal>
    </div>
  );
};

// DEPARTMENTS
// ── SupervisorIdInput — ID type करो, auto details fill ──
const SupervisorIdInput = ({ value, supId, onSupIdChange, onNameChange }) => {
  const [idVal, setIdVal] = React.useState(supId||"");
  const [found, setFound] = React.useState(null);
  const [notFound, setNotFound] = React.useState(false);
  const [showList, setShowList] = React.useState(false);

  const search = (val) => {
    setIdVal(val);
    setNotFound(false);
    if (!val.trim()) { setFound(null); setShowList(false); onSupIdChange("", null); return; }
    const q = val.trim().toLowerCase();
    const match = SUPERVISOR_POOL.find(s =>
      s.staffId.toLowerCase() === q ||
      s.staffId.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      s.mobile === q ||
      s.name.toLowerCase().includes(q)
    );
    if (match) { setFound(match); setNotFound(false); setShowList(false); onSupIdChange(match.staffId, match); }
    else if (val.length >= 3) { setFound(null); setNotFound(true); }
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-2">
      <p className="text-sm font-bold text-gray-800">Supervisor ID <span className="text-gray-400 font-normal text-xs">(ID डालें — auto fill होगा)</span></p>

      <div className="relative">
        <svg className="absolute left-3.5 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-gray-400" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none">
          <circle cx="11" cy="11" r="7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.8"/><path d="M21 21l-4-4" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/>
        </svg>
        <input
          value={idVal}
          onChange={e=>search(e.target.value)}
          onFocus={()=>setShowList(true)}
          placeholder="SUP001 या नाम से खोजें..."
          className={"w-full border-2 rounded-2xl pl-10 pr-4 py-3 font-bold focus:outline-none transition "+(found?"bg-blue-50 border-blue-400 text-blue-900":"bg-gray-50 border-gray-200 text-gray-900")}
          style={{fontSize:"16px"}}
        />
        {idVal && (
          <button onClick={()=>{setIdVal("");setFound(null);setNotFound(false);onSupIdChange("",null);}}
            className="absolute right-3.5 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-gray-400 active:text-gray-600">✕</button>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Suggestions dropdown */}
      {showList && !found && !idVal && (
        <div className="bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-2xl shadow-lg overflow-hidden">
          {SUPERVISOR_POOL.map(s=>(
            <button key={s.id} onMouseDown={()=>{setFound(s);setIdVal(s.staffId);setShowList(false);onSupIdChange(s.staffId,s);}}
              className="w-full flex items-center gap-3 px-4 py-3 hover:bg-blue-50 active:bg-blue-100 text-left border-b border-gray-50 last:border-0 transition">
              <div className="w-9 h-9 rounded-xl bg-blue-100 flex items-center justify-center text-blue-700 font-extrabold text-sm shrink-0">
                {s.name.charAt(0)}
              </div>
              <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-sm truncate">{s.name}</p>
                <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{s.staffId} · {s.designation}</p>
              </div>
              <span className="text-blue-400 text-xs font-bold shrink-0">Select</span>
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Found result card */}
      {found && (
        <div className="bg-blue-50 border-2 border-blue-300 rounded-2xl overflow-hidden">
          <div className="bg-blue-500 px-4 py-1.5">
            <p className="text-white text-xs font-bold">✓ Supervisor मिल गया!</p>
          </div>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3 px-4 py-3">
            <div className="w-12 h-12 rounded-2xl bg-blue-500 flex items-center justify-center text-white font-black text-lg shrink-0">
              {found.name.charAt(0)}
            </div>
            <div className="flex-1">
              <p className="text-blue-900 font-extrabold text-base">{found.name}</p>
              <p className="text-blue-500 text-sm">{found.staffId} · {found.designation}</p>
              <p className="text-blue-400 text-xs">{found.mobile} · Joined {found.joinDate}</p>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Not found — manual input */}
      {notFound && !found && (
        <div className="space-y-2">
          <div className="bg-amber-50 border border-amber-200 rounded-xl px-3 py-2.5 text-amber-700 text-sm">
            "{idVal}" — system में नहीं मिला। नाम manually डालें:
          </div>
          <Input label="Supervisor Name" value={value} placeholder="Supervisor का नाम"
            onChange={e=>onNameChange(e.target.value)}/>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};


// ── Supervisor pool for ID lookup ──
const SUPERVISOR_POOL = [
  { id:"sup1", staffId:"SUP001", name:"Anita Sharma",   mobile:"9811111111", department:"Stitching", designation:"Supervisor", joinDate:"2020-01-15" },
  { id:"sup2", staffId:"SUP002", name:"Ravi Gupta",     mobile:"9822222222", department:"Finishing",  designation:"Supervisor", joinDate:"2019-06-01" },
  { id:"sup3", staffId:"SUP003", name:"Deepak Mehta",   mobile:"9833333333", department:"QC",         designation:"Supervisor", joinDate:"2021-03-10" },
  { id:"sup4", staffId:"SUP004", name:"Suresh Patel",   mobile:"9844444444", department:"Cutting",    designation:"Supervisor", joinDate:"2020-09-20" },
  { id:"sup5", staffId:"SUP005", name:"Kavita Singh",   mobile:"9855555555", department:"Embroidery", designation:"Supervisor", joinDate:"2022-01-05" },
  { id:"sup6", staffId:"SUP006", name:"Mahesh Yadav",   mobile:"9866666666", department:"Packing",    designation:"Supervisor", joinDate:"2021-07-15" },
  { id:"sup7", staffId:"SUP007", name:"Preeti Sharma",  mobile:"9877777777", department:"Stitching",  designation:"Senior Supervisor", joinDate:"2018-04-10" },
];


const Departments = () => {
  const [depts, setDepts] = useState(MOCK_DB.departments.map(d=>({...d})));
  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(null);  // dept id for inline detail
  const [editing, setEditing]   = useState(null);  // dept id for inline edit
  const [editForm, setEditForm] = useState({});
  const [showAdd, setShowAdd]   = useState(false);
  const [addForm, setAddForm]   = useState({name:"",nameHindi:"",supervisor:"",color:"#3B82F6"});
  const [savedMsg, setSavedMsg] = useState("");

  const showToast = (m) => { setSavedMsg(m); setTimeout(()=>setSavedMsg(""),2500); };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4 pb-24">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between flex-wrap gap-3">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-extrabold text-gray-900">Departments / विभाग</h1>
          <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm">Factory departments management</p>
        </div>
        <button onClick={()=>setShowAdd(s=>!s)}
          className="bg-orange-500 text-white font-extrabold text-sm px-4 py-2.5 rounded-2xl shadow-md shadow-orange-200 active:scale-[0.98] transition">
          {showAdd ? "✕ Cancel" : "+ Add Department"}
        </button>
      </div>

      {savedMsg && (
        <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-2xl px-4 py-3 flex items-center gap-2">
          <div className="w-5 h-5 rounded-full bg-green-500 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
            <svg width="10" height="10" viewBox="0 0 12 12" fill="none"><path d="M2 6l3 3 5-5" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
          </div>
          <p className="text-green-700 text-sm font-semibold">{savedMsg}</p>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Add form — inline */}
      {showAdd && (
        <div className="bg-orange-50 border-2 border-orange-200 rounded-2xl p-4 space-y-3">
          <p className="font-extrabold text-orange-700">नया Department जोड़ें</p>
          <Input label="Department Name *" value={addForm.name} placeholder="Embroidery"
            onChange={e=>setAddForm(f=>({...f,name:e.target.value}))}/>
          <Input label="Hindi Name" value={addForm.nameHindi} placeholder="कढ़ाई"
            onChange={e=>setAddForm(f=>({...f,nameHindi:e.target.value}))}/>
          {/* Supervisor ID lookup */}
          <SupervisorIdInput
            value={addForm.supervisor}
            supId={addForm.supervisorId||""}
            onSupIdChange={(id, found)=>{
              if (found) setAddForm(f=>({...f, supervisorId:found.staffId, supervisor:found.name, supervisorMobile:found.mobile, supervisorDetail:found}));
              else setAddForm(f=>({...f, supervisorId:id}));
            }}
            onNameChange={v=>setAddForm(f=>({...f,supervisor:v}))}
          />
          <div>
            <p className="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700 mb-2">Color</p>
            <div className="flex gap-2 flex-wrap">
              {["#3B82F6","#10B981","#F59E0B","#EF4444","#8B5CF6","#EC4899","#F97316","#14B8A6"].map(c=>(
                <button key={c} onClick={()=>setAddForm(f=>({...f,color:c}))}
                  className={"w-9 h-9 rounded-xl border-4 transition active:scale-110 "+(addForm.color===c?"border-gray-800":"border-transparent")}
                  style={{background:c}}/>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
          <button onClick={()=>{
            if (!addForm.name.trim()) return;
            setDepts(prev=>[...prev,{id:"d"+Date.now(),...addForm,workerCount:0,nameHindi:addForm.nameHindi||addForm.name}]);
            setAddForm({name:"",nameHindi:"",supervisor:"",color:"#3B82F6"});
            setShowAdd(false); showToast("Department add हो गई! ✅");
          }} className="w-full bg-orange-500 text-white font-extrabold py-3.5 rounded-2xl active:scale-[0.98] transition">
            Add Department →
          </button>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Department cards */}
      <div className="space-y-3">
        {depts.map(d => {
          const dWorkers = MOCK_DB.workers.filter(w => w.department === d.name);
          const isExpanded = expanded === d.id;
          const isEditing  = editing  === d.id;
          return (
            <div key={d.id} className="bg-white rounded-2xl border-2 border-gray-100 overflow-hidden shadow-sm">
              <div className="h-1.5" style={{background: d.color}}/>
              <div className="p-4">
                {/* Card header */}
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-3">
                  <div className="w-12 h-12 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center font-black text-xl text-white shrink-0"
                    style={{background: d.color}}>{d.name.charAt(0)}</div>
                  <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                    <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-base">{d.name}</p>
                    <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm">{d.nameHindi}</p>
                    <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">Supervisor: {d.supervisor}</p>
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-right shrink-0">
                    <p className="text-2xl font-black" style={{color:d.color}}>{dWorkers.length||d.workerCount}</p>
                    <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">workers</p>
                  </div>
                </div>

                {/* Action buttons */}
                <div className="flex gap-2">
                  <button onClick={()=>{ setExpanded(isExpanded?null:d.id); setEditing(null); }}
                    className={"flex-1 font-bold text-xs py-2.5 rounded-xl border-2 active:scale-[0.98] transition "+(isExpanded?"text-white border-transparent":"border-gray-200 text-gray-600 bg-gray-50")}
                    style={isExpanded?{background:d.color,borderColor:d.color}:{}}>
                    {isExpanded ? "✕ Close" : "View Details"}
                  </button>
                  <button onClick={()=>{ setEditing(isEditing?null:d.id); setEditForm({...d}); setExpanded(null); }}
                    className={"flex-1 font-bold text-xs py-2.5 rounded-xl border-2 active:scale-[0.98] transition "+(isEditing?"bg-gray-800 text-white border-gray-800":"border-gray-200 text-gray-600 bg-gray-50")}>
                    {isEditing ? "✕ Cancel" : "✏️ Edit"}
                  </button>
                </div>

                {/* Inline View Details */}
                {isExpanded && (
                  <div className="mt-3 space-y-3 border-t border-gray-100 pt-3">
                    <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2">
                      {[
                        {label:"Total Workers", val:dWorkers.length||d.workerCount, color:d.color},
                        {label:"Active",  val:dWorkers.filter(w=>w.status==="active").length, color:"#10B981"},
                        {label:"Entries", val:MOCK_DB.workEntries.filter(e=>e.department===d.name).length, color:"#F97316"},
                      ].map(s=>(
                        <div key={s.label} className="rounded-xl py-3 text-center bg-gray-50 border border-gray-100">
                          <p className="text-xl font-black" style={{color:s.color}}>{s.val}</p>
                          <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{s.label}</p>
                        </div>
                      ))}
                    </div>
                    {dWorkers.length > 0 && (
                      <div className="space-y-1.5">
                        <p className="text-xs font-extrabold text-gray-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Workers</p>
                        {dWorkers.map(w=>(
                          <div key={w.id} className="flex items-center gap-2 bg-gray-50 border border-gray-100 rounded-xl px-3 py-2">
                            <div className="w-7 h-7 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center text-white text-xs font-extrabold shrink-0"
                              style={{background:d.color}}>{w.name.charAt(0)}</div>
                            <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                              <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-sm truncate">{w.name}</p>
                              <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{w.staffId}</p>
                            </div>
                            <span className={"text-xs font-bold px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full "+(w.status==="active"?"bg-green-50 text-green-600":"bg-gray-100 text-gray-400")}>
                              {w.status}
                            </span>
                          </div>
                        ))}
                      </div>
                    )}
                  </div>
                )}

                {/* Inline Edit */}
                {isEditing && (
                  <div className="mt-3 space-y-3 border-t border-gray-100 pt-3">
                    <Input label="Department Name" value={editForm.name||""} onChange={e=>setEditForm(f=>({...f,name:e.target.value}))}/>
                    <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
                      <Input label="Hindi Name" value={editForm.nameHindi||""} onChange={e=>setEditForm(f=>({...f,nameHindi:e.target.value}))}/>
                    </div>
                    {/* Supervisor ID lookup */}
                    <SupervisorIdInput
                      value={editForm.supervisor||""}
                      supId={editForm.supervisorId||""}
                      onSupIdChange={(id, found)=>{
                        if (found) setEditForm(f=>({...f, supervisorId:found.staffId, supervisor:found.name, supervisorMobile:found.mobile, supervisorDetail:found}));
                        else setEditForm(f=>({...f, supervisorId:id}));
                      }}
                      onNameChange={v=>setEditForm(f=>({...f,supervisor:v}))}
                    />
                    <div>
                      <p className="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700 mb-2">Color</p>
                      <div className="flex gap-2 flex-wrap">
                        {["#3B82F6","#10B981","#F59E0B","#EF4444","#8B5CF6","#EC4899","#F97316","#14B8A6"].map(c=>(
                          <button key={c} onClick={()=>setEditForm(f=>({...f,color:c}))}
                            className={"w-9 h-9 rounded-xl border-4 transition active:scale-110 "+(editForm.color===c?"border-gray-800":"border-transparent")}
                            style={{background:c}}/>
                        ))}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    <button onClick={()=>{
                      setDepts(prev=>prev.map(x=>x.id===d.id?{...x,...editForm}:x));
                      setEditing(null); showToast(editForm.name+" update हो गई! ✅");
                    }} className="w-full text-white font-extrabold py-3.5 rounded-2xl active:scale-[0.98] transition"
                      style={{background:editForm.color||d.color}}>
                      Save Changes ✓
                    </button>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
          );
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

// PAYMENTS — Auto Monthly Payment Report
const Payments = () => {
  const { user } = useContext(AppContext);
  const now = new Date();
  const MONTHS = [
    { label: "January 2024", value: "2024-01", closed: false },
    { label: "December 2023", value: "2023-12", closed: true },
    { label: "November 2023", value: "2023-11", closed: true },
  ];

  const [selectedMonth, setSelectedMonth] = useState("2024-01");
  const [payments, setPayments] = useState(MOCK_DB.payments);
  const [showSlip, setShowSlip] = useState(null);
  const [showCloseConfirm, setShowCloseConfirm] = useState(false);
  const [advanceModal, setAdvanceModal] = useState(null);
  const [advanceAmt, setAdvanceAmt] = useState("");

  const selectedMonthData = MONTHS.find(m => m.value === selectedMonth);
  const isClosed = selectedMonthData?.closed;

  // Auto-calculate from work entries (only verified ones)
  const WORK_ENTRIES_VERIFIED = MOCK_DB.workEntries.map(e => ({ ...e, status: "verified" }));

  // Rule 10: Build payment report from verified work entries
  const buildReport = (monthKey) => {
    const [yr, mo] = monthKey.split("-").map(Number);
    // Group verified entries by worker
    const grouped = {};
    WORK_ENTRIES_VERIFIED.forEach(e => {
      const d = new Date(e.date);
      if (d.getFullYear() !== yr || d.getMonth() + 1 !== mo) return;
      if (!grouped[e.workerName]) {
        grouped[e.workerName] = {
          workerName: e.workerName, staffId: e.staffId, department: e.department,
          entries: [], totalQty: 0, grossAmount: 0,
        };
      }
      grouped[e.workerName].entries.push(e);
      grouped[e.workerName].totalQty += e.pieces;
      grouped[e.workerName].grossAmount += e.amount;
    });

    // Merge with payments data for deductions/status
    return Object.values(grouped).map(g => {
      const saved = payments.find(p => p.workerName === g.workerName);
      return {
        ...g,
        deductions: saved?.deductions || 0,
        advance: saved?.advance_deduction || 0,
        netAmount: g.grossAmount - (saved?.deductions || 0) - (saved?.advance_deduction || 0),
        status: saved?.status || "pending",
        id: saved?.id || `auto-${g.staffId}`,
      };
    });
  };

  const report = buildReport(selectedMonth);
  const totalQty = report.reduce((s, r) => s + r.totalQty, 0);
  const totalGross = report.reduce((s, r) => s + r.grossAmount, 0);
  const totalDeduct = report.reduce((s, r) => s + r.deductions + r.advance, 0);
  const totalNet = report.reduce((s, r) => s + r.netAmount, 0);

  const markPaid = (id) => setPayments(payments.map(p => p.id === id ? { ...p, status: "paid" } : p));

  const exportCSV = () => {
    const rows = [
      ["Staff ID", "Worker Name", "Department", "Total Qty", "Gross Amount", "Deductions", "Net Amount", "Status"],
      ...report.map(r => [r.staffId, r.workerName, r.department, r.totalQty, r.grossAmount.toFixed(2), (r.deductions + r.advance).toFixed(2), r.netAmount.toFixed(2), r.status]),
    ];
    const csv = rows.map(r => r.join(",")).join("\n");
    const blob = new Blob([csv], { type: "text/csv" });
    const a = document.createElement("a");
    a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    a.download = `payment-report-${selectedMonth}.csv`;
    a.click();
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-5">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between flex-wrap gap-3">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-extrabold text-gray-900">Payment Report / भुगतान रिपोर्ट</h1>
          <p className="text-gray-600 text-sm">Verified entries से auto monthly report</p>
        </div>
        <div className="flex gap-2 flex-wrap">
          <select value={selectedMonth} onChange={e => setSelectedMonth(e.target.value)}
            className="bg-white border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 text-gray-900 text-sm font-semibold focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-400">
            {MONTHS.map(m => (
              <option key={m.value} value={m.value}>{m.label} {m.closed ? " [Closed]" : ""}</option>
            ))}
          </select>
          {user.role === "admin" && !isClosed && (
            <Btn variant="secondary" size="sm" onClick={() => setShowCloseConfirm(true)}>Close Month</Btn>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Month closed banner */}
      {isClosed && (
        <div className="bg-red-50 border-2 border-red-300 rounded-xl p-3 flex items-center gap-3">
          <span className="text-2xl"></span>
          <div>
            <p className="text-red-800 font-bold text-sm">Month Closed / महीना बंद</p>
            <p className="text-red-600 text-xs">{selectedMonthData?.label} की entries lock हो चुकी हैं। कोई नई entry या बदलाव नहीं होगा।</p>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Rule 10 info */}
      <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-xl p-3">
        <p className="text-green-800 text-xs font-bold mb-1">Payment Report Rule (Rule 10):</p>
        <p className="text-green-700 text-xs">सिर्फ <strong>Verified</strong> work entries से auto payment calculate होती है। Pending entries payment में नहीं जाएंगी।</p>
      </div>

      {/* Summary cards */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-4 gap-3">
        {[
          { label: "Total Workers", value: report.length, color: "text-blue-600", bg: "bg-blue-50 border-blue-200" },
          { label: "Total Pieces", value: totalQty.toLocaleString(), color: "text-orange-600", bg: "bg-orange-50 border-orange-200" },
          { label: "Gross Amount", value: `₹${totalGross.toLocaleString()}`, color: "text-purple-600", bg: "bg-purple-50 border-purple-200" },
          { label: "Net Payable", value: `₹${totalNet.toLocaleString()}`, color: "text-green-600", bg: "bg-green-50 border-green-200" },
        ].map(s => (
          <div key={s.label} className={`rounded-xl border-2 p-3 text-center ${s.bg}`}>
            <p className={`text-xl font-extrabold ${s.color}`}>{s.value}</p>
            <p className="text-gray-600 text-xs font-semibold mt-0.5">{s.label}</p>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Payment table */}
      <div className="space-y-3">
        {report.length === 0 && (
          <div className="text-center py-10 text-gray-400">इस month में कोई verified entry नहीं है।</div>
        )}
        {report.map((r, i) => (
          <div key={r.id || i} className={`bg-white rounded-2xl border-2 p-4 shadow-sm ${r.status === "paid" ? "border-green-200" : "border-gray-100"}`}>
            <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-3">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                <div className="w-10 h-10 bg-gradient-to-br from-orange-500 to-orange-600 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center text-white font-extrabold text-base shrink-0">
                  {r.workerName?.charAt(0)}
                </div>
                <div>
                  <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold">{r.workerName}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs">{r.staffId} • {r.department}</p>
                </div>
              </div>
              <Badge color={r.status === "paid" ? "green" : r.status === "hold" ? "red" : "amber"} size="xs">
                {r.status === "paid" ? "Paid" : r.status === "hold" ? "Hold" : "Pending"}
              </Badge>
            </div>

            {/* Rule 10 breakdown table */}
            <div className="bg-gray-50 rounded-xl p-3 mb-3">
              <p className="text-gray-600 text-xs font-bold mb-2">Auto Calculated — Verified Entries Only</p>
              <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-2 text-center">
                <div>
                  <p className="text-orange-600 font-extrabold text-base">{r.totalQty.toLocaleString()}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs">Total Qty</p>
                </div>
                <div>
                  <p className="text-blue-600 font-bold text-base">₹{r.grossAmount.toLocaleString()}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs">Gross</p>
                </div>
                <div>
                  <p className="text-red-500 font-bold text-base">-₹{(r.deductions + r.advance).toFixed(0)}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs">Deduct</p>
                </div>
                <div className="bg-green-50 rounded-lg py-1">
                  <p className="text-green-600 font-extrabold text-base">₹{r.netAmount.toLocaleString()}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs">Net Pay</p>
                </div>
              </div>
              {/* Formula reminder */}
              <p className="text-center text-gray-400 text-xs mt-2">
                Formula: {r.totalQty} pcs × avg rate = ₹{r.grossAmount.toFixed(0)} − ₹{(r.deductions + r.advance).toFixed(0)} = <strong className="text-green-600">₹{r.netAmount.toFixed(0)}</strong>
              </p>
            </div>

            {/* Entry breakdown (expand) */}
            {r.entries?.length > 0 && (
              <details className="mb-3">
                <summary className="text-xs text-blue-600 font-semibold cursor-pointer hover:text-blue-800">
                  {r.entries.length} verified entries देखें
                </summary>
                <div className="mt-2 space-y-1">
                  {r.entries.map((e, j) => (
                    <div key={j} className="flex justify-between text-xs bg-gray-50 rounded-lg px-3 py-1.5">
                      <span className="text-gray-700">{e.date} • {e.operation}</span>
                      <span className="text-gray-500">{e.pieces} × ₹{e.pieceRate}</span>
                      <span className="text-green-600 font-bold">₹{e.amount}</span>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </details>
            )}

            <div className="flex gap-2">
              {r.status !== "paid" && !isClosed && user.role !== "worker" && (
                <Btn variant="success" size="sm" className="flex-1 font-bold" onClick={() => markPaid(r.id)}>
                  Mark Paid
                </Btn>
              )}
              {r.status === "paid" && (
                <div className="flex-1 flex items-center justify-center gap-1 bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-xl py-2 text-green-600 text-xs font-bold">
                  ✓ Payment Done
                </div>
              )}
              <Btn variant="secondary" size="sm" onClick={() => setShowSlip(r)}>Slip</Btn>
              {user.role !== "worker" && (
                <Btn variant="ghost" size="sm" className="border border-gray-200" onClick={() => { setAdvanceModal(r); setAdvanceAmt(""); }}>
                  Advance
                </Btn>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Export & Close */}
      <div className="flex gap-3">
        <Btn variant="secondary" className="flex-1" onClick={exportCSV}>Export CSV</Btn>
        {user.role === "admin" && !isClosed && (
          <Btn className="flex-1" onClick={() => setShowCloseConfirm(true)}>Close Month & Lock</Btn>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Payment Slip Modal */}
      <Modal open={!!showSlip} onClose={() => setShowSlip(null)} title="Payment Slip / भुगतान पर्ची" size="sm">
        {showSlip && (
          <div className="space-y-3">
            <div className="border-2 border-dashed border-gray-300 rounded-xl p-4">
              <div className="text-center mb-3">
                <p className="font-extrabold text-gray-900 text-lg">Sharma Garments</p>
                <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs">Payment Slip — {selectedMonthData?.label}</p>
                <div className="border-t border-dashed border-gray-300 my-2" />
              </div>
              <div className="space-y-2 text-sm">
                {[
                  ["Worker", showSlip.workerName],
                  ["Staff ID", showSlip.staffId],
                  ["Department", showSlip.department],
                  ["Total Pieces", `${showSlip.totalQty} pcs`],
                  ["Gross Amount", `₹${showSlip.grossAmount.toFixed(2)}`],
                  ["Deductions", `-₹${(showSlip.deductions + showSlip.advance).toFixed(2)}`],
                ].map(([k, v]) => (
                  <div key={k} className="flex justify-between border-b border-gray-100 pb-1">
                    <span className="text-gray-500 font-semibold">{k}</span>
                    <span className="text-gray-900 font-bold">{v}</span>
                  </div>
                ))}
                <div className="flex justify-between bg-green-50 rounded-lg px-3 py-2 mt-2">
                  <span className="text-green-700 font-extrabold">Net Payable / कुल</span>
                  <span className="text-green-600 font-extrabold text-lg">₹{showSlip.netAmount.toFixed(2)}</span>
                </div>
              </div>
              <div className="text-center mt-3 text-gray-400 text-xs">
                Status: <strong className={showSlip.status === "paid" ? "text-green-600" : "text-amber-600"}>{showSlip.status.toUpperCase()}</strong>
              </div>
            </div>
            <Btn className="w-full" onClick={() => window.print()}>Print Slip</Btn>
          </div>
        )}
      </Modal>

      {/* Advance Deduction Modal */}
      <Modal open={!!advanceModal} onClose={() => setAdvanceModal(null)} title="Advance Deduction" size="sm">
        {advanceModal && (
          <div className="space-y-4">
            <div className="bg-amber-50 border border-amber-200 rounded-xl p-3">
              <p className="text-amber-800 font-bold text-sm">{advanceModal.workerName}</p>
              <p className="text-amber-600 text-xs">Current Net: ₹{advanceModal.netAmount.toFixed(0)}</p>
            </div>
            <Input label="Advance Amount / अग्रिम राशि" type="number" value={advanceAmt} onChange={e => setAdvanceAmt(e.target.value)} placeholder="₹500" />
            <div className="flex gap-3">
              <Btn variant="secondary" onClick={() => setAdvanceModal(null)} className="flex-1">Cancel</Btn>
              <Btn onClick={() => {
                setPayments(payments.map(p => p.workerName === advanceModal.workerName ? { ...p, advance_deduction: (p.advance_deduction || 0) + +advanceAmt } : p));
                setAdvanceModal(null);
              }} className="flex-1">Apply Deduction</Btn>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </Modal>

      {/* Close Month Confirm */}
      <Modal open={showCloseConfirm} onClose={() => setShowCloseConfirm(false)} title="Month Close करें?" size="sm">
        <div className="space-y-4">
          <div className="bg-red-50 border-2 border-red-200 rounded-xl p-4">
            <p className="text-red-800 font-bold">Warning / चेतावनी</p>
            <p className="text-red-600 text-sm mt-1">{selectedMonthData?.label} को close करने के बाद:</p>
            <ul className="text-red-500 text-xs mt-2 space-y-1 list-disc list-inside">
              <li>कोई नई entry नहीं होगी</li>
              <li>Worker entries read-only हो जाएंगी</li>
              <li>सिर्फ Supervisor ही edit कर सकेगा</li>
              <li>यह action undo नहीं हो सकती</li>
            </ul>
          </div>
          <div className="flex gap-3">
            <Btn variant="secondary" onClick={() => setShowCloseConfirm(false)} className="flex-1">Cancel</Btn>
            <Btn onClick={() => { LOCKED_MONTHS.push(selectedMonth); setShowCloseConfirm(false); }} className="flex-1 bg-red-500 hover:bg-red-600 text-white">
               Confirm Close
            </Btn>
          </div>
        </div>
      </Modal>
    </div>
  );
};

// HOURLY REPORTS
const DEPT_TARGETS = {};
MOCK_DB.departments.forEach(d => { DEPT_TARGETS[d.name] = d.dailyTarget || 400; });

const WORK_HOURS = 8; // total working hours per day
const ALL_HOUR_SLOTS = ["08:00-09:00","09:00-10:00","10:00-11:00","11:00-12:00","12:00-13:00","14:00-15:00","15:00-16:00","16:00-17:00"];

const HourlyReports = () => {
  const [reports,    setReports]    = useState(MOCK_DB.hourlyReports);
  const [showModal,  setShowModal]  = useState(false);
  const [selDept,    setSelDept]    = useState("all");
  const [selDate,    setSelDate]    = useState(new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0]);
  const [deptTargets, setDeptTargets] = useState({...DEPT_TARGETS});
  const [editTargetDept, setEditTargetDept] = useState(null);
  const [editTargetVal, setEditTargetVal]   = useState("");
  const [form, setForm] = useState({ date:"", department:"", style:"", hourSlot:"", total:"", pass:"", alter:"", reject:"" });

  const handleAdd = () => {
    const total = +form.total, pass = +form.pass;
    setReports(prev => [...prev, { ...form, id:`h${Date.now()}`, total, pass, alter:+form.alter, reject:+form.reject,
      passPercent: total ? ((pass/total)*100).toFixed(1) : 0 }]);
    setShowModal(false);
  };

  const depts = ["all", ...new Set(MOCK_DB.departments.map(d=>d.name))];
  const filteredDepts = selDept === "all" ? MOCK_DB.departments : MOCK_DB.departments.filter(d=>d.name===selDept);

  return (
    <div className="space-y-5 pb-24">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between flex-wrap gap-3">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-extrabold text-gray-900">Hourly Production Report</h1>
          <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm">घंटेवार target vs actual</p>
        </div>
        <div className="flex gap-2">
          <input type="date" value={selDate} onChange={e=>setSelDate(e.target.value)}
            className="bg-gray-50 border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 text-sm font-bold focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-400"
            style={{fontSize:"16px"}}/>
          <button onClick={()=>{ setForm({date:selDate,department:"",style:"",hourSlot:"",total:"",pass:"",alter:"",reject:""}); setShowModal(true); }}
            className="bg-orange-500 text-white font-extrabold text-sm px-4 py-2 rounded-xl shadow-md shadow-orange-200 active:scale-[0.98] whitespace-nowrap">
            + Add
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Dept filter */}
      <div className="flex gap-2 overflow-x-auto pb-1 no-scrollbar">
        {depts.map(d=>(
          <button key={d} onClick={()=>setSelDept(d)}
            className={"shrink-0 px-3.5 py-1.5 rounded-full text-xs font-extrabold border transition "+(selDept===d?"bg-orange-500 text-white border-orange-500":"bg-white text-gray-500 border-gray-200")}>
            {d==="all"?"सभी":d}
          </button>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Per-department hourly breakdown */}
      {filteredDepts.map(dept => {
        const dailyTarget  = deptTargets[dept.name] || 400;
        const hourlyTarget = Math.round(dailyTarget / WORK_HOURS);
        const deptReports  = reports.filter(r => r.department === dept.name && r.date === selDate);

        // Map slot → actual pieces
        const slotMap = {};
        deptReports.forEach(r => { slotMap[r.hourSlot] = (slotMap[r.hourSlot]||0) + (+r.total||0); });

        const totalActual = Object.values(slotMap).reduce((s,v)=>s+v, 0);
        const hoursLogged = Object.keys(slotMap).length;
        const totalExpected = hoursLogged * hourlyTarget;
        const overallDiff = totalActual - totalExpected;

        return (
          <div key={dept.id} className="bg-white rounded-2xl border-2 border-gray-100 shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
            {/* Dept header bar */}
            <div className="h-1.5" style={{background: dept.color}}/>
            <div className="p-4">
              {/* Dept title + target */}
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                  <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center text-white font-black text-base shrink-0"
                    style={{background: dept.color}}>{dept.name.charAt(0)}</div>
                  <div>
                    <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-base">{dept.name}</p>
                    <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{dept.nameHindi} · {dept.supervisor}</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div className="text-right">
                  {editTargetDept === dept.name ? (
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
                      <input type="number" inputMode="numeric" value={editTargetVal}
                        onChange={e=>setEditTargetVal(e.target.value)}
                        className="w-20 bg-gray-50 border-2 border-orange-300 rounded-lg px-2 py-1 text-sm font-bold text-center focus:outline-none"
                        style={{fontSize:"16px"}}/>
                      <button onClick={()=>{ setDeptTargets(t=>({...t,[dept.name]:+editTargetVal})); setEditTargetDept(null); }}
                        className="text-xs bg-orange-500 text-white font-bold px-2 py-1 rounded-lg">✓</button>
                    </div>
                  ) : (
                    <button onClick={()=>{ setEditTargetDept(dept.name); setEditTargetVal(String(dailyTarget)); }}
                      className="text-right active:opacity-70">
                      <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-base">{dailyTarget} <span className="text-gray-400 text-xs font-normal">pcs/day</span></p>
                      <p className="text-orange-500 text-xs font-bold">{hourlyTarget} pcs/hr · tap to edit ✏️</p>
                    </button>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* Overall summary */}
              {hoursLogged > 0 && (
                <div className={"flex items-center justify-between rounded-xl px-4 py-3 mb-3 border "+(overallDiff>=0?"bg-green-50 border-green-200":"bg-red-50 border-red-200")}>
                  <div>
                    <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs font-bold">आज का कुल ({hoursLogged} hrs logged)</p>
                    <p className={"text-xl font-black "+(overallDiff>=0?"text-green-700":"text-red-600")}>{totalActual} <span className="text-sm font-bold">/ {totalExpected}</span></p>
                  </div>
                  <div className={"text-2xl font-black px-3 py-1 rounded-xl "+(overallDiff>=0?"text-green-600 bg-green-100":"text-red-600 bg-red-100")}>
                    {overallDiff>=0?"+":""}{overallDiff}
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}

              {/* Hour-by-hour rows */}
              <div className="space-y-2">
                <div className="grid grid-cols-4 px-2 mb-1">
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs font-bold">Hour</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs font-bold text-center">Target</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs font-bold text-center">Actual</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs font-bold text-right">+/-</p>
                </div>
                {ALL_HOUR_SLOTS.map(slot => {
                  const actual = slotMap[slot] || 0;
                  const diff   = actual - hourlyTarget;
                  const hasData = slot in slotMap;
                  return (
                    <div key={slot} className={"grid grid-cols-4 items-center rounded-xl px-3 py-2.5 border "+(
                      !hasData ? "bg-gray-50 border-gray-100 opacity-50" :
                      diff >= 0 ? "bg-green-50 border-green-200" : "bg-red-50 border-red-200"
                    )}>
                      <p className={"text-xs font-extrabold "+(hasData?"text-gray-900":"text-gray-400")}>{slot.split("-")[0]}</p>
                      <p className="text-center text-xs font-bold text-gray-500">{hourlyTarget}</p>
                      <p className={"text-center text-sm font-black "+(
                        !hasData ? "text-gray-300" : diff>=0?"text-green-700":"text-red-600"
                      )}>{hasData ? actual : "—"}</p>
                      <div className="text-right">
                        {hasData ? (
                          <span className={"text-sm font-black px-2 py-0.5 rounded-lg "+(diff>=0?"bg-green-200 text-green-800":"bg-red-200 text-red-800")}>
                            {diff>=0?"+":""}{diff}
                          </span>
                        ) : <span className="text-gray-300 text-xs">—</span>}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  );
                })}
              </div>

              {deptReports.length === 0 && (
                <div className="text-center py-6 text-gray-400 text-sm mt-2">
                  इस date पर कोई report नहीं · "+" से add करें
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
        );
      })}

      {/* Add Report Modal */}
      <Modal open={showModal} onClose={()=>setShowModal(false)} title="Hourly Report Add करें">
        <div className="space-y-4">
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            <Input label="Date" type="date" value={form.date} onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({...f,date:e.target.value}))}/>
            <Select label="Hour Slot" value={form.hourSlot} onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({...f,hourSlot:e.target.value}))}>
              <option value="">-- Slot --</option>
              {ALL_HOUR_SLOTS.map(s=><option key={s} value={s}>{s}</option>)}
            </Select>
          </div>
          <Select label="Department" value={form.department} onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({...f,department:e.target.value}))}>
            <option value="">-- Department --</option>
            {MOCK_DB.departments.map(d=><option key={d.id} value={d.name}>{d.name}</option>)}
          </Select>
          <Select label="Style" value={form.style} onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({...f,style:e.target.value}))}>
            <option value="">-- Style --</option>
            {MOCK_DB.styles.map(s=><option key={s.id} value={s.styleName}>{s.styleName}</option>)}
          </Select>
          {form.department && (
            <div className="bg-orange-50 border border-orange-200 rounded-xl px-4 py-2.5 flex items-center justify-between">
              <p className="text-orange-600 text-sm font-bold">Per Hour Target:</p>
              <p className="text-orange-700 font-black text-lg">{Math.round((deptTargets[form.department]||400)/WORK_HOURS)} pcs</p>
            </div>
          )}
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            <Input label="Total Pieces" type="number" value={form.total} placeholder="0" onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({...f,total:e.target.value}))}/>
            <Input label="Pass ✓" type="number" value={form.pass} placeholder="0" onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({...f,pass:e.target.value}))}/>
          </div>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            <Input label="Alter ↻" type="number" value={form.alter} placeholder="0" onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({...f,alter:e.target.value}))}/>
            <Input label="Reject ✗" type="number" value={form.reject} placeholder="0" onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({...f,reject:e.target.value}))}/>
          </div>
          {form.total && form.department && (
            <div className={"rounded-xl px-4 py-3 border flex items-center justify-between "+(
              +form.total >= Math.round((deptTargets[form.department]||400)/WORK_HOURS)
              ? "bg-green-50 border-green-200" : "bg-red-50 border-red-200"
            )}>
              <p className="text-sm font-bold text-gray-600">Target vs Actual:</p>
              <p className={"font-black text-lg "+(+form.total >= Math.round((deptTargets[form.department]||400)/WORK_HOURS)?"text-green-700":"text-red-600")}>
                {+form.total >= Math.round((deptTargets[form.department]||400)/WORK_HOURS) ? "✅ On Track" : "🔴 Below Target"}
                <span className="text-sm ml-1">
                  ({+form.total - Math.round((deptTargets[form.department]||400)/WORK_HOURS) >= 0 ? "+" : ""}
                  {+form.total - Math.round((deptTargets[form.department]||400)/WORK_HOURS)})
                </span>
              </p>
            </div>
          )}
          <div className="flex gap-3">
            <Btn variant="secondary" className="flex-1" onClick={()=>setShowModal(false)}>Cancel</Btn>
            <Btn className="flex-1" onClick={handleAdd}>Save Report →</Btn>
          </div>
        </div>
      </Modal>
    </div>
  );
};

const JobPortal = () => {
  const { user } = useContext(AppContext);
  const [jobs, setJobs] = useState(MOCK_DB.jobs);
  const [showModal, setShowModal] = useState(false);
  const [applyModal, setApplyModal] = useState(null);
  const [form, setForm] = useState({ title: "", department: "", salary: "", experience: "", openings: "1", description: "", workType: "" });
  const [error, setError] = useState("");

  const emptyForm = { title: "", department: "", salary: "", experience: "", openings: "1", description: "", workType: "" };

  const postJob = () => {
    if (!form.title || !form.department) { setError("Job Title और Department जरूरी है।"); return; }
    const newJob = {
      id: "j" + Date.now(),
      title: form.title,
      department: form.department,
      salary: form.salary || "Not specified",
      experience: form.experience || "Any",
      openings: +form.openings || 1,
      description: form.description,
      workType: form.workType,
      status: "active",
      postedDate: new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0],
      applications: 0,
    };
    setJobs([newJob, ...jobs]);
    setShowModal(false);
    setForm(emptyForm);
    setError("");
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-5">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between flex-wrap gap-3">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-extrabold text-gray-900">Job Portal / नौकरी</h1>
          <p className="text-gray-900 text-sm">{jobs.filter(j => j.status === "active").length} active openings</p>
        </div>
        {(user.role === "admin" || user.role === "supervisor") && (
          <Btn onClick={() => setShowModal(true)}>+ Post Job</Btn>
        )}
      </div>

      <div className="grid sm:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
        {jobs.map(job => (
          <div key={job.id} className="bg-gray-50 rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 p-5 hover:border-orange-500/30 transition">
            <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-3">
              <div className="w-12 h-12 bg-gradient-to-br from-blue-500/20 to-blue-600/20 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center text-2xl border border-blue-500/20">
                Dept
              </div>
              <Badge color={job.status === "active" ? "green" : "slate"} size="xs">{job.status}</Badge>
            </div>
            <h3 className="text-gray-900 font-bold">{job.title}</h3>
            <p className="text-gray-900 text-sm mt-0.5">{job.department} Department</p>
            {job.workType && (
              <span className={"inline-block mt-1 text-xs font-bold px-2.5 py-0.5 rounded-lg " +
                (job.workType === "salary" ? "bg-blue-50 text-blue-700" :
                 job.workType === "piece_rate" ? "bg-orange-50 text-orange-600" :
                 "bg-green-50 text-green-700")}>
                {job.workType === "salary" ? "Salary Based" : job.workType === "piece_rate" ? "Piece Rate" : "Commission"}
              </span>
            )}
            <p className="text-gray-700 text-xs mt-2">{job.description}</p>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2 mt-3 text-xs">
              <div className="bg-gray-100 rounded-lg p-2">
                <p className="text-gray-900">Work Type</p>
                <p className={"font-semibold " + (job.workType === "salary" ? "text-blue-600" : job.workType === "piece_rate" ? "text-orange-500" : "text-green-600")}>
                  {job.workType === "salary" ? "Salary" : job.workType === "piece_rate" ? "Piece Rate" : job.workType === "commission" ? "Commission" : "—"}
                </p>
              </div>
              {job.workType === "salary" && (
                <div className="bg-blue-50 rounded-lg p-2">
                  <p className="text-gray-900">Salary</p>
                  <p className="text-blue-700 font-extrabold">{job.salary}</p>
                </div>
              )}
              <div className="bg-gray-100 rounded-lg p-2">
                <p className="text-gray-900">Experience</p>
                <p className="text-blue-400 font-semibold">{job.experience}</p>
              </div>
              <div className="bg-gray-100 rounded-lg p-2">
                <p className="text-gray-900">Kitne Workers Chahiye</p>
                <p className="text-orange-400 font-bold">{job.openings}</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="flex gap-2 mt-3">
              {user.role === "worker" || user.role === "contractor" ? (
                <Btn onClick={() => setApplyModal(job)} className="flex-1">Apply Now</Btn>
              ) : (
                <>
                  <Btn variant="secondary" size="sm" className="flex-1">View Applications</Btn>
                  <Btn variant="danger" size="sm">Close</Btn>
                </>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      <Modal open={showModal} onClose={() => setShowModal(false)} title="Post New Job / नौकरी पोस्ट करें">
        <div className="space-y-4">
          {error && <div className="bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-xl p-3 text-red-700 text-sm font-semibold">{error}</div>}
          <Input label="Job Title" value={form.title} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, title: e.target.value })} placeholder="Experienced Tailor" />
          <Select label="Department" value={form.department} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, department: e.target.value })}>
            <option value="">Select Department</option>
            {MOCK_DB.departments.map(d => <option key={d.id}>{d.name}</option>)}
          </Select>

          {/* Work Type Cards */}
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-bold text-gray-900 mb-2">Work Type / काम का प्रकार</label>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2">
              {[
                { key: "salary",     label: "Salary",      hindi: "मासिक वेतन", icon: "jobs", color: "blue"   },
                { key: "piece_rate", label: "Piece Rate",  hindi: "पीस रेट",    icon: "", color: "orange" },
                { key: "commission", label: "Commission",  hindi: "कमीशन",      icon: "", color: "green"  },
              ].map(t => (
                <button key={t.key} type="button"
                  onClick={() => setForm({ ...form, workType: t.key })}
                  className={"rounded-2xl border-2 p-3 text-center transition " +
                    (form.workType === t.key
                      ? t.color === "blue"   ? "border-blue-500 bg-blue-50"
                      : t.color === "orange" ? "border-orange-500 bg-orange-50"
                      :                        "border-green-500 bg-green-50"
                      : "border-gray-200 bg-white hover:border-gray-300")}>
                  <div className="text-2xl mb-1">{t.icon}</div>
                  <p className={"text-xs font-extrabold " +
                    (form.workType === t.key
                      ? t.color === "blue" ? "text-blue-700" : t.color === "orange" ? "text-orange-600" : "text-green-700"
                      : "text-gray-700")}>
                    {t.label}
                  </p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs mt-0.5">{t.hindi}</p>
                </button>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Salary field — only when Salary type selected */}
          {form.workType === "salary" && (
            <div className="bg-blue-50 border-2 border-blue-200 rounded-2xl p-3 space-y-3">
              <p className="text-blue-700 text-xs font-extrabold">Salary Details</p>
              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
                <Input label="Min Salary (Rs)" type="number" value={form.salaryMin || ""} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, salaryMin: e.target.value, salary: `Rs ${e.target.value}${form.salaryMax ? " - Rs " + form.salaryMax : ""}` })} placeholder="8000" />
                <Input label="Max Salary (Rs)" type="number" value={form.salaryMax || ""} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, salaryMax: e.target.value, salary: `Rs ${form.salaryMin || ""}${e.target.value ? " - Rs " + e.target.value : ""}` })} placeholder="12000" />
              </div>
              {form.salaryMin && (
                <div className="bg-white rounded-xl px-3 py-2 text-sm">
                  <span className="text-gray-500">Salary Range: </span>
                  <span className="text-blue-700 font-extrabold">Rs {form.salaryMin}{form.salaryMax ? " - Rs " + form.salaryMax : "+"} / month</span>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          )}

          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            {form.workType !== "salary" && (
              <Input label="Salary Range" value={form.salary} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, salary: e.target.value })} placeholder="Rs 8,000-12,000" />
            )}
            <Input label="Experience" value={form.experience} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, experience: e.target.value })} placeholder="2+ years" className={form.workType === "salary" ? "" : ""} />
          </div>
          <Input label="Kitne Workers Chahiye" type="number" value={form.openings} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, openings: e.target.value })} />
          <div className="space-y-1.5">
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">Description</label>
            <textarea value={form.description} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, description: e.target.value })}
              rows={3} placeholder="Job description..."
              className="w-full bg-white border border-slate-600 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 text-gray-900 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-500 placeholder-slate-400" />
          </div>
          <div className="flex gap-3">
            <Btn variant="secondary" onClick={() => { setShowModal(false); setError(""); setForm(emptyForm); }} className="flex-1">Cancel</Btn>
            <Btn onClick={postJob} className="flex-1">Post Job</Btn>
          </div>
        </div>
      </Modal>

      <Modal open={!!applyModal} onClose={() => setApplyModal(null)} title="Apply for Job / आवेदन करें">
        {applyModal && (
          <div className="space-y-4">
            <div className="bg-blue-500/10 border border-blue-500/20 rounded-xl p-3">
              <p className="text-blue-400 font-semibold">{applyModal.title}</p>
              <p className="text-gray-900 text-sm">{applyModal.department} • {applyModal.salary}</p>
            </div>
            <Input label="Your Name" placeholder="Full name" />
            <Input label="Mobile Number" type="tel" placeholder="Your mobile" />
            <Input label="Experience (years)" type="number" placeholder="2" />
            <Input label="Expected Salary" placeholder="₹10,000" />
            <div className="space-y-1.5">
              <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">Skills / कौशल</label>
              <textarea rows={2} placeholder="Stitching, Overlock, etc."
                className="w-full bg-white border border-slate-600 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 text-gray-900 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-500 placeholder-slate-400" />
            </div>
            <div className="flex gap-3">
              <Btn variant="secondary" onClick={() => setApplyModal(null)} className="flex-1">Cancel</Btn>
              <Btn onClick={() => setApplyModal(null)} className="flex-1">Submit Application</Btn>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </Modal>
    </div>
  );
};


// PROFILE
const Profile = ({ onLogout }) => {
