                                    <div key={i} className={`grid grid-cols-4 px-3.5 py-2.5 border-t border-gray-50 ${i%2===0?"bg-white":"bg-gray-50/40"}`}>
                                      <div className="flex items-center">
                                        <span className="w-6 h-6 rounded-lg bg-red-100 text-red-600 text-[9px] font-black flex items-center justify-center">{row.size}</span>
                                      </div>
                                      <p className="text-gray-600 text-xs font-semibold text-center self-center">{row.bundles}</p>
                                      <p className="text-gray-600 text-xs font-semibold text-center self-center">{row.pcsPerBundle}</p>
                                      <p className="text-red-600 font-extrabold text-xs text-right self-center">{row.total}</p>
                                    </div>
                                  ))}
                                  <div className="grid grid-cols-4 px-3.5 py-3 bg-gradient-to-r from-red-50 to-orange-50 border-t border-red-100">
                                    <p className="text-red-700 font-black text-xs col-span-3 flex items-center gap-1">
                                      <span className="w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-red-500 inline-block"/>TOTAL
                                    </p>
                                    <p className="text-red-700 font-black text-sm text-right">{c.totalPieces}</p>
                                  </div>
                                </div>
                              )}
                            </div>
                          );
                        })}

                        {/* Add new entry button */}
                        <button
                          onClick={e=>{e.stopPropagation();setShowCutForm(true);setCutErr("");setCutForm({date:TODAY_CUT,styleId:style.id,marker:"",sizes:[{size:"",bundles:"",pcsPerBundle:""}]});autoFillSizes(style.id);}}
                          className="w-full flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5 border-2 border-dashed border-red-200 text-red-400 text-xs font-extrabold py-3 rounded-2xl active:bg-red-50 transition">
                          <svg width="13" height="13" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M12 5v14M5 12h14" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
                          नई Cutting Entry जोड़ें
                        </button>
                      </div>
                    )}
                  </div>
                )}

              </div>
            );
          })}
        </div>

        {/* Add Cutting Modal */}
        <Modal open={showCutForm} onClose={()=>setShowCutForm(false)} title={cutForm._editId?"Cutting Edit करें":"नई Cutting Entry"}>
          <div className="space-y-5">
            {cutErr && <div className="bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-xl p-3 text-red-600 text-sm">{cutErr}</div>}

            {/* Date + Style */}
            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
              <Input label="Date" type="date" value={cutForm.date} max={TODAY}
                onChange={e=>setCutForm(f=>({...f,date:e.target.value}))}/>
              <Input label="Cutting No." value={cutForm.marker} placeholder="C-001"
                onChange={e=>setCutForm(f=>({...f,marker:e.target.value}))}/>
            </div>
            <Select label="Style / Order" value={cutForm.styleId}
              onChange={e=>{ if(!cutForm._editId) autoFillSizes(e.target.value); else setCutForm(f=>({...f,styleId:e.target.value})); }}>
              <option value="">-- Style चुनें --</option>
              {svVisibleStyles.map(s=><option key={s.id} value={s.id}>{s.styleName}</option>)}
            </Select>

            {/* Size rows */}
            <div>
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
                <p className="text-gray-700 text-sm font-extrabold">Size-wise Layers</p>
                <span className="text-red-500 text-xs font-bold bg-red-50 px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full border border-red-100">
                  {grandTotal > 0 ? `Total: ${grandTotal} pcs` : "0 pcs"}
                </span>
              </div>

              {/* Header */}
              <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 mb-1.5 px-1">
                <p className="w-20 shrink-0 text-gray-400 text-xs font-bold text-center">Size</p>
                <p className="flex-1 text-gray-400 text-xs font-bold text-center">Bundles</p>
                <p className="flex-1 text-gray-400 text-xs font-bold text-center">Pcs/Bundle</p>
                <p className="w-11 shrink-0 text-gray-400 text-xs font-bold text-center">Total</p>
              </div>
              {/* First row hint */}
              {cutForm.sizes.length > 1 && (!cutForm.sizes[0].bundles || !cutForm.sizes[0].pcsPerBundle) && (
                <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 bg-orange-50 border border-orange-200 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 mb-1">
                  <svg width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="9" stroke="#F97316" strokeWidth="1.8"/><path d="M12 8v4M12 16h.01" stroke="#F97316" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
                  <p className="text-orange-600 text-xs font-semibold">पहली row में Bundles & Pcs/Bundle डालें — सभी sizes में auto-fill होगा</p>
                </div>
              )}

              <div className="space-y-2">
                {cutForm.sizes.map((row,idx)=>(
                  <SizeRow
                    key={idx}
                    row={row}
                    idx={idx}
                    onUpdate={updateSize}
                    onRemove={removeSizeRow}
                    sizeTotal={sizeTotal}
                  />
                ))}
              </div>

              {/* Total row */}
              {grandTotal > 0 && (
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between bg-red-50 border border-red-100 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 mt-3">
                  <div>
                    <p className="text-red-700 text-xs font-bold">{grandBundles} total bundles</p>
                    <p className="text-red-400 text-xs">{cutForm.sizes.filter(r=>r.size).length} sizes</p>
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-right">
                    <p className="text-red-700 font-black text-2xl">{grandTotal}</p>
                    <p className="text-red-400 text-xs">total pieces</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}

              {/* Quick preset buttons */}
              <div className="mt-2 space-y-2">
                <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs font-bold uppercase tracking-wider">Quick Fill</p>
                <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1.5">
                  {[
                    { label:"Standard", sizes:["XS","S","M","L","XL","XXL","XXXL"] },
                    { label:"Waist",    sizes:["28","30","32","34","36","38","40"] },
                    { label:"Kids",     sizes:["2Y","4Y","6Y","8Y","10Y","12Y"] },
                    { label:"Baby",     sizes:["3M","6M","9M","12M","18M","24M"] },
                    { label:"Kurta",    sizes:["36","38","40","42","44","46"] },
                  ].map(preset=>(
                    <button key={preset.label}
                      onClick={()=>setCutForm(f=>({...f, sizes:preset.sizes.map(s=>({size:s,bundles:"",pcsPerBundle:""}))}))}
                      className="bg-gray-100 border border-gray-200 text-gray-600 text-xs font-bold px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl active:bg-red-50 active:border-red-300 active:text-red-600 transition">
                      {preset.label}
                    </button>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* Add custom size row */}
              <button onClick={addSizeRow}
                className="mt-1 w-full flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5 bg-gray-50 border border-dashed border-gray-300 text-gray-500 font-bold text-sm py-2.5 rounded-xl active:bg-gray-100 transition">
                <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M12 5v14M5 12h14" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2.2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
                Custom Size जोड़ें
              </button>
            </div>

            <div className="flex gap-3">
              <Btn variant="secondary" className="flex-1" onClick={()=>setShowCutForm(false)}>Cancel</Btn>
              <Btn className="flex-1 bg-red-500 hover:bg-red-600" onClick={handleAddCut}>{cutForm._editId?"Save Changes →":"Add Cutting →"}</Btn>
            </div>
          </div>
        </Modal>
      </div>
    );
  };

  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  // TAB 2: MY TEAM (TAILORS)
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  const TeamTab = () => {
    const byDept = myTeam.reduce((acc,w)=>{ (acc[w.department]||(acc[w.department]=[])).push(w); return acc; },{});
    const [search, setSearch] = useState("");
    const filtered = search ? myTeam.filter(w=>w.name.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase())||w.staffId.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase())) : null;

    if (selectedWorker) {
      const w = myTeam.find(x=>x.id===selectedWorker);
      const wEntries = MOCK_DB.workEntries.filter(e=>e.workerId===selectedWorker);
      const totalAmt = wEntries.reduce((s,e)=>s+e.amount, 0);
      const totalPcs = wEntries.reduce((s,e)=>s+e.pieces, 0);
      const color    = DEPT_COLOR[w.department]||"#64748B";
      return (
        <div className="px-4 pt-4 pb-28 space-y-4">
          <button onClick={()=>setSelectedWorker(null)}
            className="flex items-center gap-1.5 text-blue-500 font-bold text-sm active:opacity-70 transition">
            <svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M19 12H5M5 12l7 7M5 12l7-7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2.2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/></svg>
            My Team पर वापस
          </button>
          {/* Work Entries */}
          <p className="text-xs font-extrabold text-gray-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Work Entries</p>
          {wEntries.length===0 ? (
            <div className="text-center py-12 bg-gray-50 rounded-2xl border border-gray-100">
              <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm">कोई work entry नहीं</p>
            </div>
          ) : (
            <div className="space-y-2">
              {wEntries.map(e=>(
                <div key={e.id} className="bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-2xl px-4 py-3.5 flex items-center gap-3 shadow-sm">
                  <div className="w-9 h-9 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center shrink-0" style={{background:color+"22"}}>
                    <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M9 12l2 2 4-4" stroke={color} strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="9" stroke={color} strokeWidth="1.5"/></svg>
                  </div>
                  <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                    <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-sm truncate">{e.styleName}</p>
                    <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{e.operation} · {e.date}</p>
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-right shrink-0">
                    <p className="text-green-600 font-extrabold text-sm">Rs {e.amount}</p>
                    <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{e.pieces} pcs</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      );
    }

    const listToShow = filtered || [];

    return (
      <div className="px-4 pt-5 pb-28 space-y-4">
        {/* Add Member Button */}
        <button onClick={()=>{setShowAddMember(true);setMemberErr("");setMemberForm({name:"",mobile:"",department:"",staffId:"SG0"+(myTeam.length+2),joinDate:TODAY,address:"",aadhaar:""});}}
          className="w-full bg-blue-500 active:bg-blue-600 text-white font-extrabold text-base py-4 rounded-2xl shadow-md shadow-blue-200 active:scale-[0.98] transition flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
          <svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M16 11c1.66 0 3-1.34 3-3s-1.34-3-3-3M22 21v-1a4 4 0 0 0-3-3.87M1 21v-2a4 4 0 0 1 4-4h4a4 4 0 0 1 4 4v2" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/><circle cx="9" cy="7" r="3" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2"/><path d="M19 8v6M22 11h-6" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
          नया Member जोड़ें
        </button>

        {memberSaved && (
          <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-2xl px-4 py-3 flex items-center gap-2">
            <div className="w-5 h-5 rounded-full bg-green-500 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
              <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 12 12" fill="none"><path d="M2 6l3 3 5-5" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
            </div>
            <p className="text-green-700 text-sm font-semibold">नया member team में add हो गया!</p>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Search */}
        <div className="relative">
          <svg className="absolute left-3.5 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-gray-400" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><circle cx="11" cy="11" r="7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.8"/><path d="M16.5 16.5L21 21" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
          <input value={search} onChange={e=>setSearch(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="Worker नाम या ID से ढूंढें..."
            className="w-full bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-2xl pl-10 pr-4 py-3 text-sm text-gray-900 placeholder-gray-400 focus:outline-none focus:border-blue-400 shadow-sm" style={{fontSize:"16px"}}/>
        </div>

        {/* Worker list or search results */}
        {search ? (
          <div className="space-y-2">
            {listToShow.length===0 ? (
              <div className="text-center py-10 bg-gray-50 rounded-2xl border border-gray-100">
                <p className="text-gray-400">कोई worker नहीं मिला</p>
              </div>
            ) : listToShow.map(w=>(
              <WorkerCard key={w.id} w={w} onClick={()=>setSelectedWorker(w.id)}/>
            ))}
          </div>
        ) : (
          Object.entries(byDept).map(([dept,workers])=>(
            <div key={dept} className="bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-2xl shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 border-b border-gray-50"
                style={{borderLeftWidth:"4px",borderLeftColor:DEPT_COLOR[dept]||"#64748B",borderLeftStyle:"solid"}}>
                <div>
                  <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-sm">{dept}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{workers.length} active tailors</p>
                </div>
                <span className="text-xs font-bold px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full"
                  style={{background:(DEPT_COLOR[dept]||"#64748B")+"22",color:DEPT_COLOR[dept]||"#64748B"}}>
                  {workers.length}
                </span>
              </div>
              <div className="divide-y divide-gray-50">
                {workers.map(w=><WorkerCard key={w.id} w={w} onClick={()=>setSelectedWorker(w.id)}/>)}
              </div>
            </div>
          ))
        )}

        {/* Add Member Modal — ID Lookup */}
        <Modal open={showAddMember} onClose={()=>{setShowAddMember(false);setMemberErr("");setMemberForm({name:"",mobile:"",department:"",staffId:"",joinDate:"",address:"",aadhaar:""});}} title="Worker ID से जोड़ें">
          <AddMemberById
            myTeam={myTeam}
            onAdd={(worker)=>{
              setMyTeam(prev=>[...prev,{...worker,status:"active"}]);
              setShowAddMember(false);
              setMemberSaved(true); setTimeout(()=>setMemberSaved(false),3000);
            }}
            onClose={()=>setShowAddMember(false)}
            TODAY={TODAY}
          />
        </Modal>

        {/* Remove Confirm Modal */}
        {removeConfirm && (() => {
          const w = myTeam.find(x=>x.id===removeConfirm);
          if (!w) return null;
          return (
            <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-end justify-center" style={{background:"rgba(0,0,0,0.5)"}}>
              <div className="bg-white w-full max-w-lg rounded-t-3xl p-6 space-y-4 shadow-2xl">
                <div className="w-12 h-12 bg-red-100 rounded-2xl flex items-center justify-center mx-auto">
                  <svg width="22" height="22" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none">
                    <path d="M3 6h18M8 6V4h8v2M19 6l-1 14H6L5 6" stroke="#EF4444" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
                  </svg>
                </div>
                <div className="text-center">
                  <h3 className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-lg">{w.name} को हटाएं?</h3>
                  <p className="text-gray-500 text-sm mt-1">{w.staffId} · {w.department}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs mt-2">इस worker को आपकी team से remove किया जाएगा।</p>
                </div>
                <div className="flex gap-3">
                  <button onClick={()=>setRemoveConfirm(null)}
                    className="flex-1 bg-gray-100 text-gray-700 font-bold text-sm py-3.5 rounded-2xl active:scale-[0.98] transition">
                    Cancel
                  </button>
                  <button onClick={()=>{
                    setMyTeam(prev=>prev.filter(x=>x.id!==removeConfirm));
                    if (selectedWorker===removeConfirm) setSelectedWorker(null);
                    setRemoveConfirm(null);
                  }}
                    className="flex-1 bg-red-500 text-white font-bold text-sm py-3.5 rounded-2xl shadow-md shadow-red-200 active:scale-[0.98] transition">
                    हाँ, हटाएं
                  </button>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          );
        })()}

      </div>
    );
  };

  const WorkerCard = ({w, onClick}) => (
    <div className="flex items-center group">
      <button onClick={onClick}
        className="flex-1 flex items-center gap-3 px-4 py-3.5 active:bg-gray-50 transition text-left min-w-0">
        <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center font-extrabold text-white text-sm shrink-0"
          style={{background:DEPT_COLOR[w.department]||"#64748B"}}>
          {w.name.charAt(0)}
        </div>
        <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
          <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-sm">{w.name}</p>
          <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{w.staffId} · {w.department}</p>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 shrink-0 mr-2">
          <div className="w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-green-500"/>
          <span className="text-gray-400 text-xs">Active</span>
          <span className="text-gray-300 text-lg ml-1">›</span>
        </div>
      </button>
      {/* Remove button */}
      <button onClick={e=>{e.stopPropagation();setRemoveConfirm(w.id);}}
        className="shrink-0 mr-3 w-8 h-8 rounded-xl bg-red-50 border border-red-200 flex items-center justify-center active:bg-red-100 transition">
        <svg width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none">
          <path d="M17 7l-10 10M7 7l10 10" stroke="#EF4444" strokeWidth="2.2" strokeLinecap="round"/>
        </svg>
      </button>
    </div>
  );

  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  // TAB 3: HOURLY REPORT
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  const HourlyTab = () => {
    // Department locked to supervisor's own dept
    const totalPass   = reports.reduce((s,r)=>s+(+r.pass||0),0);
    const totalAlter  = reports.reduce((s,r)=>s+(+r.alter||0),0);
    const totalReject = reports.reduce((s,r)=>s+(+r.reject||0),0);
    const totalPcs    = reports.reduce((s,r)=>s+(+r.total||0),0);
    const avgPass     = totalPcs ? (totalPass/totalPcs*100).toFixed(1) : 0;

    const addReport = () => {
      const total = +hForm.total, pass = +hForm.pass;
      if (!hForm.department || !hForm.hourSlot || !hForm.total) return;
      setReports(prev=>[...prev,{ ...hForm, id:"h"+Date.now(), passPercent:total?(pass/total*100).toFixed(1):0 }]);
      setHForm({ date:TODAY, department:"", style:"", hourSlot:"", total:"", pass:"", alter:"", reject:"" });
      setShowHForm(false);
    };

    const bySlot = reports.reduce((acc,h)=>{ (acc[h.hourSlot]||(acc[h.hourSlot]=[])).push(h); return acc; },{});

    return (
      <div className="px-4 pt-5 pb-28 space-y-4">
        <button onClick={()=>setShowHForm(true)}
          className="w-full bg-amber-500 active:bg-amber-600 text-white font-extrabold text-base py-4 rounded-2xl shadow-md shadow-amber-200 active:scale-[0.98] transition flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
          <svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M12 5v14M5 12h14" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
          Add Hourly Report
        </button>

        <p className="text-xs font-extrabold text-gray-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Hour-wise Data</p>

        <div className="space-y-3">
          {Object.entries(bySlot).sort().map(([slot,rows])=>{
            const sp   = rows.reduce((s,r)=>s+(+r.pass||0),0);
            const st   = rows.reduce((s,r)=>s+(+r.total||0),0);
            const pct  = st?(sp/st*100).toFixed(1):0;
            const good = +pct>=90;
            return (
              <div key={slot} className="bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-2xl shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
                {/* Slot header */}
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3" style={{background:"#1E293B"}}>
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                    <div className="w-6 h-6 rounded-lg bg-white/10 flex items-center justify-center">
                      <svg width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="8" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8"/><path d="M12 8v4l2.5 2.5" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
                    </div>
                    <span className="text-white font-extrabold text-sm">{slot}</span>
                  </div>
                  <span className={`text-xs font-bold px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full ${good?"bg-green-500 text-white":"bg-red-500 text-white"}`}>
                    {pct}% Pass
                  </span>
                </div>
                {/* Pass bar */}
                <div className="h-1 bg-gray-100">
                  <div className="h-1 transition-all" style={{width:pct+"%", background:good?"#10B981":"#EF4444"}}/>
                </div>
                {/* Dept rows */}
                {rows.map((r,i)=>(
                  <div key={r.id} className={`grid grid-cols-5 px-4 py-3 text-sm items-center gap-2 ${i>0?"border-t border-gray-50":""}`}>
                    <div className="col-span-2">
                      <p className="text-gray-900 font-semibold text-xs">{r.department}</p>
                      <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs truncate">{r.style}</p>
                    </div>
                    <div className="text-center">
                      <p className="text-gray-700 font-bold text-xs">{r.total}</p>
                      <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">Total</p>
                    </div>
                    <div className="text-center">
                      <p className="text-green-600 font-bold text-xs">{r.pass}</p>
                      <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">Pass</p>
                    </div>
                    <div className="text-center">
                      <p className="text-red-500 font-bold text-xs">{r.reject}</p>
                      <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">Rej</p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
            );
          })}
        </div>

        <Modal open={showHForm} onClose={()=>setShowHForm(false)} title="Add Hourly Report">
          <div className="space-y-4">
            <Input label="Date" type="date" value={hForm.date} max={TODAY} onChange={e=>setHForm(f=>({...f,date:e.target.value}))}/>
            <Select label="Department" value={hForm.department} onChange={e=>setHForm(f=>({...f,department:e.target.value}))}>
              <option value="">-- Department --</option>
              {MOCK_DB.departments.map(d=><option key={d.id} value={d.name}>{d.name}</option>)}
            </Select>
            <Select label="Style" value={hForm.style} onChange={e=>setHForm(f=>({...f,style:e.target.value}))}>
              <option value="">-- Style --</option>
              {MOCK_DB.styles.map(s=><option key={s.id} value={s.styleName}>{s.styleName}</option>)}
            </Select>
            <Select label="Hour Slot" value={hForm.hourSlot} onChange={e=>setHForm(f=>({...f,hourSlot:e.target.value}))}>
              <option value="">-- Time Slot चुनें --</option>
              {HOUR_SLOTS.map(s=><option key={s}>{s}</option>)}
            </Select>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
              <Input label="Total" type="number" value={hForm.total} placeholder="0" onChange={e=>setHForm(f=>({...f,total:e.target.value}))}/>
              <Input label="Pass" type="number" value={hForm.pass} placeholder="0" onChange={e=>setHForm(f=>({...f,pass:e.target.value}))}/>
              <Input label="Alter" type="number" value={hForm.alter} placeholder="0" onChange={e=>setHForm(f=>({...f,alter:e.target.value}))}/>
              <Input label="Reject" type="number" value={hForm.reject} placeholder="0" onChange={e=>setHForm(f=>({...f,reject:e.target.value}))}/>
            </div>
            {hForm.total && hForm.pass && (
              <div className="rounded-xl p-3 text-center" style={{background:"linear-gradient(135deg,#F59E0B22,#10B98122)"}}>
                <p className="text-green-700 font-extrabold text-xl">{((+hForm.pass/+hForm.total)*100).toFixed(1)}% Pass Rate</p>
              </div>
            )}
            <div className="flex gap-3">
              <Btn variant="secondary" className="flex-1" onClick={()=>setShowHForm(false)}>Cancel</Btn>
              <Btn className="flex-1 bg-amber-500 hover:bg-amber-600" onClick={addReport}>Submit Report →</Btn>
            </div>
          </div>
        </Modal>
      </div>
    );
  };

  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  // TAB 4: JOBS
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  const JobsTab = () => {
    const active = jobs.filter(j=>j.status==="active");
    return (
      <div className="px-4 pt-5 pb-28 space-y-4">
        <div className="rounded-3xl p-5" style={{background:"linear-gradient(135deg,#1D4ED8,#3B82F6)"}}>
          <p className="text-blue-200 text-xs font-bold uppercase tracking-widest">Available Now</p>
          <p className="text-white text-4xl font-black mt-1">{active.length} Jobs</p>
          <p className="text-blue-200 text-sm mt-1">Sharma Garments Pvt Ltd</p>
        </div>

        <div className="space-y-3">
          {jobs.map(job=>(
            <div key={job.id} className="bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-2xl shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
              <div className="h-1 bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-400 to-cyan-400"/>
              <div className="p-4">
                <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-2 mb-3">
                  <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                    <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold">{job.title}</p>
                    <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs mt-0.5">{job.department}{job.postedDate?" · "+job.postedDate:""}</p>
                  </div>
                  <div className="flex flex-col items-end gap-1 shrink-0">
                    <span className={`text-xs font-bold px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full border ${job.status==="active"?"bg-green-50 text-green-600 border-green-200":"bg-gray-50 text-gray-400 border-gray-200"}`}>
                      {job.status==="active"?"Active":"Closed"}
                    </span>
                    <span className="text-xs text-gray-400">{job.openings} posts</span>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-3">
                  {job.salary && <span className="bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 text-gray-600 text-xs font-semibold px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl">{job.salary}</span>}
                  {job.experience && <span className="bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 text-gray-600 text-xs font-semibold px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl">{job.experience}</span>}
                  {job.applications > 0 && <span className="bg-blue-50 border border-blue-200 text-blue-600 text-xs font-semibold px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl">{job.applications} applied</span>}
                </div>
                {job.description && <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs leading-relaxed">{job.description}</p>}
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  };

  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  // TAB 5: PROFILE
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  const ProfileTab = () => {
    const saveProf = () => { setProf(draft); setEditMode(false); setProfSaved(true); setTimeout(()=>setProfSaved(false),2500); };
    const fld = (label, key, type="text", opts=null) => (
      <div key={key} className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-gray-50 last:border-0">
        <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs font-semibold mb-1">{label}</p>
        {editMode ? (
          opts ? (
            <select value={draft[key]} onChange={e=>setDraft(p=>({...p,[key]:e.target.value}))}
              className="w-full bg-gray-50 border border-orange-300 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 text-gray-900 text-sm font-semibold focus:outline-none" style={{fontSize:"16px"}}>
              {opts.map(o=><option key={o}>{o}</option>)}
            </select>
          ) : (
            <input type={type} value={draft[key]} onChange={e=>setDraft(p=>({...p,[key]:e.target.value}))}
              className="w-full bg-gray-50 border border-orange-300 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 text-gray-900 text-sm font-semibold focus:outline-none" style={{fontSize:"16px"}}/>
          )
        ) : (
          <p className="text-gray-900 text-sm font-bold">{prof[key]||"—"}</p>
        )}
      </div>
    );

    return (
      <><div className="px-4 pt-5 pb-28 space-y-4">
        {profSaved && (
          <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-2xl px-4 py-3 flex items-center gap-2">
            <div className="w-5 h-5 rounded-full bg-green-500 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
              <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 12 12" fill="none"><path d="M2 6l3 3 5-5" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
            </div>
            <p className="text-green-700 text-sm font-semibold">Profile save हो गई!</p>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Avatar hero — dept color based */}
        {/* Stats row */}
        <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-3">
          {[
            { label:"Team",    val:myTeam.length,   color:"text-blue-600",  bg:"bg-blue-50"  },
            { label:"Reports", val:reports.length,  color:"text-amber-600", bg:"bg-amber-50" },
            { label:"Cuts",    val:cuts.length,     color:"text-red-600",   bg:"bg-red-50"   },
          ].map(x=>(
            <div key={x.label} className={`${x.bg} rounded-2xl py-4 text-center`}>
              <p className={"text-2xl font-black "+x.color}>{x.val}</p>
              <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs mt-0.5">{x.label}</p>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* Edit / Save */}
        <div className="flex gap-2">
          {editMode ? (
            <>
              <button onClick={()=>{setEditMode(false);setDraft(prof);}}
                className="flex-1 bg-gray-100 text-gray-700 font-bold text-sm py-3 rounded-2xl active:scale-[0.98] transition">Cancel</button>
              <button onClick={saveProf}
                className="flex-1 bg-orange-500 text-white font-bold text-sm py-3 rounded-2xl shadow-md shadow-orange-200 active:scale-[0.98] transition">Save Changes</button>
            </>
          ) : (
            <button onClick={()=>{setEditMode(true);setDraft(prof);}}
              className="flex-1 flex items-center justify-center gap-2 bg-white border-2 border-orange-400 text-orange-500 font-bold text-sm py-3 rounded-2xl active:scale-[0.98] transition">
              <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M11 4H4a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v14a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h14a2 2 0 0 0 2-2v-7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/><path d="M18.5 2.5a2.12 2.12 0 0 1 3 3L12 15l-4 1 1-4z" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
              Edit Profile
            </button>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* Personal Info */}
        <div className="bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-2xl shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
          <div className="px-4 py-3 bg-gray-50 border-b border-gray-100 flex items-center justify-between">
            <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wider">Personal Info</p>
            {editMode && <span className="text-orange-400 text-xs font-bold">Editing...</span>}
          </div>
          {fld("Full Name",   "name")}
          {fld("Mobile",      "mobile",     "tel")}
          {fld("Email",       "email",      "email")}
          {/* Department — read-only, set by admin */}
          <div className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-gray-50">
            <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs font-semibold mb-1">Department / विभाग</p>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <span className="w-3 h-3 rounded-full shrink-0" style={{background:deptColor}}/>
              <p className="text-gray-900 text-sm font-extrabold">{myDept}</p>
              <span className="text-xs text-gray-400 ml-auto bg-gray-100 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full">Admin assigned</span>
            </div>
          </div>
          {fld("Address",     "address")}
          {fld("Language",    "language",   "text", ["Hindi","English","Hindi + English"])}
        </div>

        {/* Factory Info */}
        <div className="bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-2xl shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
          <div className="px-4 py-3 bg-gray-50 border-b border-gray-100">
            <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wider">Factory Info</p>
          </div>
          {[
            { label:"Factory",       value:user.tenantName||"Sharma Garments" },
            { label:"Team Size",     value:myTeam.length+" tailors"           },
            { label:"Reports Today", value:reports.length+" entries"          },
            { label:"Status",        value:"Active Supervisor"                 },
          ].map(item=>(
            <div key={item.label} className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3.5 border-b border-gray-50 last:border-0">
              <span className="text-gray-500 text-sm">{item.label}</span>
              <span className="text-gray-900 text-sm font-bold">{item.value}</span>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* Jobs Button */}
        <button onClick={()=>setShowJobs(true)}
          className="w-full bg-blue-500 text-white font-extrabold text-sm py-4 rounded-2xl shadow-md shadow-blue-200 active:scale-[0.98] active:bg-blue-600 transition flex items-center justify-center gap-3">
          <svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><rect x="2" y="7" width="20" height="14" rx="2" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2" fill="none"/><path d="M16 7V5a2 2 0 0 0-2-2h-4a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v2M12 12v4M10 14h4" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
          Available Jobs
          <span className="bg-white text-blue-600 text-xs font-black px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full">{jobs.filter(j=>j.status==="active").length}</span>
        </button>

        <button onClick={onLogout}
          className="w-full bg-red-50 border border-red-200 text-red-500 font-bold text-sm py-4 rounded-2xl active:scale-[0.98] transition">
          Sign Out / लॉगआउट
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* Jobs Full Panel */}
      {showJobs && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-gray-50 flex flex-col" style={{fontFamily:"'DM Sans','Segoe UI',sans-serif"}}>
          <div className="bg-white border-b border-gray-100 px-4 py-4 flex items-center gap-3 shadow-sm">
            <button onClick={()=>setShowJobs(false)}
              className="w-9 h-9 rounded-xl bg-gray-100 flex items-center justify-center active:scale-95 transition">
              <svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M15 18l-6-6 6-6" stroke="#374151" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/></svg>
            </button>
            <div>
              <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-base">Available Jobs</p>
              <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{jobs.filter(j=>j.status==="active").length} openings • Sharma Garments</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto px-4 py-4 space-y-3 pb-8">
            <div className="rounded-3xl p-5" style={{background:"linear-gradient(135deg,#1D4ED8,#3B82F6)"}}>
              <p className="text-blue-200 text-xs font-bold uppercase tracking-widest">Hiring Now</p>
              <p className="text-white text-3xl font-black mt-1">{jobs.filter(j=>j.status==="active").length} Jobs Open</p>
              <p className="text-blue-200 text-sm mt-1">Sharma Garments Pvt Ltd</p>
            </div>
            {jobs.map(job=>(
              <div key={job.id} className="bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-2xl shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
                <div className="h-1 bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-400 to-cyan-400"/>
                <div className="p-4">
                  <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-2 mb-2">
                    <div>
                      <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold">{job.title}</p>
                      <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs mt-0.5">{job.department}{job.postedDate?" · "+job.postedDate:""}</p>
                    </div>
                    <span className={`text-xs font-bold px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full border shrink-0 ${job.status==="active"?"bg-green-50 text-green-600 border-green-200":"bg-gray-50 text-gray-400 border-gray-200"}`}>
                      {job.status==="active"?"Active":"Closed"}
                    </span>
                  </div>
                  <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-2">
                    {job.salary && <span className="bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 text-gray-600 text-xs font-semibold px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl">{job.salary}</span>}
                    {job.experience && <span className="bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 text-gray-600 text-xs font-semibold px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl">{job.experience} exp</span>}
                    {job.openings && <span className="bg-blue-50 border border-blue-100 text-blue-600 text-xs font-semibold px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl">{job.openings} posts</span>}
                  </div>
                  {job.description && <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs leading-relaxed">{job.description}</p>}
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </>
    );
  };

  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  // WORK ENTRIES TAB (Approve / Reject)
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  const WorkEntriesTab = () => {
    // 🔗 Use live shared entries from context
    const contextEntries = sharedEntries
      ? sharedEntries.filter(e => perms.canViewAllDepts || e.department === myDept)
      : MOCK_DB.workEntries.map(e=>({...e, status:e.status||"pending"}));
    const [wEntries, setWEntries] = useState(contextEntries);

    // Sync with new entries from shared state
    React.useEffect(() => {
      if (sharedEntries) {
        setWEntries(sharedEntries.filter(e => perms.canViewAllDepts || e.department === myDept));
      }
    }, [sharedEntries?.length]);
    const [filter,      setFilter]      = useState("pending");
    const [selected,    setSelected]    = useState(null);
    const [expandedRow, setExpandedRow] = useState(null);
    const [showAdd,     setShowAdd]     = useState(false);
    const [addErr,      setAddErr]      = useState("");
    const [addSaved,    setAddSaved]    = useState(false);
    // Style Balance — lifted up so approve/reject doesn't reset page
    const [selectedStyleId, setSelectedStyleId] = useState(null);
    const [expandedOpId,    setExpandedOpId]    = useState(null);
    const [historyStyle,    setHistoryStyle]    = useState(null);
    // Cutting form states — must be at top level (no hooks in conditionals)
    const [showCutForm, setShowCutForm] = useState(false);
    const [cutForm,     setCutForm]     = useState({ date:TODAY, styleId:"", marker:"", sizes:[{size:"",bundles:"",pcsPerBundle:""}] });
    const [cutErr,      setCutErr]      = useState("");
    const [cutOk,       setCutOk]       = useState(false);
    const EMPTY_ADD = { workerId:"", date:TODAY, styleId:"", operationId:"", pieces:"", note:"", addCutting:false, cuttingMarker:"", cuttingSizes:[{size:"",bundles:"",pcsPerBundle:""}], selectedCuts:[] };
    const [addForm,  setAddForm]  = useState(EMPTY_ADD);

    const filtered = filter === "all" ? wEntries : wEntries.filter(e => e.status === filter);

    const updateStatus = (id, status) => {
      setWEntries(prev => prev.map(e => e.id === id ? { ...e, status } : e));
      // 🔗 Share status update with worker & admin
      if (sharedActions?.updateEntryStatus) sharedActions.updateEntryStatus(id, status, user.name);
      setSelected(null);
    };

    const pendingCount = wEntries.filter(e => e.status === "pending").length;

    const selWorker   = MOCK_DB.workers.find(w => w.id === addForm.workerId);
    const selStyle    = MOCK_DB.styles.find(s => s.id === addForm.styleId);
    const selOp       = MOCK_DB.operations.find(o => o.id === addForm.operationId);
    const addAmount   = selOp ? (parseFloat(selOp.pieceRate) * (parseInt(addForm.pieces)||0)) : 0;

    // Balance pieces — operation wise (style ki total cutting - is operation mein already used)
    const balancePieces = (() => {
      if (!addForm.styleId || !addForm.operationId) return null;
      // Us style ki saari cutting ka total
      const allStyleCuts = (sharedCuts||cuts||[]).filter(c => c.styleId === addForm.styleId);
      const cuttingTotal = allStyleCuts.reduce((s,c) => s+(+c.totalPieces||0), 0);
      if (cuttingTotal === 0) return null; // koi cutting nahi toh balance nahi dikhao
      // Is operation mein abtak kitne pieces entries hain
      const allEntriesToCheck = [...(sharedEntries||[]), ...wEntries];
      const usedPieces = allEntriesToCheck
        .filter(e => e.styleId===addForm.styleId && e.operationId===addForm.operationId && e.status!=="rejected")
        .reduce((s,e) => s+(+e.pieces||0), 0);
      return { total: cuttingTotal, used: usedPieces, remaining: Math.max(0, cuttingTotal - usedPieces) };
    })();

    const handleAddEntry = () => {
      if (!addForm.workerId)   { setAddErr("Worker चुनें।"); return; }
      if (!addForm.date)       { setAddErr("Date डालें।"); return; }
      if (!addForm.styleId)    { setAddErr("Style चुनें।"); return; }
      if (!addForm.operationId){ setAddErr("Operation चुनें।"); return; }
      if (!addForm.pieces || +addForm.pieces < 1) { setAddErr("Pieces डालें।"); return; }

      // Balance check — pieces balance se zyada nahi honi chahiye
      if (balancePieces !== null && +addForm.pieces > balancePieces.remaining) {
        setAddErr(`⚠️ Pieces (${addForm.pieces}) balance (${balancePieces.remaining}) से ज्यादा हैं! Entry save नहीं होगी।`);
        return;
      }

      // Duplicate check — sharedEntries + wEntries dono check karo
      const allEntries = [...(sharedEntries||[]), ...wEntries];
      const duplicate = allEntries.find(e =>
        e.workerId    === addForm.workerId &&
        e.styleId     === addForm.styleId &&
        e.operationId === addForm.operationId &&
        e.date        === addForm.date &&
        e.status      !== "rejected"
      );
      if (duplicate) {
        setAddErr(`⚠️ ${duplicate.workerName} की इस style+operation में ${addForm.date} को entry पहले से है! (${duplicate.pieces} pcs)`);
        return;
      }
      const w = MOCK_DB.workers.find(x => x.id === addForm.workerId);
      const s = MOCK_DB.styles.find(x => x.id === addForm.styleId);
      const o = MOCK_DB.operations.find(x => x.id === addForm.operationId);
      // Save work entry with selected cutting info
      const selCutsData = (addForm.selectedCuts||[]).map(id => {
        const c = (sharedCuts||cuts||[]).find(x=>x.id===id);
        return c ? { id:c.id, marker:c.marker, totalPieces:c.totalPieces, date:c.date } : null;
      }).filter(Boolean);

      const newEntry = {
        id: "we"+Date.now(),
        workerId:    w.id,        workerName:  w.name,
        staffId:     w.staffId,   department:  w.department,
        styleId:     s.id,        styleName:   s.styleName,
        operationId: o.id,        operation:   o.name,
        date:        addForm.date,
        pieces:      +addForm.pieces,
        pieceRate:   o.pieceRate,
        amount:      addAmount,
        note:        addForm.note,
        status:      "pending",
        addedBy:     "supervisor",
        cuttingRefs: selCutsData,
      };

      setWEntries(prev => [newEntry, ...prev]);
      // sharedEntries mein bhi save — worker panel mein bhi dikhega
      if (sharedActions?.addEntry) sharedActions.addEntry(newEntry);
      setShowAdd(false); setAddErr(""); setAddForm(EMPTY_ADD);
      setAddSaved(true); setTimeout(()=>setAddSaved(false), 2500);
    };

    const statusMeta = {
      pending:  { label:"Pending",  bar:"bg-amber-400",  text:"text-amber-600",  bg:"bg-amber-50",  border:"border-amber-200"  },
      approved: { label:"Approved", bar:"bg-green-500",  text:"text-green-600",  bg:"bg-green-50",  border:"border-green-200"  },
      rejected: { label:"Rejected", bar:"bg-red-400",    text:"text-red-500",    bg:"bg-red-50",    border:"border-red-200"    },
    };

    const selEntry = selected ? wEntries.find(e => e.id === selected) : null;

    return (
      <div className="px-4 pt-5 pb-28 space-y-4">

        {/* Section toggle removed — Style Balance only */}

        {/* ── STYLE BALANCE — All Styles ── */}
        {entriesSection === "balance" && (() => {

          // Build stats for ALL styles
          const allStyleStats = MOCK_DB.styles.map(style => {
            const styleCuts = (sharedCuts || cuts || []).filter(c => c.styleId === style.id);
            const cuttingLimit = styleCuts.reduce((s, c) => s + (+c.totalPieces || 0), 0);
            const limit = cuttingLimit > 0 ? cuttingLimit : style.totalQuantity;
            const styleEntries = wEntries.filter(e => e.styleId === style.id && e.status !== "rejected");
            const done     = styleEntries.reduce((s, e) => s + (e.pieces || 0), 0);
            const pending  = wEntries.filter(e => e.styleId === style.id && e.status === "pending").reduce((s, e) => s + (e.pieces || 0), 0);
            const approved = wEntries.filter(e => e.styleId === style.id && e.status === "approved").reduce((s, e) => s + (e.pieces || 0), 0);
            const balance  = Math.max(0, limit - done);
            const pct      = limit > 0 ? Math.round((done / limit) * 100) : 0;
            const ops = MOCK_DB.operations
              .filter(op => perms.canViewAllDepts || op.department === myDept)
              .map(op => {
                const opDone    = wEntries.filter(e => e.styleId === style.id && e.operationId === op.id && e.status !== "rejected").reduce((s,e)=>s+e.pieces,0);
                const opPending = wEntries.filter(e => e.styleId === style.id && e.operationId === op.id && e.status === "pending").reduce((s,e)=>s+e.pieces,0);
                const opBal     = Math.max(0, limit - opDone);
                const opPct     = limit > 0 ? Math.round((opDone / limit) * 100) : 0;
                return { op, done: opDone, pending: opPending, balance: opBal, pct: opPct };
              });
            const history = [...wEntries].filter(e => e.styleId === style.id).sort((a,b) => new Date(b.date)-new Date(a.date)).slice(0,10);
            return { style, limit, done, pending, approved, balance, pct, ops, history };
          });

          const totalStyles  = allStyleStats.length;
          const activeStyles = allStyleStats.filter(s => s.style.status === "active").length;

          // ── FULL DETAIL PAGE ──
          if (selectedStyleId) {
            const stat = allStyleStats.find(s => s.style.id === selectedStyleId);
            if (!stat) { setSelectedStyleId(null); return null; }
            const { style, limit, done, pending, balance, pct, ops, history } = stat;
            const barColor = pct >= 100 ? "bg-red-400" : pct >= 80 ? "bg-amber-400" : "bg-green-500";

            // Cutting entries for this style
            const styleCuts = (sharedCuts||cuts||[]).filter(c => c.styleId === style.id);
            const cuttingTotal = styleCuts.reduce((s,c)=>s+(+c.totalPieces||0),0);

            const updateSize = (idx, field, val) =>
              setCutForm(f => ({ ...f, sizes: f.sizes.map((r,i)=> i===idx ? {...r,[field]:val} : (idx===0&&(field==="bundles"||field==="pcsPerBundle")?{...r,[field]:val}:r)) }));

            const handleAddCut = () => {
              if (!cutForm.date) { setCutErr("Date डालें।"); return; }
              const validSizes = cutForm.sizes.filter(r=>r.size&&r.bundles&&r.pcsPerBundle);
              if (!validSizes.length) { setCutErr("कम से कम एक size भरें।"); return; }
              const sizesWithTotal = validSizes.map(r=>({...r,bundles:+r.bundles,pcsPerBundle:+r.pcsPerBundle,total:sizeTotal(r)}));
              const totalP = sizesWithTotal.reduce((s,r)=>s+r.total,0);
              const totalL = sizesWithTotal.reduce((s,r)=>s+(+r.bundles||0),0);
              const newCut = { id:"c"+Date.now(), date:cutForm.date, styleId:style.id, style:style.styleName, marker:cutForm.marker, sizes:sizesWithTotal, totalPieces:totalP, totalLayers:totalL, status:"done" };
              setCuts(prev=>[newCut,...prev]);
              if (sharedActions?.addCut) sharedActions.addCut(newCut);
              setCutForm({date:TODAY,styleId:style.id,marker:"",sizes:[{size:"",bundles:"",pcsPerBundle:""}]});
              setCutErr(""); setShowCutForm(false); setCutOk(true);
              setTimeout(()=>setCutOk(false),2500);
            };

            return (
              <div className="space-y-4">
                {/* Back button */}
                <button onClick={() => { setSelectedStyleId(null); setExpandedOpId(null); }}
                  className="flex items-center gap-1.5 text-orange-500 font-extrabold text-sm active:opacity-70 transition">
                  <svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none">
                    <path d="M19 12H5M5 12l7 7M5 12l7-7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2.2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
                  </svg>
                  Style Balance पर वापस
                </button>

                {/* Style header card */}
                <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border-2 border-gray-100 overflow-hidden shadow-sm">
                  <div className={`h-1.5 ${barColor}`}/>
                  <div className="px-4 py-3">
                    <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-2">
                      <div>
                        <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-base">{style.styleName}</p>
                        <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs mt-0.5">{style.styleNumber} · {style.buyer}</p>
                      </div>
                      <span className={`text-[10px] font-extrabold px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full border shrink-0 ${style.status==="active"?"border-green-200 bg-green-50 text-green-600":"border-gray-200 bg-gray-50 text-gray-400"}`}>
                        {style.status}
                      </span>
                    </div>
                    {/* Progress bar */}
                    <div className="mt-3">
                      <div className="flex justify-between text-[10px] mb-1">
                        <span className="text-gray-400">Done: <span className="text-green-600 font-extrabold">{done}</span></span>
                        <span className="text-gray-400">Balance: <span className={`font-extrabold ${balance===0?"text-red-500":"text-orange-500"}`}>{balance}</span></span>
                      </div>
                      <div className="w-full bg-gray-100 rounded-full h-2.5">
                        <div className={`${barColor} h-2.5 rounded-full`} style={{width:`${Math.min(pct,100)}%`}}/>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    {/* Summary pills */}
                    <div className="flex gap-2 mt-2.5 flex-wrap">
                      <span className="bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 text-gray-600 text-[10px] font-bold px-2 py-0.5 rounded-lg">Limit {limit}</span>
                      {pending > 0 && <span className="bg-amber-50 border border-amber-200 text-amber-600 text-[10px] font-bold px-2 py-0.5 rounded-lg">Pend {pending}</span>}
                      {balance === 0 && <span className="bg-red-50 border border-red-200 text-red-500 text-[10px] font-bold px-2 py-0.5 rounded-lg">Full</span>}
                      <span className={`text-[10px] font-black px-2 py-0.5 rounded-lg ${pct>=100?"bg-red-50 text-red-500":pct>=80?"bg-amber-50 text-amber-600":"bg-green-50 text-green-600"}`}>{pct}%</span>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>

                {/* Operation-wise Balance — with accordion */}
                <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border-2 border-gray-100 overflow-hidden shadow-sm">
                  <div className="bg-gray-900 px-4 py-2.5">
                    <p className="text-white text-xs font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wide">Operation-wise Balance</p>
                  </div>
                  {/* Header row */}
                  <div className="grid bg-gray-800 px-3 py-2" style={{gridTemplateColumns:"2fr 0.8fr 0.8fr 0.8fr 0.6fr"}}>
                    {["Operation","QTY","Done","Bal","+"].map((h,i)=>(
                      <div key={h+i} className={`text-[9px] font-extrabold text-gray-300 uppercase ${i>0?"text-right":""}`}>{h}</div>
                    ))}
                  </div>

                  {ops.map((r, idx) => {
                    const rBar = r.balance===0?"bg-red-400":r.pct>=75?"bg-amber-400":"bg-green-400";
                    const opKey = `${style.id}_${r.op.id}`;
                    const isOpExp = expandedOpId === opKey;
                    const opWorkers = wEntries.filter(e => e.styleId===style.id && e.operationId===r.op.id)
                      .sort((a,b)=>new Date(b.date)-new Date(a.date));

                    return (
                      <div key={r.op.id} className={idx%2===0?"bg-white":"bg-gray-50/50"}>
                        <div className="h-0.5 bg-gray-100"><div className={`${rBar} h-0.5`} style={{width:`${r.pct}%`}}/></div>

                        {/* Op row — tap to expand */}
                        <div className="grid px-3 py-2.5 items-center cursor-pointer active:bg-purple-50 transition"
                          style={{gridTemplateColumns:"2fr 0.8fr 0.8fr 0.8fr 0.6fr"}}
                          onClick={()=>setExpandedOpId(isOpExp?null:opKey)}>
                          <div>
                            <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
                              <p className="text-gray-800 font-bold text-xs leading-tight">{r.op.name}</p>
                              <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"
                                className={`text-purple-400 transition-transform duration-200 shrink-0 ${isOpExp?"rotate-180":""}`}>
                                <path d="M6 9l6 6 6-6" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
                              </svg>
                            </div>
                            <p className="text-gray-400 text-[8px]">₹{r.op.pieceRate}/pc{opWorkers.length>0?` · ${opWorkers.length}w`:""}</p>
                          </div>
                          {/* QTY = cutting total only */}
                          <p className="text-red-600 font-bold text-xs text-right">{cuttingTotal>0?cuttingTotal:"—"}</p>
                          {/* Done */}
                          <p className="text-green-600 font-extrabold text-xs text-right">{r.done}</p>
                          {/* BAL */}
                          <p className={`font-extrabold text-xs text-right ${r.balance===0?"text-red-500":r.balance<30?"text-amber-500":"text-blue-600"}`}>{r.balance}</p>
                          <div className="flex justify-end" onClick={ev=>ev.stopPropagation()}>
                            {r.balance>0?(
                              <button onClick={()=>{setAddForm(f=>({...EMPTY_ADD,styleId:style.id,operationId:r.op.id}));setShowAdd(true);}}
                                className="w-7 h-7 rounded-xl bg-green-500 active:scale-90 flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm transition">
                                <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M12 5v14M5 12h14" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
                              </button>
                            ):(
                              <div className="w-7 h-7 rounded-xl bg-red-100 flex items-center justify-center">
                                <svg width="10" height="10" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M18 6L6 18M6 6l12 12" stroke="#EF4444" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
                              </div>
                            )}
                          </div>
                        </div>

                        {/* Accordion: workers on this op */}
                        {isOpExp && (
                          <div className="bg-purple-50 border-t border-purple-100 px-3 py-3 space-y-2">
                            <p className="text-purple-600 text-[9px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wide">🔧 {r.op.name} — सभी Workers</p>
                            {opWorkers.length===0?(
                              <div className="text-center py-3 bg-white rounded-xl border border-purple-100">
                                <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">अभी कोई entry नहीं</p>
                              </div>
                            ):(
                              <>
                                {opWorkers.map((w,wi)=>{
                                  const wS = {approved:{t:"text-green-600",b:"bg-green-50",bo:"border-green-200",l:"Approved"},pending:{t:"text-amber-600",b:"bg-amber-50",bo:"border-amber-200",l:"Pending"},rejected:{t:"text-red-500",b:"bg-red-50",bo:"border-red-200",l:"Rejected"}}[w.status]||{t:"text-amber-600",b:"bg-amber-50",bo:"border-amber-200",l:"Pending"};
                                  return (
                                    <div key={w.id} className="bg-white rounded-xl border border-gray-100 shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
                                      {/* Worker info */}
                                      <div className="flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2.5">
                                        <div className="w-6 h-6 rounded-full bg-purple-500 text-white text-[9px] font-black flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">{wi+1}</div>
                                        <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                                          <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-xs truncate">{w.workerName}</p>
                                          <p className="text-gray-400 text-[8px]">{w.staffId} · {w.date}</p>
                                        </div>
                                        <div className="text-center shrink-0">
                                          <p className="text-orange-500 font-extrabold text-sm leading-none">{w.pieces}</p>
                                          <p className="text-gray-400 text-[8px]">pcs</p>
                                        </div>
                                        <div className="text-right shrink-0">
                                          <p className={`font-extrabold text-xs ${wS.t}`}>₹{(+w.amount||0).toFixed(0)}</p>
                                          <span className={`text-[8px] font-bold px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full border ${wS.b} ${wS.t} ${wS.bo}`}>{wS.l}</span>
                                        </div>
                                      </div>
                                      {/* Action buttons — Pending */}
                                      {w.status==="pending" && perms.canApproveEntries && (
                                        <div className="flex border-t border-gray-100">
                                          <button onClick={()=>{ setWEntries(prev=>prev.map(x=>x.id===w.id?{...x,status:"approved"}:x)); }}
                                            className="flex-1 flex items-center justify-center gap-1 py-2 bg-green-50 active:bg-green-100 border-r border-gray-100 transition">
                                            <svg width="13" height="13" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M5 13l4 4L19 7" stroke="#16a34a" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/></svg>
                                            <span className="text-green-700 font-extrabold text-[10px]">Approve</span>
                                          </button>
                                          <button onClick={()=>setSelected(w.id)}
                                            className="flex-1 flex items-center justify-center gap-1 py-2 bg-blue-50 active:bg-blue-100 border-r border-gray-100 transition">
                                            <svg width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M11 4H4a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v14a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h14a2 2 0 0 0 2-2v-7" stroke="#2563eb" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round" fill="none"/><path d="M18.5 2.5a2.12 2.12 0 0 1 3 3L12 15l-4 1 1-4z" stroke="#2563eb" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round" fill="none"/></svg>
                                            <span className="text-blue-600 font-extrabold text-[10px]">Edit</span>
                                          </button>
                                          <button onClick={()=>{ setWEntries(prev=>prev.map(x=>x.id===w.id?{...x,status:"rejected"}:x)); }}
                                            className="flex-1 flex items-center justify-center gap-1 py-2 bg-red-50 active:bg-red-100 transition">
                                            <svg width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M18 6L6 18M6 6l12 12" stroke="#dc2626" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
                                            <span className="text-red-500 font-extrabold text-[10px]">Reject</span>
                                          </button>
                                        </div>
                                      )}
                                      {/* Approved — undo */}
                                      {w.status==="approved" && (
                                        <div className="flex border-t border-gray-100">
                                          <div className="flex-1 flex items-center justify-center gap-1 py-1.5 bg-green-50">
                                            <span className="text-green-600 font-bold text-[9px]">✓ Approved</span>
                                          </div>
                                          <button onClick={()=>setWEntries(prev=>prev.map(x=>x.id===w.id?{...x,status:"pending"}:x))}
                                            className="px-3 py-1.5 bg-gray-50 active:bg-gray-100 border-l border-gray-100 transition">
                                            <span className="text-gray-500 font-bold text-[9px]">Undo</span>
                                          </button>
                                        </div>
                                      )}
                                    </div>
                                  );
                                })}
                                <div className="flex justify-between bg-purple-100 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 border border-purple-200">
                                  <div>
                                    <p className="text-purple-700 text-[9px] font-extrabold uppercase">Total · {opWorkers.length} workers</p>
                                  </div>
                                  <div className="text-right">
                                    <p className="text-orange-600 font-black text-sm">{opWorkers.reduce((s,x)=>s+(+x.pieces||0),0)} pcs</p>
                                    <p className="text-green-600 font-extrabold text-[10px]">₹{opWorkers.reduce((s,x)=>s+(+x.amount||0),0).toFixed(0)}</p>
                                  </div>
                                </div>
                              </>
                            )}
                          </div>
                        )}
                      </div>
                    );
                  })}
                </div>

                {/* Entry History */}
                <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border-2 border-gray-100 overflow-hidden shadow-sm">
                  <div className="bg-gray-900 px-4 py-2.5">
                    <p className="text-white text-xs font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wide">Entry History</p>
                  </div>
                  {history.length===0?(
                    <div className="text-center py-8"><p className="text-gray-400 text-sm">कोई entry नहीं</p></div>
                  ):(
                    <div className="divide-y divide-gray-50">
                      {history.map(e=>{
                        const sm={approved:"bg-green-50 text-green-600",pending:"bg-amber-50 text-amber-600",rejected:"bg-red-50 text-red-500"};
                        return (
                          <div key={e.id} className="flex items-center gap-3 px-4 py-3">
                            <div className="w-9 h-9 rounded-xl bg-orange-100 flex items-center justify-center text-orange-600 font-extrabold text-sm shrink-0">
                              {(e.workerName||"W").charAt(0)}
                            </div>
                            <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                              <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-xs truncate">{e.workerName}</p>
                              <p className="text-gray-400 text-[9px]">{e.operation} · {e.date}</p>
                            </div>
                            <div className="text-right shrink-0">
                              <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-xs">{e.pieces} pcs</p>
                              <span className={`text-[9px] font-extrabold px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full ${sm[e.status]||sm.pending}`}>{e.status}</span>
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        );
                      })}
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>

              </div>
            );
          }

          // ── STYLE LIST (cards — no arrow, full tap) ──
          return (
            <div className="space-y-3">
              <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2">
                <div className="bg-white border-2 border-gray-100 rounded-2xl p-3 text-center">
                  <p className="text-gray-900 font-black text-xl leading-none">{totalStyles}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs font-semibold mt-0.5">Total Styles</p>
                </div>
                <div className="bg-green-50 border-2 border-green-100 rounded-2xl p-3 text-center">
                  <p className="text-green-600 font-black text-xl leading-none">{activeStyles}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs font-semibold mt-0.5">Active</p>
                </div>
                <div className="bg-orange-50 border-2 border-orange-100 rounded-2xl p-3 text-center">
                  <p className="text-orange-500 font-black text-xl leading-none">{allStyleStats.reduce((s,x)=>s+x.balance,0)}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs font-semibold mt-0.5">Total Balance</p>
                </div>
              </div>

              {allStyleStats.map(({ style, limit, done, pending, balance, pct }) => {
                const barColor = pct>=100?"bg-red-400":pct>=80?"bg-amber-400":"bg-green-500";
                const statusColor = style.status==="active"?"border-green-200 bg-green-50":"border-gray-200 bg-gray-50";
                const statusText  = style.status==="active"?"text-green-600":"text-gray-400";
                return (
                  <button key={style.id}
                    onClick={()=>{ setSelectedStyleId(style.id); setExpandedOpId(null); }}
                    className="w-full text-left bg-white border-2 border-gray-100 rounded-2xl overflow-hidden shadow-sm active:scale-[0.99] active:border-orange-300 transition">
                    <div className={`h-1.5 ${barColor}`}/>
                    <div className="px-4 py-3">
                      <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-2">
                        <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                          <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-sm truncate">{style.styleName}</p>
                          <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs mt-0.5">{style.styleNumber} · {style.buyer}</p>
                        </div>
                        <span className={`text-[10px] font-extrabold px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full border shrink-0 ${statusColor} ${statusText}`}>
                          {style.status}
                        </span>
                      </div>
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mt-3">
                        <div className="flex-1">
                          <div className="flex justify-between text-[10px] mb-1">
                            <span className="text-gray-400">Done: <span className="text-green-600 font-extrabold">{done}</span></span>
                            <span className="text-gray-400">Balance: <span className={`font-extrabold ${balance===0?"text-red-500":"text-orange-500"}`}>{balance}</span></span>
                          </div>
                          <div className="w-full bg-gray-100 rounded-full h-2">
                            <div className={`${barColor} h-2 rounded-full`} style={{width:`${Math.min(pct,100)}%`}}/>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                        <p className={`font-black text-lg shrink-0 ${pct>=100?"text-red-500":pct>=80?"text-amber-500":"text-green-600"}`}>{pct}%</p>
                      </div>
                      <div className="flex gap-2 mt-2.5">
                        <span className="bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 text-gray-600 text-[10px] font-bold px-2 py-0.5 rounded-lg">Limit {limit}</span>
                        {pending>0 && <span className="bg-amber-50 border border-amber-200 text-amber-600 text-[10px] font-bold px-2 py-0.5 rounded-lg">Pend {pending}</span>}
                        {balance===0 && <span className="bg-red-50 border border-red-200 text-red-500 text-[10px] font-bold px-2 py-0.5 rounded-lg">Full</span>}
                        <span className="ml-auto text-[10px] text-orange-400 font-bold">Tap for detail →</span>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </button>
                );
              })}
            </div>
          );
        })()}

        {/* ── WORK ENTRIES — hidden ── */}
        {false && <>
          {addSaved && (
            <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-2xl px-4 py-3 flex items-center gap-2">
              <div className="w-5 h-5 rounded-full bg-green-500 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
                <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 12 12" fill="none"><path d="M2 6l3 3 5-5" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
              </div>
              <p className="text-green-700 text-sm font-semibold">Entry add हो गई — Approved!</p>
            </div>
          )}

          {/* ── Green Add Entry Button ── */}
          {perms.canAddEntries && (
            <button onClick={()=>{ setShowAdd(true); setAddErr(""); setAddForm(EMPTY_ADD); }}
              className="w-full bg-green-500 active:bg-green-600 text-white font-extrabold text-base py-4 rounded-2xl shadow-lg shadow-green-200 active:scale-[0.98] transition flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
              <svg width="22" height="22" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none">
                <path d="M12 5v14M5 12h14" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round"/>
              </svg>
              + Work Entry Add करें
            </button>
          )}

          {/* Filter tabs */}
          <div className="flex bg-gray-100 rounded-2xl p-1 gap-0.5">
            {["pending","approved","rejected","all"].map(f=>(
              <button key={f} onClick={()=>setFilter(f)}
                className={"flex-1 py-2.5 rounded-xl text-xs font-bold transition relative "+(filter===f?"bg-white text-gray-900 shadow-sm":"text-gray-400")}>
                {f==="all"?"All":f.charAt(0).toUpperCase()+f.slice(1)}
                {f==="pending" && pendingCount > 0 && (
                  <span className="absolute -top-1 -right-1 w-4 h-4 bg-amber-400 text-white text-[9px] font-black rounded-full flex items-center justify-center">
                    {pendingCount}
                  </span>
                )}
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>

          {/* Table view */}
          {filtered.length === 0 ? (
            <div className="text-center py-12 bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-100">
              <div className="w-12 h-12 bg-gray-100 rounded-2xl flex items-center justify-center mx-auto mb-3">
                <svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M9 11l3 3L22 4" stroke="#9ca3af" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/><path d="M21 12v7a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V5a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h11" stroke="#9ca3af" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
              </div>
              <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm font-semibold">कोई entry नहीं</p>
            </div>
          ) : (
            <div className="rounded-2xl overflow-hidden border-2 border-gray-100 shadow-sm">
              {/* Table header */}
              <div className="bg-gray-900 grid px-2 py-2.5 text-[9px] font-extrabold text-white uppercase tracking-wider"
                style={{gridTemplateColumns:"1.4fr 1.6fr 1.8fr 1.8fr 0.9fr 1.1fr 0.9fr 0.4fr"}}>
                <div>DATE</div>
                <div>WORKER</div>
                <div>STYLE</div>
                <div>OPERATION</div>
                <div className="text-right">QTY</div>
                <div className="text-right">RATE</div>
                <div className="text-right">AMT</div>
                <div></div>
              </div>

              {/* Rows — Accordion on tap */}
              {filtered.map((e, i) => {
                const m = statusMeta[e.status] || statusMeta.pending;
                const leftBorder = e.status==="approved"?"border-l-green-500":e.status==="rejected"?"border-l-red-400":"border-l-amber-400";
                const isExpanded = expandedRow === e.id;

                // Same operation ke saare workers (current filtered entries mein)
                const sameOpWorkers = wEntries.filter(x =>
                  x.operationId === e.operationId &&
                  x.styleId     === e.styleId &&
                  x.id          !== e.id
                );

                return (
                  <div key={e.id} className={`border-b border-gray-100 last:border-0 ${i%2===0?"bg-white":"bg-gray-50/50"}`}>

                    {/* ── Main Row ── */}
                    <div
                      className={`grid px-2 py-2.5 border-l-4 ${leftBorder} cursor-pointer active:bg-orange-50/50 transition`}
                      style={{gridTemplateColumns:"1.4fr 1.6fr 1.8fr 1.8fr 0.9fr 1.1fr 0.9fr 0.4fr"}}
                      onClick={()=> setExpandedRow(isExpanded ? null : e.id)}>

                      {/* DATE */}
                      <div>
                        <p className="text-gray-800 font-bold text-[10px] leading-tight">{e.date?.slice(5)}</p>
                        <p className="text-gray-400 text-[8px]">{e.date?.slice(0,4)}</p>
                      </div>
                      {/* WORKER */}
                      <div className="min-w-0">
                        <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-[10px] truncate leading-tight">{e.workerName?.split(" ")[0]}</p>
                        <p className="text-gray-400 text-[8px]">{e.staffId}</p>
                      </div>
                      {/* STYLE */}
                      <div className="min-w-0">
                        <p className="text-gray-600 text-[10px] truncate leading-tight">{(e.styleName||e.style||"").replace(/Men's |Women's /g,"")}</p>
                        <p className={`text-[8px] font-bold ${m.text}`}>{m.label}</p>
                      </div>
                      {/* OPERATION */}
                      <div className="min-w-0">
                        <span className={`text-[10px] font-bold truncate block ${m.text==="text-amber-600"?"text-amber-500":"text-blue-600"}`}>{e.operation}</span>
                        {sameOpWorkers.length > 0 && (
                          <span className="text-[8px] text-purple-500 font-bold">+{sameOpWorkers.length} more</span>
                        )}
                      </div>
                      {/* QTY */}
                      <div className="text-right">
                        <p className="text-orange-500 font-extrabold text-sm leading-tight">{e.pieces}</p>
                        <p className="text-gray-400 text-[8px]">pcs</p>
                      </div>
                      {/* RATE */}
                      <div className="text-right">
                        <p className="text-gray-700 font-bold text-[10px]">₹{(+e.pieceRate||0).toFixed(1)}</p>
                        <p className="text-gray-400 text-[8px]">/pc</p>
                      </div>
                      {/* AMOUNT */}
                      <div className="text-right">
                        <p className={`font-extrabold text-sm leading-tight ${e.status==="approved"?"text-green-600":e.status==="rejected"?"text-red-400":"text-amber-600"}`}>
                          ₹{(+e.amount||0).toFixed(0)}
                        </p>
                      </div>
                      {/* Arrow */}
                      <div className="flex items-center justify-end">
                        <svg width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"
                          className={`text-gray-400 transition-transform duration-200 ${isExpanded?"rotate-180":""}`}>
                          <path d="M6 9l6 6 6-6" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2.2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
                        </svg>
                      </div>
                    </div>

                    {/* ── Expanded: Operation-wise all workers ── */}
                    {isExpanded && (
