                      <div className="bg-purple-50 border-t border-purple-100 px-3 py-3">

                        {/* Header */}
                        <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2.5">
                          <div>
                            <p className="text-purple-700 font-extrabold text-xs">
                              🔧 {e.operation} — सभी Workers
                            </p>
                            <p className="text-purple-400 text-[9px] mt-0.5">{e.styleName || e.style}</p>
                          </div>
                          <button onClick={()=>setSelected(e.id)}
                            className="text-[9px] font-bold text-blue-600 bg-white border border-blue-200 rounded-lg px-2 py-1 active:opacity-70">
                            Detail →
                          </button>
                        </div>

                        {/* This entry (current row) */}
                        <div className="space-y-1.5">
                          {/* Current worker row */}
                          {[e, ...sameOpWorkers].map((w, wi) => {
                            const wm = statusMeta[w.status] || statusMeta.pending;
                            const isThis = w.id === e.id;
                            return (
                              <div key={w.id}
                                className={`flex items-center gap-2 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 border ${isThis ? "bg-white border-purple-200 shadow-sm" : "bg-white/70 border-gray-100"}`}>
                                {/* Rank number */}
                                <div className={`w-5 h-5 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center text-[9px] font-black shrink-0 ${isThis?"bg-purple-500 text-white":"bg-gray-200 text-gray-600"}`}>
                                  {wi+1}
                                </div>
                                {/* Worker info */}
                                <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                                  <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
                                    <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-xs truncate">{w.workerName}</p>
                                    {isThis && <span className="text-[8px] bg-purple-100 text-purple-600 font-bold px-1 rounded">This</span>}
                                  </div>
                                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-[9px]">{w.staffId} · {w.date}</p>
                                </div>
                                {/* Pieces */}
                                <div className="text-center shrink-0">
                                  <p className="text-orange-500 font-extrabold text-sm leading-none">{w.pieces}</p>
                                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-[8px]">pcs</p>
                                </div>
                                {/* Amount */}
                                <div className="text-right shrink-0">
                                  <p className={`font-extrabold text-xs leading-none ${w.status==="approved"?"text-green-600":w.status==="rejected"?"text-red-400":"text-amber-600"}`}>
                                    ₹{(+w.amount||0).toFixed(0)}
                                  </p>
                                  <span className={`text-[8px] font-bold px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full ${wm.bg} ${wm.text} border ${wm.border}`}>
                                    {wm.label}
                                  </span>
                                </div>
                              </div>
                            );
                          })}
                        </div>

                        {/* Operation total */}
                        {(() => {
                          const allOpEntries = [e, ...sameOpWorkers];
                          const totalPcs = allOpEntries.reduce((s,x)=>s+(+x.pieces||0),0);
                          const totalAmt = allOpEntries.reduce((s,x)=>s+(+x.amount||0),0);
                          const approvedPcs = allOpEntries.filter(x=>x.status==="approved").reduce((s,x)=>s+(+x.pieces||0),0);
                          return (
                            <div className="mt-2 flex items-center justify-between bg-purple-100 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 border border-purple-200">
                              <div>
                                <p className="text-purple-700 text-[9px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wide">Operation Total</p>
                                <p className="text-purple-500 text-[8px]">{allOpEntries.length} workers · {approvedPcs} approved pcs</p>
                              </div>
                              <div className="text-right">
                                <p className="text-orange-600 font-black text-sm leading-none">{totalPcs} pcs</p>
                                <p className="text-green-600 font-extrabold text-xs">₹{totalAmt.toFixed(0)}</p>
                              </div>
                            </div>
                          );
                        })()}
                      </div>
                    )}
                  </div>
                );
              })}

              {/* Footer total row */}
              <div className="bg-gray-900 grid px-2 py-2.5 text-[9px] font-extrabold"
                style={{gridTemplateColumns:"1.4fr 1.6fr 1.8fr 1.8fr 0.9fr 1.1fr 0.9fr 0.4fr"}}>
                <div className="text-gray-400">{filtered.length} rows</div>
                <div className="col-span-3 text-gray-300 uppercase tracking-wide">TOTAL</div>
                <div className="text-orange-400 text-right text-sm font-black">
                  {filtered.reduce((s,e)=>s+(+e.pieces||0),0)}
                </div>
                <div></div>
                <div className="text-green-400 text-right text-sm font-black">
                  ₹{filtered.reduce((s,e)=>s+(+e.amount||0),0).toFixed(0)}
                </div>
                <div></div>
              </div>
            </div>
          )}
        </>}

        {/* ── CUTTING ENTRIES ── */}
        {entriesSection === "team" && (() => {
          const [tmSearch, setTmSearch] = React.useState("");
          const [tmSelWorker, setTmSelWorker] = React.useState(null);
          const DEPT_C = { Stitching:"#3B82F6", Finishing:"#10B981", QC:"#F59E0B", Cutting:"#EF4444", Embroidery:"#8B5CF6" };
          const byDept = myTeam.reduce((acc,w)=>{ (acc[w.department]||(acc[w.department]=[])).push(w); return acc; },{});
          const filteredTm = tmSearch ? myTeam.filter(w=>w.name.toLowerCase().includes(tmSearch.toLowerCase())||w.staffId.toLowerCase().includes(tmSearch.toLowerCase())) : null;

          if (tmSelWorker) {
            const w = myTeam.find(x=>x.id===tmSelWorker);
            const wEnt = [...(sharedEntries||[]), ...wEntries].filter(e=>e.workerId===w.id);
            const tAmt = wEnt.reduce((s,e)=>s+(e.amount||0),0);
            const tPcs = wEnt.reduce((s,e)=>s+(e.pieces||0),0);
            const col  = DEPT_C[w.department]||"#64748B";
            return (
              <div className="space-y-4">
                <button onClick={()=>setTmSelWorker(null)}
                  className="flex items-center gap-1.5 text-blue-500 font-bold text-sm">
                  <svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M19 12H5M5 12l7 7M5 12l7-7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2.2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/></svg>
                  My Team पर वापस
                </button>
                {/* Worker info card */}
                <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-100 shadow-sm p-4">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-3">
                    <div className="w-12 h-12 rounded-2xl flex items-center justify-center text-white font-extrabold text-lg shrink-0" style={{background:col}}>
                      {w.name.charAt(0)}
                    </div>
                    <div className="flex-1">
                      <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-base">{w.name}</p>
                      <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{w.staffId} · {w.department}</p>
                      <p className="text-gray-300 text-xs">Joined {w.joinDate}</p>
                    </div>
                    <span className={`text-xs font-bold px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full border ${w.status==="active"?"bg-green-50 text-green-600 border-green-200":"bg-gray-50 text-gray-400 border-gray-200"}`}>
                      {w.status==="active"?"Active":"Inactive"}
                    </span>
                  </div>
                  <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2">
                    {[
                      {label:"Total Pcs", val:tPcs, color:"text-blue-600", bg:"bg-blue-50"},
                      {label:"Earnings",  val:"₹"+Math.round(tAmt), color:"text-green-600", bg:"bg-green-50"},
                      {label:"Entries",   val:wEnt.length, color:"text-orange-600", bg:"bg-orange-50"},
                    ].map(x=>(
                      <div key={x.label} className={`${x.bg} rounded-xl py-2.5 text-center`}>
                        <p className={"font-extrabold text-sm "+x.color}>{x.val}</p>
                        <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs mt-0.5">{x.label}</p>
                      </div>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                </div>
                {/* Entries list */}
                <p className="text-xs font-extrabold text-gray-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Work Entries</p>
                {wEnt.length===0 ? (
                  <div className="text-center py-10 bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-100">
                    <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm">कोई entry नहीं</p>
                  </div>
                ) : (
                  <div className="space-y-2">
                    {wEnt.slice(0,20).map(e=>(
                      <div key={e.id} className="bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-2xl px-4 py-3 flex items-center gap-3 shadow-sm">
                        <div className="w-9 h-9 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center shrink-0" style={{background:col+"22"}}>
                          <svg width="15" height="15" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M9 12l2 2 4-4" stroke={col} strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="9" stroke={col} strokeWidth="1.5"/></svg>
                        </div>
                        <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                          <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-sm truncate">{e.styleName||e.style}</p>
                          <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{e.operation} · {e.date}</p>
                        </div>
                        <div className="text-right shrink-0">
                          <p className="text-green-600 font-extrabold text-sm">₹{Math.round(e.amount||0)}</p>
                          <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{e.pieces} pcs</p>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            );
          }

          return (
            <div className="space-y-3">
              {/* Search + Add button */}
              <div className="flex gap-2">
                <div className="flex-1 relative">
                  <svg className="absolute left-3.5 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-gray-400" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><circle cx="11" cy="11" r="7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.8"/><path d="M16.5 16.5L21 21" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
                  <input value={tmSearch} onChange={e=>setTmSearch(e.target.value)}
                    placeholder="Worker नाम या ID से ढूंढें..."
                    className="w-full bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-2xl pl-10 pr-4 py-3 text-sm text-gray-900 focus:outline-none focus:border-blue-400 shadow-sm" style={{fontSize:"16px"}}/>
                </div>
                <button onClick={()=>setShowAddMember(true)}
                  className="w-12 h-12 bg-blue-500 hover:bg-blue-600 active:scale-90 text-white rounded-2xl flex items-center justify-center shadow-md shadow-blue-200 shrink-0 transition-all">
                  <svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M12 5v14M5 12h14" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
                </button>
              </div>

              {/* Add Member Modal */}
              <Modal open={showAddMember} onClose={()=>setShowAddMember(false)} title="Worker ID से जोड़ें">
                <AddMemberById
                  myTeam={myTeam}
                  onAdd={(worker)=>{ setMyTeam(prev=>[...prev,{...worker,status:"active"}]); setShowAddMember(false); }}
                  onClose={()=>setShowAddMember(false)}
                  TODAY={TODAY}
                />
              </Modal>
              {/* List */}
              {tmSearch ? (
                <div className="space-y-2">
                  {(filteredTm||[]).length===0 ? (
                    <div className="text-center py-10 bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-100">
                      <p className="text-gray-400">कोई worker नहीं मिला</p>
                    </div>
                  ) : (filteredTm||[]).map(w=>(
                    <button key={w.id} onClick={()=>setTmSelWorker(w.id)} className="w-full text-left">
                      <WorkerCard w={w} onClick={()=>setTmSelWorker(w.id)}/>
                    </button>
                  ))}
                </div>
              ) : (
                Object.entries(byDept).map(([dept,workers])=>(
                  <div key={dept} className="bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-2xl shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
                    <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 border-b border-gray-50"
                      style={{borderLeftWidth:"4px",borderLeftColor:DEPT_C[dept]||"#64748B",borderLeftStyle:"solid"}}>
                      <div>
                        <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-sm">{dept}</p>
                        <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{workers.length} workers</p>
                      </div>
                      <span className="text-xs font-bold px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full"
                        style={{background:(DEPT_C[dept]||"#64748B")+"22",color:DEPT_C[dept]||"#64748B"}}>
                        {workers.length}
                      </span>
                    </div>
                    <div className="divide-y divide-gray-50">
                      {workers.map(w=>(
                        <button key={w.id} onClick={()=>setTmSelWorker(w.id)} className="w-full text-left">
                          <WorkerCard w={w} onClick={()=>setTmSelWorker(w.id)}/>
                        </button>
                      ))}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))
              )}
            </div>
          );
        })()}

        {/* Detail / Action bottom sheet */}
        {/* Add Entry Modal */}
        <Modal open={showAdd} onClose={()=>setShowAdd(false)} title="नई Work Entry जोड़ें">
          <div className="space-y-4">
            {addErr && <div className="bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-xl p-3 text-red-600 text-sm">{addErr}</div>}

            {/* Worker select — prominent */}
            <div>
              <p className="text-sm font-bold text-gray-800 mb-1.5">Worker <span className="text-red-500">*</span></p>
              <select value={addForm.workerId}
                onChange={e=>setAddForm(f=>({...f,workerId:e.target.value}))}
                className={"w-full border-2 rounded-2xl px-4 py-3.5 font-bold focus:outline-none transition "+(addForm.workerId?"bg-green-50 border-green-400 text-green-800":"bg-gray-50 border-gray-200 text-gray-500")}
                style={{fontSize:"16px"}}>
                <option value="">-- Worker चुनें --</option>
                {myTeam.filter(w=>w.status==="active" && (perms.canViewAllDepts || w.department===myDept)).map(w=>(
                  <option key={w.id} value={w.id}>{w.name} ({w.staffId})</option>
                ))}
              </select>
              {addForm.workerId && selWorker && (
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mt-2 bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-xl px-3 py-2">
                  <div className="w-7 h-7 rounded-lg bg-green-500 flex items-center justify-center text-white font-extrabold text-xs shrink-0">
                    {selWorker.name.charAt(0)}
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    <p className="text-green-800 font-extrabold text-sm">{selWorker.name}</p>
                    <p className="text-green-500 text-xs">{selWorker.staffId} · {selWorker.department}</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>

            <Input label="Date" type="date" value={addForm.date} max={TODAY}
              onChange={e=>setAddForm(f=>({...f,date:e.target.value}))}/>

            <Select label="Style / Order" value={addForm.styleId}
              onChange={e=>setAddForm(f=>({...f,styleId:e.target.value,selectedCuts:[]}))}>
              <option value="">-- Style चुनें --</option>
              {MOCK_DB.styles.filter(s=>s.status==="active").map(s=>(
                <option key={s.id} value={s.id}>{s.styleName}</option>
              ))}
            </Select>

            {/* ── Cutting Cards — sirf UNLOCKED cuts dikhenge ── */}
            {addForm.styleId && (() => {
              const allCuts = (sharedCuts||cuts||[]);
              const styleCuts = allCuts.filter(c => c.styleId === addForm.styleId);
              // Sirf UNLOCKED cuts (lockedCuts mein false/undefined = open)
              const openCuts = styleCuts.filter(c => !lockedCuts[c.id]);
              if (styleCuts.length === 0) return null;
              if (openCuts.length === 0) return (
                <div className="bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-2xl px-4 py-4 flex items-start gap-3">
                  <svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" className="shrink-0 mt-0.5">
                    <rect x="3" y="11" width="18" height="11" rx="2" stroke="#EF4444" strokeWidth="2"/>
                    <path d="M7 11V7a5 5 0 0 1 10 0v4" stroke="#EF4444" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/>
                  </svg>
                  <div>
                    <p className="text-red-700 font-extrabold text-sm">सभी Cutting Records 🔒 Locked हैं</p>
                    <p className="text-red-400 text-xs mt-0.5">Cutting tab में जाकर पहले lock खोलें, तभी work entry हो सकती है।</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
              );
              const selCuts = addForm.selectedCuts || [];
              const totalSelPcs = openCuts
                .filter(c => selCuts.includes(c.id))
                .reduce((s,c) => s + (+c.totalPieces||0), 0);
              return (
                <div className="space-y-2">
                  <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                    <p className="text-xs font-extrabold text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wide">✂️ Cutting Records — Select करें</p>
                    {selCuts.length > 0 && (
                      <span className="text-xs font-bold bg-orange-50 text-orange-600 border border-orange-200 px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full">
                        {selCuts.length} selected · {totalSelPcs} pcs
                      </span>
                    )}
                  </div>
                  <div className="space-y-2">
                    {openCuts.map(c => {
                      const isSel = selCuts.includes(c.id);
                      return (
                        <button key={c.id} type="button"
                          onClick={() => setAddForm(f => {
                            const newSel = isSel
                              ? (f.selectedCuts||[]).filter(id=>id!==c.id)
                              : [...(f.selectedCuts||[]), c.id];
                            // Auto-calculate total pieces from selected cuts
                            const allCutsRef = (sharedCuts||cuts||[]);
                            const totalPcs = allCutsRef
                              .filter(x => newSel.includes(x.id))
                              .reduce((s,x) => s+(+x.totalPieces||0), 0);
                            return { ...f, selectedCuts: newSel, pieces: totalPcs > 0 ? String(totalPcs) : f.pieces };
                          })}
                          className={`w-full text-left rounded-2xl border-2 p-3 transition-all active:scale-[0.98] ${
                            isSel
                              ? "border-orange-400 bg-orange-50 shadow-md shadow-orange-100"
                              : "border-gray-200 bg-white hover:border-orange-200"
                          }`}>
                          <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                            {/* Checkbox */}
                            <div className={`w-6 h-6 rounded-lg border-2 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 transition-all ${
                              isSel ? "bg-orange-500 border-orange-500" : "border-gray-300 bg-white"
                            }`}>
                              {isSel && <svg width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M5 13l4 4L19 7" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/></svg>}
                            </div>
                            {/* Cutting No + date */}
                            <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                              <p className={`font-extrabold text-sm ${isSel ? "text-orange-700" : "text-gray-800"}`}>
                                {c.marker ? `Cut No: ${c.marker}` : `Cut #${c.id.slice(-4)}`}
                              </p>
                              <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs mt-0.5">{c.date}</p>
                            </div>
                            {/* Quantity only */}
                            <div className="text-right shrink-0">
                              <p className={`font-black text-xl ${isSel ? "text-orange-600" : "text-gray-700"}`}>{c.totalPieces}</p>
                              <p className="text-gray-400 text-[10px]">pieces</p>
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        </button>
                      );
                    })}
                  </div>
                  {selCuts.length > 0 && (
                    <div className="bg-orange-50 border-2 border-orange-200 rounded-xl px-4 py-2.5 flex items-center justify-between">
                      <p className="text-orange-700 text-xs font-bold">Selected Cutting Total</p>
                      <p className="text-orange-600 font-black text-base">{totalSelPcs} pcs</p>
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>
              );
            })()}

            <Select label="Operation" value={addForm.operationId}
              onChange={e=>setAddForm(f=>({...f,operationId:e.target.value}))}>
              <option value="">-- Operation चुनें --</option>
              {MOCK_DB.operations.map(o=>(
                <option key={o.id} value={o.id}>{o.name} — Rs {o.pieceRate}/pc</option>
              ))}
            </Select>

            <Input label="Pieces" type="number" min="1" value={addForm.pieces} placeholder="कितने pieces?"
              onChange={e=>setAddForm(f=>({...f,pieces:e.target.value}))}/>

            {/* Balance pieces indicator */}
            {balancePieces !== null && (
              <div className={`rounded-xl border-2 overflow-hidden ${
                balancePieces.remaining === 0 ? "border-red-200" :
                (+addForm.pieces||0) > balancePieces.remaining ? "border-red-200" :
                "border-blue-200"
              }`}>
                <div className="grid grid-cols-3 divide-x divide-gray-100">
                  <div className="px-3 py-2.5 text-center bg-gray-50">
                    <p className="text-gray-400 text-[10px] font-bold uppercase">Total Cut</p>
                    <p className="text-gray-800 font-black text-base">{balancePieces.total}</p>
                  </div>
                  <div className="px-3 py-2.5 text-center bg-gray-50">
                    <p className="text-gray-400 text-[10px] font-bold uppercase">Used</p>
                    <p className="text-orange-600 font-black text-base">{balancePieces.used}</p>
                  </div>
                  <div className={`px-3 py-2.5 text-center ${balancePieces.remaining === 0 || (+addForm.pieces||0) > balancePieces.remaining ? "bg-red-50" : "bg-blue-50"}`}>
                    <p className={`text-[10px] font-bold uppercase ${balancePieces.remaining === 0 || (+addForm.pieces||0) > balancePieces.remaining ? "text-red-400" : "text-blue-400"}`}>Balance</p>
                    <p className={`font-black text-base ${balancePieces.remaining === 0 || (+addForm.pieces||0) > balancePieces.remaining ? "text-red-600" : "text-blue-600"}`}>
                      {Math.max(0, balancePieces.remaining - (+addForm.pieces||0))}
                    </p>
                  </div>
                </div>
                {(+addForm.pieces||0) > balancePieces.remaining && (
                  <div className="bg-red-50 px-3 py-1.5 border-t border-red-100">
                    <p className="text-red-500 text-xs font-bold text-center">⚠️ Pieces balance से ज्यादा हैं!</p>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            )}

            {addAmount > 0 && (
              <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-100 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 flex items-center justify-between">
                <div>
                  <p className="text-green-700 font-extrabold text-xl">Rs {addAmount.toFixed(2)}</p>
                  <p className="text-green-400 text-xs">{addForm.pieces} pcs × Rs {selOp?.pieceRate}/pc</p>
                </div>
                {selWorker && (
                  <div className="text-right">
                    <p className="text-green-700 font-bold text-sm">{selWorker.name}</p>
                    <p className="text-green-400 text-xs">{selWorker.staffId}</p>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            )}

            <Input label="Note (optional)" value={addForm.note} placeholder="कोई comment?"
              onChange={e=>setAddForm(f=>({...f,note:e.target.value}))}/>

            <div className="flex gap-3">
              <Btn variant="secondary" className="flex-1" onClick={()=>setShowAdd(false)}>Cancel</Btn>
              <Btn className="flex-1 bg-green-600 hover:bg-green-700" onClick={handleAddEntry}>
                Add Entry →
              </Btn>
            </div>
          </div>
        </Modal>

        {selEntry && (() => {
          const m = statusMeta[selEntry.status] || statusMeta.pending;
          // Edit state inside IIFE using ref trick — avoids hooks-in-function issue
          return (
            <EntryDetailSheet
              selEntry={selEntry}
              m={m}
              onClose={()=>setSelected(null)}
              onStatus={updateStatus}
              allWEntries={wEntries}
              onSave={(id, updated) => {
                const op = MOCK_DB.operations.find(o => o.id === updated.operationId);
                const newPieceRate = op?.pieceRate || selEntry.pieceRate;
                const newAmount = (parseInt(updated.pieces)||0) * newPieceRate;
                setWEntries(prev => prev.map(e => e.id === id ? {
                  ...e,
                  pieces: parseInt(updated.pieces),
                  date: updated.date,
                  operationId: updated.operationId,
                  operation: op?.name || e.operation,
                  pieceRate: newPieceRate,
                  amount: newAmount,
                  note: updated.note,
                } : e));
                setSelected(null);
              }}
              workers={MOCK_DB.workers}
              operations={MOCK_DB.operations}
              styles={MOCK_DB.styles}
            />
          );
        })()}
      </div>
    );
  };


  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  // TAB: ATTENDANCE
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════

  // ── Monthly History Sub-view ──
  const MonthlyAttendanceHistory = () => {
    const now = new Date();
    const currentMonthStr = `${now.getFullYear()}-${String(now.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, "0")}`;
    const [selMonth, setSelMonth] = useState(currentMonthStr);
    const [selWorker, setSelWorker] = useState(myTeam[0]?.id || "");

    const [yr, mn] = selMonth.split("-").map(Number);
    const daysInMonth = new Date(yr, mn, 0).getDate();
    const firstDay = new Date(yr, mn - 1, 1).getDay(); // 0=Sun
    const monthLabel = new Date(yr, mn - 1, 1).toLocaleString("default", { month: "long", year: "numeric" });

    const key = `${selWorker}_${selMonth}`;
    const history = MOCK_ATTENDANCE_HISTORY[key] || {};

    // counts
    const counts = { present: 0, absent: 0, leave: 0, half: 0, holiday: 0, none: 0 };
    for (let d = 1; d <= daysInMonth; d++) {
      const ds = `${selMonth}-${String(d).padStart(2, "0")}`;
      const st = history[ds] || "none";
      counts[st] = (counts[st] || 0) + 1;
    }
    const workingDays = daysInMonth - counts.holiday - counts.none;
    const attendRate = workingDays > 0
      ? Math.round(((counts.present + counts.half * 0.5) / workingDays) * 100)
      : 0;

    const goPrev = () => {
      const d = new Date(yr, mn - 2, 1);
      setSelMonth(`${d.getFullYear()}-${String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, "0")}`);
    };
    const goNext = () => {
      const d = new Date(yr, mn, 1);
      const nm = `${d.getFullYear()}-${String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, "0")}`;
      if (nm <= currentMonthStr) setSelMonth(nm);
    };
    const canGoNext = selMonth < currentMonthStr;

    const STATUS = {
      present: { bg: "bg-green-500",  text: "text-white",     label: "P"  },
      absent:  { bg: "bg-red-400",    text: "text-white",     label: "A"  },
      leave:   { bg: "bg-blue-400",   text: "text-white",     label: "L"  },
      half:    { bg: "bg-amber-400",  text: "text-white",     label: "H"  },
      holiday: { bg: "bg-gray-100",   text: "text-gray-400",  label: "–"  },
      none:    { bg: "bg-gray-50",    text: "text-gray-200",  label: " "  },
    };

    // Team overview sorted by rate
    const teamSummary = myTeam.map(w => {
      const wKey = `${w.id}_${selMonth}`;
      const wHist = MOCK_ATTENDANCE_HISTORY[wKey] || {};
      const wC = { present:0, absent:0, leave:0, half:0, holiday:0, none:0 };
      for (let d = 1; d <= daysInMonth; d++) {
        const ds = `${selMonth}-${String(d).padStart(2,"0")}`;
        const st = wHist[ds] || "none";
        wC[st] = (wC[st]||0)+1;
      }
      const wWork = daysInMonth - wC.holiday - wC.none;
      const wRate = wWork > 0 ? Math.round(((wC.present + wC.half * 0.5) / wWork) * 100) : 0;
      return { ...w, ...wC, workingDays: wWork, rate: wRate };
    }).sort((a, b) => b.rate - a.rate);

    return (
      <div className="px-4 pt-4 pb-28 space-y-4">

        {/* Month Navigator */}
        <div className="bg-white border-2 border-green-100 rounded-2xl p-4 space-y-3">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
            <button onClick={goPrev}
              className="w-9 h-9 rounded-xl bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 flex items-center justify-center text-gray-600 active:scale-95 transition">
              <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none">
                <path d="M15 18l-6-6 6-6" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2.2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
              </svg>
            </button>
            <div className="text-center">
              <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-base">{monthLabel}</p>
              <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs mt-0.5">Monthly Attendance</p>
            </div>
            <button onClick={goNext} disabled={!canGoNext}
              className={`w-9 h-9 rounded-xl border flex items-center justify-center active:scale-95 transition
                ${canGoNext ? "bg-gray-50 border-gray-200 text-gray-600" : "bg-gray-50 border-gray-100 text-gray-300 cursor-not-allowed"}`}>
              <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none">
                <path d="M9 18l6-6-6-6" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2.2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
              </svg>
            </button>
          </div>

          {/* Worker dropdown */}
          <select value={selWorker} onChange={e => setSelWorker(e.target.value)}
            className="w-full bg-gray-50 border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-3 py-2.5 text-sm font-bold text-gray-800 focus:outline-none focus:border-green-400"
            style={{ fontSize: "15px" }}>
            {myTeam.map(w => (
              <option key={w.id} value={w.id}>{w.name} — {w.staffId}</option>
            ))}
          </select>
        </div>

        {/* Attendance Rate + Stats */}
        <div className="bg-white border-2 border-green-100 rounded-2xl p-4 flex items-center gap-4">
          {/* Circular progress */}
          <div className="relative w-20 h-20 shrink-0">
            <svg viewBox="0 0 36 36" className="w-full h-full -rotate-90">
              <circle cx="18" cy="18" r="14" fill="none" stroke="#f1f5f9" strokeWidth="3.5"/>
              <circle cx="18" cy="18" r="14" fill="none"
                stroke={attendRate >= 90 ? "#10b981" : attendRate >= 75 ? "#f59e0b" : "#ef4444"}
                strokeWidth="3.5"
                strokeDasharray={`${(attendRate / 100) * 87.96} 87.96`}
                strokeLinecap="round"/>
            </svg>
            <div className="absolute inset-0 flex flex-col items-center justify-center">
              <span className="text-sm font-black text-gray-800">{attendRate}%</span>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div className="flex-1">
            <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-base leading-none">Attendance Rate</p>
            <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs mt-1">{workingDays} working days this month</p>
            <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mt-2.5">
              <span className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 text-green-700 text-xs font-bold px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full">{counts.present} Present</span>
              <span className="bg-red-50 border border-red-200 text-red-500 text-xs font-bold px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full">{counts.absent} Absent</span>
              <span className="bg-blue-50 border border-blue-200 text-blue-600 text-xs font-bold px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full">{counts.leave} Leave</span>
              <span className="bg-amber-50 border border-amber-200 text-amber-600 text-xs font-bold px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full">{counts.half} Half</span>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Legend */}
        <div className="flex gap-3 flex-wrap px-1">
          {[
            { label: "Present", dot: "bg-green-500" },
            { label: "Absent",  dot: "bg-red-400"   },
            { label: "Leave",   dot: "bg-blue-400"  },
            { label: "Half Day",dot: "bg-amber-400" },
            { label: "Holiday", dot: "bg-gray-300"  },
          ].map(l => (
            <div key={l.label} className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
              <div className={`w-2.5 h-2.5 rounded-full ${l.dot}`}/>
              <span className="text-gray-500 text-xs font-semibold">{l.label}</span>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* Calendar Grid */}
        <div className="bg-white border-2 border-gray-100 rounded-2xl overflow-hidden shadow-sm">
          <div className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-gray-100 flex items-center justify-between">
            <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-sm">Calendar View</p>
            <span className="text-gray-400 text-xs font-semibold">{daysInMonth} days</span>
          </div>
          {/* Day headers */}
          <div className="grid grid-cols-7 px-2 pt-3 pb-1">
            {["S","M","T","W","T","F","S"].map((d, i) => (
              <div key={i} className={`text-center text-[11px] font-extrabold uppercase py-1
                ${i === 0 ? "text-red-400" : "text-gray-400"}`}>{d}</div>
            ))}
          </div>
          {/* Date cells */}
          <div className="grid grid-cols-7 gap-1 px-2 pb-3">
            {Array.from({ length: firstDay }).map((_, i) => <div key={`e${i}`} />)}
            {Array.from({ length: daysInMonth }).map((_, i) => {
              const day = i + 1;
              const ds = `${selMonth}-${String(day).padStart(2, "0")}`;
              const st = history[ds] || "none";
              const cfg = STATUS[st] || STATUS.none;
              const isToday = ds === new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0];
              return (
                <div key={day}
                  className={`aspect-square rounded-xl flex flex-col items-center justify-center
                    ${cfg.bg} ${isToday ? "ring-2 ring-orange-400 ring-offset-1" : ""} transition`}>
                  <span className={`text-[11px] font-black leading-none ${cfg.text}`}>{day}</span>
                  <span className={`text-[8px] font-extrabold ${cfg.text} opacity-90 mt-0.5`}>{cfg.label}</span>
                </div>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Team Leaderboard */}
        <div className="bg-white border-2 border-gray-100 rounded-2xl overflow-hidden shadow-sm">
          <div className="px-4 py-3 bg-gray-50 border-b border-gray-100 flex items-center justify-between">
            <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-sm">Team Overview</p>
            <span className="text-gray-400 text-xs font-semibold">{myTeam.length} workers</span>
          </div>
          <div className="divide-y divide-gray-50">
            {teamSummary.map((w, idx) => {
              const rankEmoji = idx === 0 ? "🥇" : idx === 1 ? "🥈" : idx === 2 ? "🥉" : null;
              const DEPT_C = { Stitching:"#3B82F6", Finishing:"#10B981", QC:"#F59E0B", Cutting:"#EF4444", Embroidery:"#8B5CF6" };
              const avatarColor = DEPT_C[w.department] || "#64748B";
              return (
                <button key={w.id} onClick={() => setSelWorker(w.id)}
                  className={`w-full px-4 py-3 flex items-center gap-3 text-left transition
                    ${selWorker === w.id ? "bg-green-50/50" : "hover:bg-gray-50 active:bg-gray-100"}`}>
                  <div className="w-6 text-center font-black text-sm shrink-0">
                    {rankEmoji || <span className="text-gray-300 text-xs font-bold">#{idx + 1}</span>}
                  </div>
                  <div className="w-9 h-9 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center text-white font-extrabold text-sm shrink-0"
                    style={{ background: avatarColor }}>
                    {w.name.charAt(0)}
                  </div>
                  <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                    <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-sm truncate">{w.name}</p>
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 mt-0.5">
                      <span className="text-gray-400 text-[11px]">{w.staffId}</span>
                      <span className="text-green-600 text-[11px] font-bold">{w.present}P</span>
                      <span className="text-red-500 text-[11px] font-bold">{w.absent}A</span>
                      {w.leave > 0 && <span className="text-blue-500 text-[11px] font-bold">{w.leave}L</span>}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <div className="shrink-0 text-right">
                    <p className={`font-black text-base leading-none
                      ${w.rate >= 90 ? "text-green-600" : w.rate >= 75 ? "text-amber-600" : "text-red-500"}`}>
                      {w.rate}%
                    </p>
                    <div className="w-14 h-1.5 bg-gray-100 rounded-full mt-1.5 overflow-hidden">
                      <div className={`h-full rounded-full transition-all
                        ${w.rate >= 90 ? "bg-green-500" : w.rate >= 75 ? "bg-amber-400" : "bg-red-400"}`}
                        style={{ width: `${w.rate}%` }}/>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </button>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  };

  const AttendanceTab = () => {
    const TODAY_ATT = new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0];
    const [attView, setAttView] = useState("today"); // "today" | "history"
    const [selDate, setSelDate] = useState(TODAY_ATT);
    const [attendance, setAttendance] = useState(() => {
      // Pre-fill with some demo data for today
      const init = {};
      myTeam.forEach(w => { init[w.id] = "none"; });
      // Demo: mark a few as present
      if (myTeam[0]) init[myTeam[0].id] = "present";
      if (myTeam[1]) init[myTeam[1].id] = "present";
      if (myTeam[2]) init[myTeam[2].id] = "absent";
      return init;
    });
    const [saved, setSaved] = useState(false);
    const [search, setSearch] = useState("");
    const [viewMode, setViewMode] = useState("all"); // "all" | "present" | "absent"

    if (attView === "history") return (
      <div className="px-4 pt-5 pb-0">
        {/* Toggle bar */}
        <div className="flex gap-2 mb-4">
          <button onClick={() => setAttView("today")}
            className="flex-1 bg-gray-100 border-2 border-gray-200 text-gray-600 font-bold text-sm py-2.5 rounded-2xl active:scale-95 transition flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5">
            <svg width="15" height="15" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><rect x="3" y="4" width="18" height="18" rx="2" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" fill="none"/><path d="M16 2v4M8 2v4M3 10h18" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
            Today
          </button>
          <button onClick={() => setAttView("history")}
            className="flex-1 bg-green-500 border-2 border-green-500 text-white font-bold text-sm py-2.5 rounded-2xl active:scale-95 transition flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5 shadow-md shadow-green-200">
            <svg width="15" height="15" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="9" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" fill="none"/><path d="M12 7v5l3 3" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
            History
          </button>
        </div>
        <MonthlyAttendanceHistory />
      </div>
    );

    const mark = (workerId, status) => {
      setAttendance(prev => ({ ...prev, [workerId]: status }));
    };

    const markAll = (status) => {
      const updated = {};
      myTeam.forEach(w => { updated[w.id] = status; });
      setAttendance(updated);
    };

    const handleSave = () => {
      // Save to shared attendance state
      myTeam.forEach(w => {
        if (sharedActions?.markAttendance) {
          sharedActions.markAttendance(w.id, selDate, { status: attendance[w.id] || "none", markedBy: user.name });
        }
      });
      setSaved(true);
      setTimeout(() => setSaved(false), 2500);
    };

    const presentCount = myTeam.filter(w => attendance[w.id] === "present").length;
    const absentCount  = myTeam.filter(w => attendance[w.id] === "absent").length;
    const unmarkedCount = myTeam.filter(w => !attendance[w.id] || attendance[w.id] === "none").length;

    const filtered = myTeam.filter(w => {
      const matchSearch = !search || w.name.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase()) || w.staffId.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase());
      const st = attendance[w.id] || "none";
      const matchView = viewMode === "all" || (viewMode === "present" && st === "present") || (viewMode === "absent" && st === "absent");
      return matchSearch && matchView;
    });

    return (
      <div className="px-4 pt-5 pb-28 space-y-4">

        {/* Today / History Toggle */}
        <div className="flex gap-2">
          <button onClick={() => setAttView("today")}
            className="flex-1 bg-green-500 border-2 border-green-500 text-white font-bold text-sm py-2.5 rounded-2xl active:scale-95 transition flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5 shadow-md shadow-green-200">
            <svg width="15" height="15" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><rect x="3" y="4" width="18" height="18" rx="2" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" fill="none"/><path d="M16 2v4M8 2v4M3 10h18" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
            Today
          </button>
          <button onClick={() => setAttView("history")}
            className="flex-1 bg-gray-50 border-2 border-gray-200 text-gray-600 font-bold text-sm py-2.5 rounded-2xl active:scale-95 transition flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5">
            <svg width="15" height="15" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="9" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" fill="none"/><path d="M12 7v5l3 3" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
            History
          </button>
        </div>

        {/* Header */}
        <div className="bg-white border-2 border-green-100 rounded-2xl p-4 space-y-3">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
            <div>
              <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-base">आज की Attendance</p>
              <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs mt-0.5">{myDept} Department</p>
            </div>
            <input type="date" value={selDate} max={TODAY_ATT}
              onChange={e => setSelDate(e.target.value)}
              className="bg-gray-50 border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 text-sm font-bold text-gray-700 focus:outline-none focus:border-green-400"
              style={{fontSize:"14px"}}/>
          </div>

          {/* Summary pills */}
          <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2">
            <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-xl p-2.5 text-center">
              <p className="text-green-700 font-black text-xl leading-none">{presentCount}</p>
              <div className="flex items-center justify-center gap-1 mt-0.5">
                <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M5 13l4 4L19 7" stroke="#16a34a" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/></svg>
                <p className="text-green-600 text-xs font-bold">Present</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-xl p-2.5 text-center">
              <p className="text-red-600 font-black text-xl leading-none">{absentCount}</p>
              <div className="flex items-center justify-center gap-1 mt-0.5">
                <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M18 6L6 18M6 6l12 12" stroke="#dc2626" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
                <p className="text-red-500 text-xs font-bold">Absent</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="bg-amber-50 border border-amber-200 rounded-xl p-2.5 text-center">
              <p className="text-amber-600 font-black text-xl leading-none">{unmarkedCount}</p>
              <div className="flex items-center justify-center gap-1 mt-0.5">
                <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="9" stroke="#d97706" strokeWidth="2"/><path d="M12 7v5l3 3" stroke="#d97706" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
                <p className="text-amber-600 text-xs font-bold">बाकी</p>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Quick Mark All */}
        <div className="flex gap-2">
          <button onClick={() => markAll("present")}
            className="flex-1 bg-green-50 border-2 border-green-200 text-green-700 font-extrabold text-sm py-3 rounded-2xl active:scale-[0.98] active:bg-green-100 transition flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
            <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M5 13l4 4L19 7" stroke="#15803d" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/></svg>
            सभी Present
          </button>
          <button onClick={() => markAll("none")}
            className="flex-1 bg-gray-50 border-2 border-gray-200 text-gray-500 font-bold text-sm py-3 rounded-2xl active:scale-[0.98] transition flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
            <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M3 12a9 9 0 1 0 18 0 9 9 0 0 0-18 0M12 8v4M12 16h.01" stroke="#6b7280" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
            Reset
          </button>
        </div>

        {saved && (
          <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-2xl px-4 py-3 flex items-center gap-2">
            <div className="w-5 h-5 rounded-full bg-green-500 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
              <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 12 12" fill="none"><path d="M2 6l3 3 5-5" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
            </div>
            <p className="text-green-700 text-sm font-semibold">Attendance save हो गई!</p>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Search + Add Member */}
        <div className="flex gap-2">
          <div className="flex-1 relative">
            <svg className="absolute left-3.5 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-gray-400" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none">
              <circle cx="11" cy="11" r="7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.8"/><path d="M21 21l-4-4" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/>
            </svg>
            <input value={search} onChange={e => setSearch(e.target.value)}
              placeholder="Worker नाम या ID से ढूंढें..."
              className="w-full bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-2xl pl-10 pr-4 py-3 text-sm text-gray-900 placeholder-gray-400 focus:outline-none focus:border-green-400 shadow-sm"
              style={{fontSize:"16px"}}/>
          </div>
          <button onClick={() => setShowAddMember(true)}
            className="w-12 h-12 bg-green-500 hover:bg-green-600 active:scale-90 text-white rounded-2xl flex items-center justify-center shadow-md shadow-green-200 shrink-0 transition-all">
            <svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M12 5v14M5 12h14" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
          </button>
        </div>

        {/* Add Member Modal */}
        <Modal open={showAddMember} onClose={() => setShowAddMember(false)} title="Worker ID से जोड़ें">
          <AddMemberById
            myTeam={myTeam}
            onAdd={(worker) => { setMyTeam(prev => [...prev, {...worker, status:"active"}]); setShowAddMember(false); }}
            onClose={() => setShowAddMember(false)}
            TODAY={TODAY}
          />
        </Modal>

        {/* Flip View Toggle */}
        <div className="bg-white border-2 border-gray-100 rounded-2xl p-1.5 flex gap-1 shadow-sm">
          {[
            { id:"all",     label:"All Workers", count: myTeam.length, active:"bg-gray-800 text-white",
              icon:<svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><circle cx="9" cy="7" r="3" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.8" fill="none"/><path d="M3 21v-2a4 4 0 0 1 4-4h4" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round" fill="none"/><circle cx="17" cy="7" r="2" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.8" fill="none"/><path d="M21 21v-1a3 3 0 0 0-2-2.83" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round" fill="none"/></svg> },
            { id:"present", label:"Present",     count: presentCount,  active:"bg-green-500 text-white",
              icon:<svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M5 13l4 4L19 7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2.2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/></svg> },
            { id:"absent",  label:"Absent",      count: absentCount,   active:"bg-red-500 text-white",
              icon:<svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M18 6L6 18M6 6l12 12" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2.2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg> },
          ].map(v => (
            <button key={v.id} onClick={() => setViewMode(v.id)}
              className={`flex-1 flex flex-col items-center py-2.5 rounded-xl font-bold text-xs transition active:scale-95 ${
                viewMode === v.id ? v.active : "text-gray-400 hover:bg-gray-50"
              }`}>
              <span className="leading-none">{v.icon}</span>
              <span className="mt-1">{v.label}</span>
              <span className={`text-lg font-black leading-none mt-0.5 ${viewMode === v.id ? "opacity-100" : "opacity-60"}`}>{v.count}</span>
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* Worker List — grouped by dept */}
        {(() => {
          const DEPT_C = { Stitching:"#3B82F6", Finishing:"#10B981", QC:"#F59E0B", Cutting:"#EF4444", Embroidery:"#8B5CF6" };
          const byDept = filtered.reduce((acc, w) => { (acc[w.department] || (acc[w.department] = [])).push(w); return acc; }, {});
          if (filtered.length === 0) return (
            <div className="text-center py-10 bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-100">
              <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm">कोई worker नहीं मिला</p>
            </div>
          );
          return Object.entries(byDept).map(([dept, workers]) => (
            <div key={dept} className="bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-2xl shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
              {/* Dept header */}
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2.5 bg-gray-50 border-b border-gray-100"
                style={{borderLeftWidth:"4px", borderLeftColor: DEPT_C[dept]||"#64748B", borderLeftStyle:"solid"}}>
                <div>
                  <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-sm">{dept}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{workers.length} workers</p>
                </div>
                <span className="text-xs font-bold px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full"
                  style={{background:(DEPT_C[dept]||"#64748B")+"22", color: DEPT_C[dept]||"#64748B"}}>
                  {workers.filter(w => attendance[w.id] === "present").length}/{workers.length}
                </span>
              </div>
              {/* Worker rows */}
              <div className="divide-y divide-gray-50">
                {workers.map(w => {
                  const status = attendance[w.id] || "none";
                  const color  = DEPT_C[w.department] || "#64748B";
                  return (
                    <div key={w.id} className={`px-4 py-3 flex items-center gap-3 transition-colors ${
                      status === "present" ? "bg-green-50/40" :
                      status === "absent"  ? "bg-red-50/40"   : "bg-white"
                    }`}>
                      {/* Avatar */}
                      <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-2xl flex items-center justify-center text-white font-extrabold text-base shrink-0 relative"
                        style={{background: color}}>
                        {w.name.charAt(0)}
                        {status !== "none" && (
                          <div className={`absolute -bottom-1 -right-1 w-4 h-4 rounded-full border-2 border-white flex items-center justify-center text-[8px] font-black ${
                            status === "present" ? "bg-green-500" : "bg-red-400"
                          }`}>
                            {status === "present" ? "✓" : "✗"}
                          </div>
                        )}
                      </div>
                      {/* Info */}
                      <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                        <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-sm truncate">{w.name}</p>
                        <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{w.staffId}</p>
                      </div>
                      {/* Flip Switch */}
                      <div className="shrink-0 flex flex-col items-center gap-0.5">
                        <div
                          onClick={() => mark(w.id, status === "present" ? "absent" : "present")}
                          className={`relative w-14 h-7 rounded-full cursor-pointer transition-all duration-300 active:scale-95 ${
                            status === "present" ? "bg-green-500" :
                            status === "absent"  ? "bg-red-500"   : "bg-gray-300"
                          }`}>
                          <div className={`absolute top-0.5 w-6 h-6 bg-white rounded-full shadow-md transition-all duration-300 flex items-center justify-center ${
                            status === "present" ? "left-7" : "left-0.5"
                          }`}>
                            {status === "present" && <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M5 13l4 4L19 7" stroke="#16a34a" strokeWidth="3" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/></svg>}
                            {status === "absent"  && <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M18 6L6 18M6 6l12 12" stroke="#ef4444" strokeWidth="3" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>}
                          </div>
                        </div>
                        <span className={`text-[9px] font-extrabold ${
                          status === "present" ? "text-green-600" :
                          status === "absent"  ? "text-red-500"   : "text-gray-400"
                        }`}>
                          {status === "present" ? "Yes" : status === "absent" ? "No" : "Mark"}
                        </span>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  );
                })}
              </div>
            </div>
          ));
        })()}

        {/* Save Button */}
        <button onClick={handleSave}
          className="w-full bg-green-500 active:bg-green-600 text-white font-extrabold text-base py-4 rounded-2xl shadow-md shadow-green-200 active:scale-[0.98] transition flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
          <svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M5 13l4 4L19 7" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/></svg>
          Attendance Save करें ({presentCount}/{myTeam.length})
        </button>
      </div>
    );
  };

  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  // TAB: STYLES
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  const StylesTab = () => {
    const STATUS_COLOR = { Active:"#10B981", Completed:"#3B82F6", Draft:"#94A3B8", Closed:"#EF4444" };
    const addStyle = () => {
      if (!styleForm.styleCode || !styleForm.styleName || !styleForm.buyerName || !styleForm.orderQuantity || !styleForm.deliveryDate) {
        setStyleErr("सभी fields भरना जरूरी है।"); return;
      }
      if (+styleForm.orderQuantity <= 0) { setStyleErr("Quantity 0 से ज्यादा होनी चाहिए।"); return; }
      if (svStyles.find(f => f.styleCode === styleForm.styleCode)) { setStyleErr("Style Code already exists!"); return; }
      setSvStyles([{ ...styleForm, id:"sv"+Date.now(), orderQuantity:+styleForm.orderQuantity, processes:[], status:"Active" }, ...svStyles]);
      setShowStyleModal(false);
      setStyleForm(emptyStyleForm);
      setStyleErr("");
      flashStyle("✅ Style add ho gayi!");
    };
    return (
      <div className="p-4 pb-32">
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
          <div>
            <h2 className="text-lg font-extrabold text-gray-800">Style Files</h2>
            <p className="text-xs text-gray-400">{svStyles.length} styles · {svStyles.filter(s=>s.status==="Active").length} active</p>
          </div>
          <button onClick={()=>{ setShowStyleModal(true); setStyleErr(""); }}
            className="bg-orange-500 active:bg-orange-600 text-white text-sm font-bold px-4 py-2 rounded-xl shadow shadow-orange-200 active:scale-95 transition">
            + New Style
          </button>
        </div>

        {/* Toast */}
        {styleToast && (
          <div className="mb-3 bg-green-50 border border-green-200 text-green-700 text-sm font-semibold px-4 py-2.5 rounded-xl text-center">{styleToast}</div>
        )}

        {/* Style Cards */}
        <div className="flex flex-col gap-3">
          {svStyles.map(s => (
            <div key={s.id} className="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border border-gray-100 p-4">
              <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-2">
                <div>
                  <p className="font-extrabold text-gray-800 text-sm">{s.styleName}</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-gray-400 font-mono mt-0.5">{s.styleCode}</p>
                </div>
                <span className="text-xs font-bold px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full" style={{background:STATUS_COLOR[s.status]+"18", color:STATUS_COLOR[s.status]}}>
                  {s.status}
                </span>
              </div>
              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-x-4 gap-y-1 text-xs text-gray-500 mt-2">
                <span>🏢 <b className="text-gray-700">{s.buyerName}</b></span>
                <span>📦 <b className="text-gray-700">{s.orderQuantity?.toLocaleString()} pcs</b></span>
                {s.fabricType && <span>🧵 {s.fabricType}</span>}
                {s.deliveryDate && <span>📅 {s.deliveryDate}</span>}
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* Modal */}
        {showStyleModal && (
          <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black/50 z-50 flex items-end" onClick={()=>setShowStyleModal(false)}>
            <div className="bg-white w-full rounded-t-3xl p-5 pb-8 max-h-[85vh] overflow-y-auto" onClick={e=>e.stopPropagation()}>
              <div className="w-10 h-1 bg-gray-200 rounded-full mx-auto mb-4"/>
              <h3 className="text-base font-extrabold text-gray-800 mb-4">New Style File</h3>
              {styleErr && <p className="text-red-500 text-xs mb-3 bg-red-50 px-3 py-2 rounded-xl">{styleErr}</p>}
              {[
                ["Style Code *","styleCode","text","e.g. SG-2024-005"],
                ["Style Name *","styleName","text","e.g. Ladies Blazer"],
                ["Buyer Name *","buyerName","text","e.g. Myntra"],
                ["Fabric Type","fabricType","text","e.g. Cotton"],
                ["Color","color","text","e.g. White"],
                ["Size Range","sizeRange","text","e.g. S-XXL"],
                ["Order Quantity *","orderQuantity","number",""],
                ["Delivery Date *","deliveryDate","date",""],
              ].map(([label, key, type, ph]) => (
                <div key={key} className="mb-3">
                  <label className="text-xs font-bold text-gray-600 mb-1 block">{label}</label>
                  <input type={type} placeholder={ph} value={styleForm[key]}
                    onChange={e=>setStyleForm(f=>({...f,[key]:e.target.value}))}
                    className="w-full border border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-3 py-2.5 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-400"/>
                </div>
              ))}
              <div className="flex gap-3 mt-4">
                <button onClick={()=>setShowStyleModal(false)}
                  className="flex-1 border border-gray-200 text-gray-600 font-bold py-3 rounded-xl text-sm active:bg-gray-50">
                  Cancel
                </button>
                <button onClick={addStyle}
                  className="flex-1 bg-orange-500 text-white font-extrabold py-3 rounded-xl text-sm active:bg-orange-600 shadow shadow-orange-200">
                  Create Style
                </button>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    );
  };

  // ── TAB CONFIG — filtered by permissions ──
  const ALL_TABS = [
    { id:"cutting",    label:"Cutting",    show: perms.canViewCutting,
      icon:<svg width="22" height="22" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><circle cx="6" cy="6" r="3" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7"/><circle cx="6" cy="18" r="3" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7"/><path d="M20 4L8.12 15.88M14.47 14.48L20 20M8.12 8.12L12 12" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg> },
    { id:"attendance", label:"Attendance", show: true,
      icon:<svg width="22" height="22" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M9 11l3 3L22 4" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/><rect x="3" y="4" width="13" height="16" rx="2" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" fill="none"/><path d="M7 8h6M7 12h4" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg> },
    { id:"entries",    label:"Entries",    show: perms.canViewEntries,
      icon:<svg width="22" height="22" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M9 11l3 3L22 4" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/><path d="M21 12v7a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V5a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h11" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg> },
    { id:"hourly",     label:"Hourly",     show: perms.canViewHourly,
      icon:<svg width="22" height="22" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="9" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" fill="none"/><path d="M12 7v5l3 3" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg> },
    { id:"profile",    label:"Profile",    show: true,
      icon:<svg width="22" height="22" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><circle cx="12" cy="8" r="4" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" fill="none"/><path d="M4 20c0-4 3.6-7 8-7s8 3 8 7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" strokeLinecap="round" fill="none"/></svg> },
  ];
  const TABS = ALL_TABS.filter(t => t.show);

  const TAB_COLORS = { cutting:"text-red-500", team:"text-blue-500", attendance:"text-green-600", entries:"text-green-600", hourly:"text-amber-500", styles:"text-orange-500", payment:"text-emerald-600", jobs:"text-indigo-500", profile:"text-purple-500" };
  const TAB_DOT    = { cutting:"bg-red-500",   team:"bg-blue-500",   attendance:"bg-green-500",   entries:"bg-green-500",   hourly:"bg-amber-500",   styles:"bg-orange-500",   payment:"bg-emerald-500",   jobs:"bg-indigo-500",   profile:"bg-purple-500"  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-50" style={{fontFamily:"'DM Sans','Segoe UI',sans-serif"}}>
      

      <main className="max-w-lg mx-auto">
        {tab==="cutting"    && <CuttingTab/>}
        {tab==="team"       && <TeamTab/>}
        {tab==="attendance" && <AttendanceTab/>}
        {tab==="entries"    && <WorkEntriesTab/>}
        {tab==="hourly"     && <HourlyTab/>}
        {tab==="styles"     && <StylesTab/>}
        {tab==="payment"    && <PaymentRotationView/>}
        {tab==="profile"    && <ProfileTab/>}
      </main>

      {/* Bottom Nav — stays below keyboard using env(safe-area-inset-bottom) */}
      <nav className="fixed bottom-0 left-0 right-0 z-30 bg-white border-t border-gray-100 shadow-[0_-4px_20px_rgba(0,0,0,0.06)]" style={{paddingBottom:"env(safe-area-inset-bottom)"}}>
        <div className="flex max-w-lg mx-auto">
          {TABS.map(t=>(
            <button key={t.id} onClick={()=>{ setTab(t.id); setSelectedWorker(null); }}
              className={"flex-1 flex flex-col items-center py-3 gap-0.5 transition "+(tab===t.id?TAB_COLORS[t.id]:"text-gray-400")}>
              <div className={tab===t.id?"scale-110 transition-transform":""}>{t.icon}</div>
              <span className="text-xs font-bold">{t.label}</span>
              {tab===t.id && <div className={"w-4 h-0.5 rounded-full mt-0.5 "+TAB_DOT[t.id]}/>}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>
      </nav>
    </div>
  );
};

// ══════════════════════════════════════════
// TODAY MY STAFF
// ══════════════════════════════════════════
const TodayMyStaff = () => {
  const TODAY_DATE = new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0];
  const [searchQ, setSearchQ] = useState("");
  const [deptFilter, setDeptFilter] = useState("all");

  const allWorkers = MOCK_DB.workers;
  const allEntries = MOCK_DB.workEntries.filter(e => e.date === TODAY_DATE || true); // show all as today demo

  // Build today's staff summary
  const todayStaff = allWorkers.map(w => {
    const todayWork = allEntries.filter(e => e.workerId === w.id);
    const pieces = todayWork.reduce((s,e)=>s+(+e.pieces||0),0);
    const amount = todayWork.reduce((s,e)=>s+(+e.amount||0),0);
    return { ...w, entries: todayWork.length, pieces, amount };
  });

  const DEPT_COLOR = { Stitching:"#3B82F6", Finishing:"#10B981", QC:"#F59E0B", Cutting:"#EF4444", Embroidery:"#8B5CF6" };

  const depts = ["all", ...new Set(allWorkers.map(w=>w.department))];

  const filtered = todayStaff
    .filter(w => deptFilter==="all" || w.department===deptFilter)
    .filter(w => !searchQ || w.name.toLowerCase().includes(searchQ.toLowerCase()) || w.staffId.toLowerCase().includes(searchQ.toLowerCase()));

  const totalPieces = filtered.reduce((s,w)=>s+w.pieces,0);
  const totalAmount = filtered.reduce((s,w)=>s+w.amount,0);
  const activeCount = filtered.filter(w=>w.entries>0).length;

  return (
    <div className="p-4 space-y-4 pb-32">
      {/* Search */}
      <div className="relative">
        <svg className="absolute left-3.5 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-gray-400" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none">
          <circle cx="11" cy="11" r="7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.8"/><path d="M21 21l-4-4" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/>
        </svg>
        <input value={searchQ} onChange={e=>setSearchQ(e.target.value)}
          placeholder="Name या Staff ID से खोजें..."
          className="w-full bg-gray-50 border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-2xl pl-10 pr-4 py-3 text-gray-900 font-medium focus:outline-none focus:border-indigo-400 transition"
          style={{fontSize:"16px"}}/>
      </div>

      {/* Dept filter */}
      <div className="flex gap-2 overflow-x-auto pb-1 no-scrollbar">
        {depts.map(d=>(
          <button key={d} onClick={()=>setDeptFilter(d)}
            className={"shrink-0 px-3.5 py-1.5 rounded-full text-xs font-extrabold border transition "+(deptFilter===d?"bg-indigo-500 text-white border-indigo-500":"bg-white text-gray-500 border-gray-200")}>
            {d==="all"?"सभी विभाग":d}
          </button>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Staff list */}
      <div className="space-y-2">
        {filtered.length === 0 && (
          <div className="text-center py-12 bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-100">
            <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm">कोई staff नहीं मिला</p>
          </div>
        )}
        {filtered.map(w=>(
          <div key={w.id} className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-100 shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
            <div className="h-1" style={{background: DEPT_COLOR[w.department]||"#64748B"}}/>
            <div className="px-4 py-3.5 flex items-center gap-3">
              {/* Avatar */}
              <div className="w-11 h-11 rounded-2xl flex items-center justify-center text-white font-extrabold text-base shrink-0"
                style={{background: DEPT_COLOR[w.department]||"#64748B"}}>
                {w.name.charAt(0)}
              </div>
              <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-sm truncate">{w.name}</p>
                <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{w.staffId} · {w.department}</p>
                {w.entries > 0 && (
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-1 mt-0.5">
                    <div className="w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-green-500"/>
                    <p className="text-green-600 text-xs font-bold">{w.entries} entries · {w.pieces} pcs</p>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
              <div className="text-right shrink-0">
                {w.amount > 0 ? (
                  <>
                    <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-sm">Rs {Math.round(w.amount)}</p>
                    <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{w.pieces} pcs</p>
                  </>
                ) : (
                  <span className="text-xs font-bold text-gray-400 bg-gray-100 px-2 py-1 rounded-full">No entry</span>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};


// ============================================================
// PAYMENT LOCK MANAGER (Admin)
// ============================================================
const PaymentLockManager = () => {
  const { sharedPaymentLock, sharedActions, sharedWorkers, sharedEntries } = useContext(AppContext);
  const pl = sharedPaymentLock || { type:"monthly", isLocked:false, lockStartDate: new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0], history:[] };

  const [unlockNote, setUnlockNote]     = useState("");
  const [showUnlock, setShowUnlock]     = useState(false);
  const [showLock,   setShowLock]       = useState(false);
  const [toast, setToast]               = useState("");
  const flash = (msg) => { setToast(msg); setTimeout(()=>setToast(""),2500); };

  const TYPES = [
    { id:"weekly",  label:"Weekly",   days:7,  icon:"📅", desc:"हर 7 दिन में payment" },
    { id:"15day",   label:"15 Days",  days:15, icon:"📆", desc:"हर 15 दिन में payment" },
    { id:"monthly", label:"Monthly",  days:30, icon:"🗓️", desc:"हर महीने payment" },
  ];

  const getNextPaymentDate = () => {
    const start = new Date(pl.lockStartDate);
    const days = TYPES.find(t=>t.id===pl.type)?.days || 30;
    start.setDate(start.getDate() + days);
    return start.toISOString().split("T")[0];
  };

  const getDaysLeft = () => {
    const next = new Date(getNextPaymentDate());
    const today = new Date();
    return Math.max(0, Math.ceil((next - today) / 86400000));
  };

  const totalPayable = (sharedEntries||[])
    .filter(e => e.status==="approved")
    .reduce((s,e) => s+(+e.amount||0), 0);
  const workerCount = (sharedWorkers||[]).filter(w=>w.status==="active").length;

  const daysLeft = getDaysLeft();
  const nextDate = getNextPaymentDate();
  const progress = Math.round((1 - daysLeft / (TYPES.find(t=>t.id===pl.type)?.days||30)) * 100);

  return (
    <div className="p-4 pb-24 max-w-lg mx-auto">
      <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-5">
        <div className="w-9 h-9 rounded-2xl bg-orange-500 flex items-center justify-center">
          <svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><rect x="2" y="7" width="20" height="14" rx="3" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8"/><path d="M16 7V5a2 2 0 0 0-2-2h-4a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v2" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8"/><circle cx="12" cy="14" r="2" fill="white"/></svg>
        </div>
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-lg font-black text-gray-800">Payment Schedule</h1>
          <p className="text-xs text-gray-400">Lock & rotation manage करें</p>
        </div>
      </div>

      {toast && <div className="mb-4 bg-green-50 border border-green-200 text-green-700 text-sm font-bold px-4 py-3 rounded-2xl text-center">{toast}</div>}

      {/* Current Status Card */}
      <div className={`rounded-3xl p-5 mb-4 ${pl.isLocked ? "bg-red-500" : "bg-emerald-500"}`}>
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
          <div>
            <p className="text-white/80 text-xs font-bold uppercase tracking-wider">Current Status</p>
            <p className="text-white font-black text-2xl mt-0.5">{pl.isLocked ? "🔒 LOCKED" : "✅ ACTIVE"}</p>
          </div>
          <div className="bg-white/20 rounded-2xl px-3 py-2 text-center">
            <p className="text-white font-black text-xl leading-none">{daysLeft}</p>
            <p className="text-white/70 text-xs font-bold">days left</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        {/* Progress bar */}
        <div className="mb-3">
          <div className="flex justify-between text-white/70 text-xs font-bold mb-1.5">
            <span>Lock Start: {pl.lockStartDate}</span>
            <span>Next: {nextDate}</span>
          </div>
          <div className="w-full bg-white/20 rounded-full h-2">
            <div className="h-2 rounded-full bg-white transition-all" style={{width:`${Math.min(progress,100)}%`}}/>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          <div className="bg-white/15 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 flex-1 text-center">
            <p className="text-white font-black text-sm">₹{totalPayable.toLocaleString()}</p>
            <p className="text-white/70 text-xs">Total Payable</p>
          </div>
          <div className="bg-white/15 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 flex-1 text-center">
            <p className="text-white font-black text-sm">{workerCount}</p>
            <p className="text-white/70 text-xs">Active Workers</p>
          </div>
          <div className="bg-white/15 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 flex-1 text-center">
            <p className="text-white font-black text-sm capitalize">{pl.type==="15day"?"15-Day":pl.type}</p>
            <p className="text-white/70 text-xs">Cycle</p>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Payment Cycle Selector */}
      <div className="bg-white rounded-3xl border border-gray-100 p-4 mb-4 shadow-sm">
        <p className="text-sm font-extrabold text-gray-700 mb-3">Payment Cycle चुनें</p>
        <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2">
          {TYPES.map(t => (
            <button key={t.id} onClick={() => { sharedActions?.setPaymentType(t.id); flash(`Cycle: ${t.label} set किया`); }}
              disabled={pl.isLocked}
              className={"p-3 rounded-2xl border-2 text-center transition " + (pl.type===t.id ? "border-orange-400 bg-orange-50" : "border-gray-100 bg-gray-50 active:bg-gray-100") + (pl.isLocked?" opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed":"")}>
              <p className="text-xl">{t.icon}</p>
              <p className={"text-xs font-extrabold mt-1 " + (pl.type===t.id?"text-orange-600":"text-gray-600")}>{t.label}</p>
              <p className="text-gray-400 text-[10px] mt-0.5">{t.desc}</p>
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>
        {pl.isLocked && <p className="text-xs text-red-400 font-semibold mt-2 text-center">Unlock के बाद cycle change करें</p>}
      </div>

      {/* Lock / Unlock Buttons */}
      <div className="flex gap-3 mb-5">
        {!pl.isLocked ? (
          <button onClick={() => setShowLock(true)}
            className="flex-1 bg-red-500 text-white font-extrabold py-4 rounded-2xl shadow shadow-red-200 active:scale-95 transition flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
            <svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><rect x="3" y="11" width="18" height="11" rx="2" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8"/><path d="M7 11V7a5 5 0 0 1 10 0v4" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
            Payment Lock करें
          </button>
        ) : (
          <button onClick={() => setShowUnlock(true)}
            className="flex-1 bg-emerald-500 text-white font-extrabold py-4 rounded-2xl shadow shadow-green-200 active:scale-95 transition flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
            <svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><rect x="3" y="11" width="18" height="11" rx="2" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8"/><path d="M7 11V7a5 5 0 0 1 9.9-1" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
            Payment Release करें
          </button>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Payment History */}
      <div className="bg-white rounded-3xl border border-gray-100 p-4 shadow-sm">
        <p className="text-sm font-extrabold text-gray-700 mb-3">Payment History</p>
