        {(pl.history||[]).length === 0 && <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm text-center py-4">कोई history नहीं है अभी तक।</p>}
        <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
          {(pl.history||[]).map((h,i) => (
            <div key={h.id||i} className="flex items-center gap-3 bg-gray-50 rounded-2xl px-3 py-3">
              <div className="w-9 h-9 rounded-xl bg-green-100 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
                <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M12 2v20M17 5H9.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 0 0 7h5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 0 7H6" stroke="#10B981" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
              </div>
              <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                <p className="text-sm font-bold text-gray-800">₹{(h.totalAmount||0).toLocaleString()}</p>
                <p className="text-xs text-gray-400">{h.date} · {h.workerCount} workers · {h.type==="15day"?"15-Day":h.type}</p>
                {h.note && <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 truncate">{h.note}</p>}
              </div>
              <span className="text-xs font-bold px-2 py-1 rounded-full bg-green-100 text-green-700">✅ Paid</span>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Lock Confirm Modal */}
      {showLock && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black/50 z-50 flex items-center justify-center p-4" onClick={() => setShowLock(false)}>
          <div className="bg-white rounded-3xl p-6 w-full max-w-sm" onClick={e=>e.stopPropagation()}>
            <div className="text-center mb-4">
              <div className="text-4xl mb-2">🔒</div>
              <h3 className="text-lg font-black text-gray-800">Payment Lock करें?</h3>
              <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 mt-1">Supervisors और Workers payment details नहीं देख पाएंगे।</p>
            </div>
            <div className="flex gap-3">
              <button onClick={() => setShowLock(false)} className="flex-1 border border-gray-200 text-gray-600 font-bold py-3 rounded-xl text-sm">Cancel</button>
              <button onClick={() => { sharedActions?.lockPayment(); setShowLock(false); flash("🔒 Payment Locked!"); }}
                className="flex-1 bg-red-500 text-white font-extrabold py-3 rounded-xl text-sm">Lock करें</button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Unlock + Release Modal */}
      {showUnlock && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black/50 z-50 flex items-end" onClick={() => setShowUnlock(false)}>
          <div className="bg-white w-full rounded-t-3xl p-5 pb-8" onClick={e=>e.stopPropagation()}>
            <div className="w-10 h-1 bg-gray-200 rounded-full mx-auto mb-4"/>
            <h3 className="text-base font-extrabold text-gray-800 mb-1">Payment Release करें</h3>
            <p className="text-xs text-gray-400 mb-4">₹{totalPayable.toLocaleString()} को {workerCount} workers में release किया जाएगा</p>
            <label className="text-xs font-bold text-gray-600 mb-1 block">Note (optional)</label>
            <input value={unlockNote} onChange={e=>setUnlockNote(e.target.value)}
              placeholder="e.g. February 2024 payment..."
              className="w-full border border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-3 py-2.5 text-sm mb-4 focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-400"/>
            <div className="flex gap-3">
              <button onClick={() => setShowUnlock(false)} className="flex-1 border border-gray-200 text-gray-600 font-bold py-3 rounded-xl text-sm">Cancel</button>
              <button onClick={() => {
                sharedActions?.unlockPayment(unlockNote, totalPayable, workerCount);
                setShowUnlock(false); setUnlockNote("");
                flash("✅ Payment Released!");
              }} className="flex-1 bg-emerald-500 text-white font-extrabold py-3 rounded-xl text-sm shadow shadow-green-200">
                Release करें ✅
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

// ============================================================
// PAYMENT ROTATION VIEW (Supervisor + Worker — read only)
// ============================================================
const PaymentRotationView = () => {
  const { sharedPaymentLock, sharedEntries, user } = useContext(AppContext);
  const pl = sharedPaymentLock || { type:"monthly", isLocked:false, lockStartDate: new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0], history:[] };

  const TYPES = { weekly:7, "15day":15, monthly:30 };
  const days = TYPES[pl.type] || 30;

  const getNextPaymentDate = () => {
    const start = new Date(pl.lockStartDate);
    start.setDate(start.getDate() + days);
    return start.toISOString().split("T")[0];
  };

  const nextDate = getNextPaymentDate();
  const daysLeft = Math.max(0, Math.ceil((new Date(nextDate) - new Date()) / 86400000));
  const progress = Math.round((1 - daysLeft / days) * 100);

  const myEntries = (sharedEntries||[]).filter(e =>
    (e.workerId===user.id || e.staffId===user.staffId) && e.status==="approved"
  );
  const myTotal = myEntries.reduce((s,e)=>s+(+e.amount||0),0);

  const typeLabel = pl.type==="15day"?"15-Day":pl.type==="weekly"?"Weekly":"Monthly";

  return (
    <div className="p-4 pb-10">
      <h2 className="text-base font-extrabold text-gray-800 mb-4">💰 Payment Rotation</h2>

      {/* Status Banner */}
      <div className={`rounded-3xl p-5 mb-4 ${pl.isLocked ? "bg-red-500" : "bg-emerald-500"}`}>
        <p className="text-white/80 text-xs font-bold uppercase tracking-wider mb-1">Payment Status</p>
        <p className="text-white font-black text-xl">{pl.isLocked ? "🔒 Payment Locked" : "✅ Payment Active"}</p>
        {pl.isLocked && <p className="text-white/80 text-xs mt-1">Admin approval का इंतज़ार है</p>}

        <div className="mt-3 mb-1">
          <div className="flex justify-between text-white/70 text-[11px] font-bold mb-1">
            <span>Cycle: {typeLabel}</span>
            <span>Next: {nextDate}</span>
          </div>
          <div className="w-full bg-white/20 rounded-full h-2">
            <div className="h-2 rounded-full bg-white" style={{width:`${Math.min(progress,100)}%`}}/>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="flex gap-2 mt-3">
          <div className="bg-white/15 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 flex-1 text-center">
            <p className="text-white font-black text-base">{daysLeft}</p>
            <p className="text-white/70 text-[11px]">Days Left</p>
          </div>
          <div className="bg-white/15 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 flex-1 text-center">
            <p className="text-white font-black text-base">₹{myTotal.toLocaleString()}</p>
            <p className="text-white/70 text-[11px]">My Earnings</p>
          </div>
          <div className="bg-white/15 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 flex-1 text-center">
            <p className="text-white font-black text-base">{myEntries.length}</p>
            <p className="text-white/70 text-[11px]">Entries</p>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Timeline */}
      <div className="bg-white rounded-3xl border border-gray-100 p-4 mb-4 shadow-sm">
        <p className="text-sm font-extrabold text-gray-700 mb-3">Payment Timeline</p>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <div className="text-center">
            <div className="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-orange-500 mx-auto"/>
            <p className="text-[10px] text-gray-500 mt-1 font-bold">Start</p>
            <p className="text-[10px] text-gray-700 font-black">{pl.lockStartDate}</p>
          </div>
          <div className="flex-1 relative h-2 bg-gray-100 rounded-full">
            <div className="absolute top-0 left-0 h-2 rounded-full bg-orange-400" style={{width:`${Math.min(progress,100)}%`}}/>
          </div>
          <div className="text-center">
            <div className={`w-3 h-3 rounded-full mx-auto ${daysLeft===0?"bg-green-500":"bg-gray-300"}`}/>
            <p className="text-[10px] text-gray-500 mt-1 font-bold">Payment</p>
            <p className="text-[10px] text-gray-700 font-black">{nextDate}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <p className="text-center text-xs text-orange-500 font-bold mt-3">
          {daysLeft === 0 ? "🎉 Payment Due Today!" : `${daysLeft} दिन बाद payment होगी`}
        </p>
      </div>

      {/* History */}
      <div className="bg-white rounded-3xl border border-gray-100 p-4 shadow-sm">
        <p className="text-sm font-extrabold text-gray-700 mb-3">Payment History</p>
        {(pl.history||[]).length === 0 && <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm text-center py-3">कोई history नहीं</p>}
        <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
          {(pl.history||[]).map((h,i) => (
            <div key={h.id||i} className="flex items-center gap-3 bg-gray-50 rounded-2xl px-3 py-2.5">
              <div className="w-8 h-8 rounded-xl bg-green-100 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 text-sm">✅</div>
              <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                <p className="text-sm font-bold text-gray-800">{h.date}</p>
                <p className="text-xs text-gray-400">{h.type==="15day"?"15-Day":h.type} · {h.workerCount} workers</p>
              </div>
              <p className="text-sm font-extrabold text-green-600 shrink-0">₹{(h.totalAmount||0).toLocaleString()}</p>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const BOTTOM_NAV = ["hourly", "styles", "today-staff"];

// ============================================================
// MAIN APP

    const meta = document.querySelector("meta[name=viewport]");
    if (meta) meta.content = "width=device-width, initial-scale=1, viewport-fit=cover, interactive-widget=resizes-visual";

    MOCK_DB.workEntries.map(e => ({ ...e, status: e.status || "pending" }))

    { id:"c1", date:"2024-01-15", style:"Men's Formal Shirt", styleId:"s1",

      totalLayers:32, totalPieces:640, marker:"M-001", status:"done", department:"Cutting" },

      sizes:[{size:"M",bundles:6,pcsPerBundle:20,total:120},{size:"L",bundles:8,pcsPerBundle:20,total:160},{size:"XL",bundles:4,pcsPerBundle:20,total:80}],

      totalLayers:46, totalPieces:690, marker:"K-001", status:"done", department:"Cutting" },
    { id:"c4b", date:"2024-01-08", style:"Women's Kurta", styleId:"s2",
      sizes:[{size:"36",bundles:8,pcsPerBundle:15,total:120},{size:"38",bundles:9,pcsPerBundle:15,total:135},{size:"40",bundles:7,pcsPerBundle:15,total:105}],
      totalLayers:24, totalPieces:360, marker:"K-002", status:"done", department:"Cutting" },
    { id:"c2", date:"2024-01-14", style:"Kids T-Shirt", styleId:"s3",
      sizes:[{size:"2Y",bundles:6,pcsPerBundle:15,total:90},{size:"4Y",bundles:8,pcsPerBundle:15,total:120},{size:"6Y",bundles:7,pcsPerBundle:15,total:105},{size:"8Y",bundles:5,pcsPerBundle:15,total:75}],
      totalLayers:26, totalPieces:390, marker:"M-002", status:"done", department:"Cutting" },
    { id:"c3", date:"2024-01-13", style:"Denim Jeans", styleId:"s4",
      sizes:[{size:"30",bundles:4,pcsPerBundle:10,total:40},{size:"32",bundles:6,pcsPerBundle:10,total:60},{size:"34",bundles:5,pcsPerBundle:10,total:50}],
      totalLayers:15, totalPieces:150, marker:"M-003", status:"pending", department:"Cutting" },
  ]);
  const [sharedStyles,   setSharedStyles]   = useState(INIT_STYLE_FILES.map(s => ({ ...s, visibleToSupervisors: [] })));
  const [sharedPaymentLock, setSharedPaymentLock] = useState({
    type: "monthly",           // "weekly" | "15day" | "monthly"
    isLocked: false,
    lockStartDate: new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0],
    history: [
      { id:"ph1", date:"2024-01-01", type:"monthly", totalAmount:45200, workerCount:12, status:"paid", note:"January 2024 payment" },
      { id:"ph2", date:"2023-12-01", type:"monthly", totalAmount:42800, workerCount:11, status:"paid", note:"December 2023 payment" },
      { id:"ph3", date:"2023-11-01", type:"monthly", totalAmount:38500, workerCount:10, status:"paid", note:"November 2023 payment" },
    ],
  });
  const [sharedHourly,   setSharedHourly]   = useState(MOCK_DB.hourlyReports);
  const [sharedWorkers,  setSharedWorkers]  = useState(MOCK_DB.workers);
  const [sharedNotifs,   setSharedNotifs]   = useState([]);
  const [sharedAttendance, setSharedAttendance] = useState({});  // { "workerId_date": {in, out, status} }
  const [sharedChat,       setSharedChat]       = useState([]);  // all messages
  const [sharedGatePasses, setSharedGatePasses] = useState([]); // gate pass requests

  // Add notification helper
  const addNotif = (msg, type="info", dept="") => {
    const n = { id: Date.now(), msg, type, dept, time: new Date().toLocaleTimeString("hi-IN") };
    setSharedNotifs(prev => [n, ...prev].slice(0, 20));
  };

  // Shared actions
  const sharedActions = {
    // Admin adds style → shared globally
    addStyle: (style) => {
      setSharedStyles(prev => [{ ...style, visibleToSupervisors: [] }, ...prev]);
    },
    // Admin sets payment lock type
    setPaymentType: (type) => {
      setSharedPaymentLock(prev => ({ ...prev, type }));
    },
    // Admin locks payment
    lockPayment: () => {
      setSharedPaymentLock(prev => ({ ...prev, isLocked: true, lockStartDate: new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0] }));
    },
    // Admin unlocks + adds to history
    unlockPayment: (note, totalAmount, workerCount) => {
      setSharedPaymentLock(prev => ({
        ...prev,
        isLocked: false,
        history: [{ id:"ph"+Date.now(), date:new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0], type:prev.type, totalAmount:totalAmount||0, workerCount:workerCount||0, status:"paid", note:note||"" }, ...prev.history],
      }));
    },
    // Admin assigns supervisors to a style
    assignSupervisors: (styleId, supervisorIds) => {
      setSharedStyles(prev => prev.map(s => s.id===styleId ? { ...s, visibleToSupervisors: supervisorIds } : s));
    },
    // Admin updates style status
    updateStyleStatus: (id, status) => {
      setSharedStyles(prev => prev.map(s => s.id===id ? { ...s, status } : s));
    },
    // Worker submits entry → goes to supervisor as pending
    addEntry: (entry) => {
      const newEntry = { ...entry, id: entry.id || "we"+Date.now(), status: entry.status || "pending" };
      setSharedEntries(prev => {
        // duplicate avoid
        if (prev.find(e => e.id === newEntry.id)) return prev;
        return [newEntry, ...prev];
      });
      addNotif(`${entry.workerName} ने नई entry submit की — ${entry.pieces} pcs`, "entry", entry.department);
    },
    // Supervisor approves/rejects
    updateEntryStatus: (id, status, byName) => {
      setSharedEntries(prev => prev.map(e => e.id===id ? {...e, status} : e));
      const e = sharedEntries.find(x=>x.id===id);
      if (e) addNotif(`${e.workerName} की entry ${status==="approved"?"✅ Approved":"❌ Rejected"} by ${byName}`, status, e.department);
    },
    // Supervisor adds cutting
    addCut: (cut, dept) => {
      setSharedCuts(prev => [{ ...cut, id:"c"+Date.now(), department:dept }, ...prev]);
      addNotif(`नई cutting entry — ${cut.style} · ${cut.totalPieces} pcs`, "cutting", dept);
    },
    // Supervisor adds hourly report
    addHourly: (report, dept) => {
      setSharedHourly(prev => [{ ...report, id:"h"+Date.now(), department:dept }, ...prev]);
      addNotif(`Hourly report: ${report.department} · ${report.hourSlot}`, "hourly", dept);
    },
    // Admin adds worker
    addWorker: (worker) => {
      setSharedWorkers(prev => [...prev, { ...worker, id:"w"+Date.now(), status:"active" }]);
      addNotif(`नया worker joined: ${worker.name} — ${worker.department}`, "worker");
    },
    // Attendance
    markAttendance: (workerId, date, record) => {
      setSharedAttendance(prev => ({ ...prev, [workerId+"_"+date]: record }));
    },
    // Chat message
    sendMessage: (msg) => {
      setSharedChat(prev => [{ ...msg, id:"msg"+Date.now(), time: new Date().toLocaleTimeString("hi-IN") }, ...prev].slice(0,200));
    },
    // Gate pass
    requestGatePass: (pass) => {
      setSharedGatePasses(prev => [{ ...pass, id:"gp"+Date.now(), status:"pending", requestTime: new Date().toLocaleTimeString("hi-IN") }, ...prev]);
      addNotif(`🚪 Gate pass request: ${pass.workerName}`, "gatepass");
    },
    approveGatePass: (id) => {
      setSharedGatePasses(prev => prev.map(g => g.id===id ? {...g, status:"approved", approvedAt:new Date().toLocaleTimeString("hi-IN")} : g));
    },
    rejectGatePass: (id) => {
      setSharedGatePasses(prev => prev.map(g => g.id===id ? {...g, status:"rejected"} : g));
    },
  };

  const handleLogin = (u) => { setUser(u); setPage("dashboard"); setPageHistory([]); };
  const handleLogout = () => { setUser(null); setPage("dashboard"); setPageHistory([]); };

  const navigate = (p) => {
    if (p !== page) {
      setPageHistory(prev => [...prev, page]);
    }
    setPage(p);
    setSidebarOpen(false);
  };

  const goBack = () => {
    if (pageHistory.length > 0) {
      const prev = pageHistory[pageHistory.length - 1];
      setPageHistory(h => h.slice(0, -1));
      setPage(prev);
    } else {
      setPage("dashboard");
    }
    setSidebarOpen(false);
  };

  // ── Phone Back Button Support ──────────────────────────────
  // Har page change pe browser history mein ek entry push karo
  useEffect(() => {
    window.history.pushState({ page }, "", window.location.pathname);
  }, [page]);

  // Phone ka back button dabane pe goBack() call hoga
  useEffect(() => {
    const handlePopState = () => {
      goBack();
      // Re-push so next back press bhi kaam kare
      window.history.pushState({ page }, "", window.location.pathname);
    };
    window.addEventListener("popstate", handlePopState);
    return () => window.removeEventListener("popstate", handlePopState);
  }, [pageHistory, page]);
  // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  if (!user) return <LoginPage onLogin={handleLogin} />;

  // Worker के लिए अलग dedicated panel
  if (user.role === "worker") {
    return (
      <AppContext.Provider value={{ user, navigate: () => {}, sharedEntries, sharedCuts, sharedPaymentLock, sharedAttendance, sharedChat, sharedGatePasses, sharedActions, sharedNotifs }}>
        <WorkerPanel onLogout={handleLogout} />
      </AppContext.Provider>
    );
  }

  // Supervisor के लिए अलग dedicated panel
  if (user.role === "supervisor") {
    return (
      <AppContext.Provider value={{ user, navigate: () => {}, sharedEntries, sharedCuts, sharedStyles, sharedPaymentLock, sharedHourly, sharedWorkers, sharedAttendance, sharedChat, sharedGatePasses, sharedActions, sharedNotifs }}>
        <SupervisorPanel onLogout={handleLogout} />
      </AppContext.Provider>
    );
  }


  const allowedNav = NAV_ITEMS.filter(n => n.roles.includes(user.role));
  const bottomNav = allowedNav.filter(n => BOTTOM_NAV.includes(n.id));

  const renderPage = () => {
    switch (page) {
      case "dashboard": return <Dashboard />;
      case "staff-payment": return <StaffPaymentFull />;
      case "work-entry": return <WorkEntry />;

      case "self-entry": return <SelfEntry />;
      case "workers": return <Workers />;
      case "styles": return <Styles />;
      case "operations": return <Operations />;
      case "departments": return <Departments />;
      case "payments": return <Payments />;
      case "hourly": return <HourlyReports />;
      case "today-staff": return <TodayMyStaff />;
      case "jobs": return <JobPortal />;

      case "export":  return <ExportCenter />;
      case "profile": return <Profile onLogout={handleLogout} />;
      case "payment-schedule": return <PaymentLockManager />;
      case "sup-permissions": return <SupervisorPermissions />;
      default: return <Dashboard />;
    }
  };

  return (
    <AppContext.Provider value={{ user, navigate, sharedEntries, sharedCuts, sharedStyles, sharedPaymentLock, sharedHourly, sharedWorkers, sharedAttendance, sharedChat, sharedGatePasses, sharedActions, sharedNotifs }}>
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-white text-gray-900 font-sans"
        style={{ fontFamily: "'DM Sans', 'Segoe UI', sans-serif" }}>

        {/* Desktop Sidebar */}
        <aside className={`fixed top-0 left-0 h-full w-64 bg-white border-r-2 border-orange-100 z-40 flex flex-col
          transform transition-transform duration-300 lg:translate-x-0 ${sidebarOpen ? "translate-x-0" : "-translate-x-full"}`}>

          {/* Nav */}
          <nav className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto py-3 px-3 space-y-0.5">
            {allowedNav.map(item => (
              <button key={item.id} onClick={() => navigate(item.id)}
                className={`w-full flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2.5 rounded-xl text-sm font-semibold transition-all
                  ${page === item.id
                    ? "bg-orange-500 text-white shadow-md shadow-orange-300/40"
                    : "text-gray-600 hover:bg-orange-50 hover:text-orange-600"}`}>
                <NavIcon id={item.id} size={17} />
                {item.label}
                {page === item.id && <div className="ml-auto w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-white/70" />}
              </button>
            ))}
          </nav>

          <div className="p-4 border-t-2 border-orange-50">
            <button onClick={handleLogout} className="w-full flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2.5 rounded-xl text-red-500 hover:bg-red-50 hover:border-red-200 border-2 border-transparent text-sm font-bold transition">
              <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
              <path d="M6 14H3a1 1 0 0 1-1-1V3a1 1 0 0 1 1-1h3M10 11l3-3-3-3M13 8H6" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
            </svg> Sign Out
            </button>
          </div>
        </aside>

        {/* Sidebar overlay (mobile) */}
        {sidebarOpen && (
          <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black/60 z-30 lg:hidden" onClick={() => setSidebarOpen(false)} />
        )}

        {/* Floating hamburger — mobile only */}
        <button onClick={() => setSidebarOpen(true)}
          className="lg:hidden fixed top-3 left-3 z-20 w-10 h-10 bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-xl shadow-md flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-1.5 active:scale-95 transition">
          <div className="w-5 h-0.5 bg-gray-700 rounded"/>
          <div className="w-4 h-0.5 bg-gray-500 rounded"/>
          <div className="w-5 h-0.5 bg-gray-700 rounded"/>
        </button>

        {/* Floating back button — non-dashboard pages */}
        {page !== "dashboard" && (
          <button onClick={goBack}
            className="lg:hidden fixed top-3 left-16 z-20 h-10 px-3 bg-orange-50 border border-orange-200 rounded-xl shadow-md flex items-center gap-1.5 text-orange-600 font-bold text-sm active:scale-95 transition">
            ← Back
          </button>
        )}

        {/* Main content */}
        <div className="lg:pl-64 flex flex-col min-h-screen">
          {/* Page content */}
          <main className="flex-1 p-4 pt-14 lg:pt-4 pb-24 lg:pb-6 max-w-5xl mx-auto w-full">
            {renderPage()}
          </main>
        </div>

        {/* Mobile Bottom Nav */}
        <nav className="lg:hidden fixed bottom-0 left-0 right-0 bg-white border-t-2 border-orange-100 z-20 px-2 py-2 safe-area-pb shadow-lg">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-around">
            {bottomNav.map(item => (
              <button key={item.id} onClick={() => navigate(item.id)}
                className={`flex flex-col items-center gap-0.5 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl transition-all
                  ${page === item.id ? "text-orange-500" : "text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-600"}`}>
                <NavIcon id={item.id} size={22} className={`transition-transform ${page === item.id ? "scale-110" : ""}`} />
                <span className="text-xs font-bold">{item.label}</span>
                {page === item.id && <div className="w-4 h-1 bg-orange-500 rounded-full mt-0.5" />}
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
        </nav>
      </div>
    </AppContext.Provider>
  );
}
